<pb n="b625"/>
<head>br̥hatī</head>
<head>(śābarabhāṣyavyākhyā)</head>
<head>tr̥tīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">athātaśśēṣalakṣaṇam ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>1<quote>nānākarmalakṣaṇaṁ vr̥ttamiti</quote> । karmānubandhabhēdācchāstrabhēdaḥ, ataḥ śāstra-
bhēdalakṣaṇaṁ vr̥ttamityarthaḥ । nanu ca śāstrabhēdē satyaidamarthyaṁ na
siddha‍yati aṅgapradhānānām । viniyōgataḥ karmabhēdaḥ uktaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b626"/>
nanu cēdānīmēva viniyōgaścintyatē । kathaṁ viniyōgatō bhēdaḥ, bhēdē
sati viniyōgaḥ । ata ēva na bhēdalakṣaṇaṁ vr̥ttamiti hētvarthatayaiva
bhēdalakṣaṇōpanyāsaḥ śēṣalakṣaṇasya । satyaṁ, hētvarthatayaiva upanyāsaḥ
satyaṁ ca bhēdādviniyōgaḥ । tathāpi śāstrabhēdō'pi viniyōgata
ēva । kintvasau viniyōgaḥ padanimittakaḥ ।</p>
<p>kimidaṁ padanimittaka iti ? pratipattau hētuḥ padanimittakaḥ
padārthānāṁ saṁbandhapratipattinimittaka ityarthaḥ । yastvayaṁ tr̥tīyē
cintyatē sa kāryanimittakaḥ । atō vākyārthabhēdēna śāstrabhēdē
sati vākyārthānāṁ parasparaṁ śēṣaśēṣicintā śēṣalakṣaṇamityucyatē
lakṣyatē hi śēṣaśēṣipratipattau na pratipādyatē1 । nanu vrīhīn
﻿<pb n="b627"/>
prōkṣatīti padārthānāṁ śēṣaśiṣicintā । aśravaṇamatrāparādhyatē
bhavataḥ । vrīhibhiryajētētyanēna sahāsya śēṣaśēṣicintā na puna-
rvrīhipadārthamātratayaiva । kimiti tarhi śēṣalakṣaṇaṁ ? viniyōjyō
hi śēṣaḥ tadviṣayāṇi śrutyādīni tasmācchēṣalakṣaṇamityucyatē ।
śēṣiparijñānaṁ tarhi kinnimittaṁ ? pramāṇāntaranimittakaṁ tat ।
﻿<pb n="b628"/>
lakṣyatē hi śēṣī śēṣapratipattau, na pratipādyatē । atō yuk‍taṁ
śēṣalakṣaṇam ।</p>
<p>yadyēvaṁ viniyōjyaḥ śēṣa iti vaktavyam । kimidaṁ śēṣaḥ parārtha-
tvāditi ? uktamasmābhiḥ padanimittakō'pi viniyōgō vidyata iti ।
ataḥ kāryē viniyōjyaḥ śēṣaḥ kathaṁ syāditi śēṣaḥ parārthatvādityu-
ktam । yasya kāryē viniyōgaḥ sa tadartha ēva bhavati । ataḥ
parārthatvāditi lakṣitam । na ca kāryaṁ parārthaṁ bhavitumarhati kāryamēva
hi tanna syāt yadyanyārtham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b629"/>
<p>ata ēva garbhadāsadr̥ṣṭāntō bhāṣyē । nanu ca parārthatāmātraṁ parārtha-
śabdēnōcyatē । kimidaṁ atyantaparārtha iti । ucyatē । ata ēvā-
tyantaparārthaḥ yasmāt parārthatāmātrataivōcyatē । ataḥ sādhu vivr̥tam ।
﻿<pb n="b630"/>
<quote>kaḥ śēṣaḥ kēna hētunā śēṣaḥ1 iti</quote> । kimidaṁ praśnadvayaṁ ? kēna hētunā śēṣa
ityētāvadvaktavyam । siddha‍yati hi parārthatvācchēṣa iti । ucyatē,
syādētadēvaṁ yadi siddhavadabhidhānaṁ hētōḥ syāt । hēturapyatra kathanīya
ēvētyadōṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ata ēva kō dharmaḥ kathaṁlakṣaṇaṁ ityuktam । kiṁ punaḥ siddhasya
kathanē prayōjanaṁ ? upayuktādanyaḥ śēṣa ityēvamādinivr̥ttyartham ।
<quote>kathaṁ ca viniyujyata 2iti ?</quote> kō'yaṁ praśnaḥ ? kēna viniyujyata iti
vaktavyam, kimidaṁ kathaṁ ca viniyujyata iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b631"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । kēna viniyujyata ityucyamānē śrutyādivyā-
pāra ēva kēvalaṁ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kathitaśca bhavati । na punaḥ saviniyōgānāṁ
śrutyādīnāṁ, na ca niyōgaśūnyāni śrutyādīni śēṣatāmāpādayituṁ
śak‍nuvanti । kāryābhāvāt । kāryanimittaṁ ca parārthamityuktam । ataḥ
kathaṁ ca viniyujyata ityuktaṁ sahētukaviniyōgasiddha‍yartham । ata ēva
ca śrutyādīni viniyōgē kāraṇānītyuktam । na punaḥ śrutyādibhiriti ।
kathamityanuṣaṅgaḥ । tēṣāṁ balavadabalavattētyanēnāpi kathaṁ cētyanuṣak‍tavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b632"/>
ēṣa tāvat lakṣaṇārthaḥ । naitāvatā vinā śēṣaparijñānasiddhiḥ । ata
ēvānyadapi sādhanasiddha‍yarthaṁ kiñcidupōddhātādinā śēṣaḥ parārtha-
tvāditi sūtraṁ sabhāṣyaṁ vyākhyātam ।</p>
<p>1<quote>atha tatra kiṁ br̥ttam ? yaistu dravyaṁ cikīrṣyatē guṇastatra pratīyētēti</quote> ।
uk‍taṁ tacchēṣalakṣaṇaṁ manvānasyaitaccōdyam । uttaraṁ tu niyōga-
viṣayatā tatrāpanītā śēṣatvaṁ tu ihaiva sarvēṣāṁ pratipādyatē ।
kō'yaṁ viniyōgaviṣayatvāpanhavaḥ ? na ca viniyōgaśūnyāni
śrūtyādīni śēṣatayā viniyōk‍tuṁ śak‍nuvantītyuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b633"/>
tasmācchēṣatvaṁ viniyōgāpahnavaścēti vipratiṣiddham । ataḥ śēṣatvaṁ
vā nāstyapūrvaviṣayatā vā nāpahnōtuṁ śakyatē । ucyatē---anabhijñō
bhavān viṣayaniyōjyānām । na brūmō guṇabhūtēṣu pusāṁ niyōjyatā
nāstīti । kiṁ tarhi ? viṣayastu na bhavatīti। kāryāntarasya darśanāt।
yasya punarniyōgasiddhirēva kāryaḥ sa viṣayaḥ <q>‘tēṣāmarthēna’</q> ityatna prakaṭa-
taramēva vakṣyāmaḥ । atō yuktamuk‍taṁ tatrāpūrvārthatā vyāvartitēti ।1</p>
﻿<pb n="b634"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣu bādariḥ ।। 3 ।।1</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratrāsyābhiprāyō dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣvēva pārārthyaṁ vadataḥ ?
ayamabhiprāyaḥ---vibhaktibhiḥ tādarthyaṁ prātipadikārthasya pratipādyatē ।
tacca dravyaguṇayōrupalabhyatē ēkahāyanyā krīṇātīti aruṇayēti
ca । saṁskārasya tu kathaṁ ? tatrāpi vibhaktyaiva vrīhin prōkṣati
vrīhīnavahanti iti । nanu ca prātipadikārthasya prādhānyaṁ
dvitīyā pratipādayati na karmaṇō guṇabhāvam । akārakajñō bhavān ।
kārakavibhak‍tayō hi kathaṁ kriyānirapēkṣāḥ । tasmāt kriyā-
nirapēkṣamēva prātipadikārthasya prādhānyaṁ guṇatvaṁ vā । ata
ēva ca vibhaktividhānē bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ kārakōddēśaḥ ।
<pb n="b635"/>
kathaṁ tarhi taddhitādiṣu tādarthyāvagatiḥ kathaṁ cōpapadavibhaktayaḥ ।
atō'nyadapi vibhaktivyatirik‍taṁ pārārthyē pramāṇaṁ dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣu
vaktavyam ।</p>
<p>nanu cōpakāradarśanamēva dravyaguṇasaṁskārāṇāṁ pārārthyē hēturiti
bādarērmatam । kimatra vibhaktyādibhi kriyatē । ucyatē---yadyu-
pakāradarśanaṁ pārārthyē hētuḥ brīhayō'pi prōkṣaṇasyōpakārakāḥ syuḥ । atha
prayōjanaṁ prati upakāradarśanaṁ hētuḥ, prayōjanavattājñānamidānīṁ kutaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b636"/>
niyōgata iti cēt । ēvaṁ tarhi niyōganirvr̥tirēva pārārthyē
hētuḥ kimidaṁ upakāradarśanaṁ kariṣyati । ata ēva ca
vibhak‍tivyatyayō'pi prayājaśēṣēṇētyēvamādiṣu siddhō bhavati ।
kr̥ttaddhitasamāsāśca tadvaśēnaiva aidamarthyapratipādakā bhavanti । ēva-
mapyupapadavibhak‍tērasaṅkaraḥ siddhō bhavati ।</p>
<p>kimiti tarhi bādariḥ dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣvēva śēṣabhāvaṁ
manyatē yadi niyōganirvr̥ttiḥ pārārthyē hētuḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b637"/>
<p>na niyōgaṁ phalē puruṣē ca manyatē yāga ēva niyōgaḥ
tannirvr̥ttyā ca niyōganirvr̥ttiḥ । dravyaguṇasaṁskāraiśca yāgō
nirvartyatē । ataḥ tēṣāmēva pārārthyaṁ ēvaṁ manyatē bādarirā-
cāryaḥ । nanu svargaṁ yāgēna kuryāṁdātmārthaṁ iti niyōgaḥ ।
ātmanēpadaprayōgāt । naivaṁ śabdāt pratipat‍tuṁ śakyatē dvitīyā hi
kārakasya prādhānyaṁ pratipādayati । yasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ tatkārakam ।

﻿<pb n="b638"/>
na ca svargē yāgasya kārakamiti siddham । na ca
vēdāt kriyākārakasaṁbandhāvagatiḥ । siddhasya hi anuṣṭhānaṁ
cōdyatē । kathaṁ tarhi yadāhavanīyē juhvatīti ? yuk‍taṁ
pramāṇāntarēṇa saṁbhavadarśanāt । svargē punarnaitadupapadyatē vēdasyā-
prāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt । kiñca kartr̥viśēṣaṇaṁ cātra svarga(kāma)śabdaḥ
na kartr̥viśēṣaṇamīpsitatamaṁ bhavati rājapuruṣaṁ paśyētivat ।
﻿<pb n="b639"/>
atō na svargaṁ kuryāditi niyōgaviṣayatā śakyatē pratipat‍tum ।
kathaṁ tarhi svargakāmapadasaṁbandhāt svargaṁ bhāvayēditi bhāṣyam । ēva-
mētadbhāṣyaṁ anyathā hi svargamiti śravaṇāt svargaṁ bhāvayēditi syāt ।
﻿<pb n="b640"/>
ata ēva svayamēva tadbhavatītyētadabhiprāyaṁ tat । nimittamātra-
kathanaṁ hi tat karmaṇaḥ । ataḥ prayōjanaṁ svargō yāgasya na
karma pākasyēva grāsaḥ । atō dravyaguṇasaṁskārāṇāmēva sādhya-
sādhanabhāvāvagatēḥ prayōjanavattayā śēṣabhāvaḥ । na punaḥ karmatvē-
nāpratīyamānayōḥ phalapuruṣayōrapi syāt । tasmāt sūk‍taṁ
dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣu bādariḥ iti । <quote>1na cēt phalayāgau guṇabhāvēna cōdyētē
kasya puruṣaḥ pradhānabhūtō bhaviṣyatīti</quote> । kō'yaṁ prādhānyapratiṣēdhaḥ
śēṣatā hi puruṣasya pratiṣēdhyā <q>“na yāgaphalapuruṣēṣu”</q> iti
pratijñānāt । ucyatē । śēṣatānivr̥ttyarthamēva prādhānyaṁ
pratiṣidhyatē । kathaṁ ? sati hi prādhānyē puruṣaḥ śēṣa iti
﻿<pb n="b641"/>
śakyatē vak‍tum । kimiti ? puruṣaśabdō hyayaṁ svargakāmē prayuktaḥ
yadi tadarthaḥ svargaṁ syāt tadā tadviśiṣṭasya śēṣatā syāt ।
svadravyaviśiṣṭasyēva prayājādēḥ । atādarthyē punaḥ svargasya kēvalaṁ
kartr̥tayaiva śēṣabhāvaḥ dravyamātratayētyarthaḥ na puruṣaśēṣatayā । na
svargakāmapadavācyatayētyabhiprāyaḥ । tasmādanavadyam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt1 ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ phalārthatā karmaṇaḥ ? kāminō hi adhikārō yāgē । sa
ca phalasādhanatāṁ yāgasyānāpādayan na siddha‍yatīti ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b642"/>
yadi punarayaṁ yāgaḥ phalē sādhanabhāvaṁ na pratipadyatē tatra kō dōṣaḥ ।
na khalu kaścit । pratīyatē tu tathā । nanu śēṣalakṣaṇē śēṣatā
pratipādayituṁ nyāyyā, kimidamucyatē 1<quote>ēnamēvārthaṁ ṣaṣṭhē sūtrairēva sādhayiṣyati</quote>
iti, kiṁ vā śrutyādivyatirik‍taṁ kiñcidanyat śēṣatvē pramāṇamasti ।
atha śrutyādīnāmanyatamaṁ tadihaivōpanyasanīyaṁ kimiti sānyāsikaṁ
kriyatē । atrōcyatē---adhikārāpēkṣiṇī hi sā na śrutyapēkṣō'dhikāra
iti sānyāsikaṁ yāgaphalaśēṣatvaṁ yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b643"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">phalaṁ ca puruṣārthatvāt ।। 5 ।।1</ab>
<p>phalamapi puruṣaṁ pratyupadiśyatē yaḥ svargō mē syādityēvaṁ
kāmayatē tasya, niyōgaḥ na svargaḥ ātmānaṁ labhētēti । kutaḥ
ātmanēpadaprayōgāt ।2</p>
<p>nanu ca svargakāmaśabdādēvēdamavagamyatē svargō mē bhavēditi ।
kimidamātmanēpadaprayōgāditi । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ parasya duḥkhaṁ
kāmayata ityatrāpi kamēḥ prayōgēnānātmasaṁbandhitvēnāpi dr̥ṣṭa iti
tadayuktam, tatra paraśabdaprayōgāt duḥ khasya ca parasambandhitvē-
nābhīṣṭatvāt । yatra punaḥ paraśabdō na śrūyatē nāpyaniṣṭaṁ duḥ khaṁ tatra
kēnānyēna kāmyamānasya saṁbandhō'nyatra kāmayituḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b644"/>
<p>atha manyasē kāmyamānēnaiva kāmaḥ saṁbadhyatē svargō bhavatviti ।
na hi; tannibandhanasukhāsmaraṇāt । na kasyacit (kāmamātrēṇa)
sadbhāvamātrē kasyacitkāmō bhavati । tasmādātmanēpadōpanyāsō
liṅgatayā pratipattavyaḥ na punaḥ prāptē pramāṇatayā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">puruṣaśca karmārthatvāt1 ।। 6 ।।</ab>
<p>svargaścētpuruṣārthaḥ svargakāmapadavācyatayaiva <q>‘yajamānēna saṁmitau-
dumbarī bhavati’</q> ityādiṣu kartuḥ śēṣatvaṁ kathaṁ ? adhikr̥tasya kartr̥tvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b645"/>
kartuśca yajamānaśabdavācyatvāt । tasmāt sūk‍taṁ sūtratrayaṁ
jaiminēḥ vr̥ttikāramatōpanyāsaḥ pūrvapakṣāparījñānārthaḥ । kimiti
kalpāntaraṁ na bhavati । na hi āpēkṣikaṁ śēṣatvamasti । viniyō-
jyanibandhanaṁ hi tat । viniyōga ēvāpēkṣika iti । satyam । śēṣaḥ
viniyōjyaṁ śēṣiṇaṁ cāpēkṣitē na punarēkasya śēṣaśēṣitāmāpādayati ।
﻿<pb n="b646"/>
vrīhyādīnāṁ ca svaśēṣāpēkṣatayā tulyatvāt । tasmāt svakauśala-
pradarśanārthaṁ paramatamupanyastaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">tēṣāmarthēna saṁbandhaḥ1 ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>uktaṁ niyōgasavyapēkṣāṇi śrutyādīni viniyōjakāni
śāstrāntaravihitasaṁbandhitayā ca kāryalābha ityuktam । śāstrā-
ntaravihitaṁ(yuktaṁ) hi śēṣi bhavati na śēṣaśāstrādēva prādhānyamava-
gamyata iti sak‍tuṣu darśitam । śāstrāntaravihitāni ca vrīhyādīni
﻿<pb n="b647"/>
kathaṁ tatsuṁyuk‍tēṣu saṁśayaḥ । kāryaśūnyē hi śēṣaśās‍traṁ kalpyaṁ kārya-
pamēkṣatē । pratyakṣaśrutakāryaṁ tu sandihyata ityayuktam । ucyatē ।
niyōgādanyat viniyōgagamyaṁ kāryamastīti na śakyatē vak‍tum ।</p>
<p>nanu ca <q>‘yaistu dravyaṁ cikīrṣyatē’</q> iti nāpūrvaṁ
kāryamityuktam । satyam । sthitē ētasmin śēṣatvē tat । śēṣa-
tvamēvēdānīṁ niyōganirvr̥ttyā vinā nāvagamyatē ityākṣēpaḥ ।
kimiti vā na niyōgōniṣpādyatē vrīhīn prōkṣatīti ।
yadyatra niyōgārthaniṣpattiḥ, darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanēna na
﻿<pb n="b648"/>
saṁbadhyēta । atha <q>‘phalavatsannidhau’</q> iti saṁbandhaḥ sa tu niyōgaikya-
lakṣaṇa iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ । atrāpicēt sa ēva saṁbandhaḥ
na tarhi vrīhīn prōkṣatītyētāvataiva niyōgasiddhiḥ । ataḥ
tuṣakaṇavipramōcanaṁ na svargāvāptivat nāntarīyakō niyōgasya ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ tarhi kō'yamupanyāsaḥ <q>‘auṣadhē sānnāyyē ca karmavyā’1</q>
iti । naiva hi padārthānāṁ prādhānyamasmin pakṣē । ucyatē---naiva hi
﻿<pb n="b649"/>
padārthānāṁ prādhānyaparō'yaṁ granthaḥ kiṁ tarhi sarvēśēṣatābhiprāyaparaḥ ।
nanu cāsminnapi pakṣē śēṣaśēṣitaiva nōpapadyatē aṅgapradhānām ।
sarvaśēṣāṇāṁ niyōgārthaśēṣatvāt । prakaraṇapramāṇasvarūpanirūpaṇē'sya
cōdyasya parihāraṁ vakṣyāmaḥ । iha tu kāryāntarāsaṁbhavāta
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanēna asaṁbandhādityuktam ।
tasmāt prayājādīnāmēva niyōgō hyētallakṣaṇaḥ sarvēṣā-
mabhisaṁbandhaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi vrīhīn ājyaṁ iti ca । asmin
pakṣē sak‍tuvadētadbhaviṣyati । gāṁ dadāti itivadvā ।
﻿<pb n="b650"/>
ata idamuktam । 1<quote>avadhātādayastu padārthāḥ śrutyā vidhīyanta</quote> iti ।
bhāvārthānāṁ śrutyā niyōgasaṁbandhaścētyarthaḥ । vākyēnaiṣāṁ vrīhyādi-
saṁbandha iti bhāvārthānupravēśēna dravyādīnāṁ tu niyōgasaṁbandha
ityarthaḥ na pradhānabhūtānāṁ, na hi dravyaparyantō niyōgaḥ
svaya2mēvasādhyatvāt tasmāt sūk‍taṁ sarvē sarvārthā iti ।
﻿<pb n="b651"/>
kimidamadr̥ṣṭaṁ bhavatīti । adr̥ṣṭamapūrvaṁ niyōga ityēkamida-
mityuk‍taṁ <q>‘atō'pūrvaṁ kr̥tvā’</q>iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">phalaṁ tu saha cēṣṭayā śabdārthō'bhāvādviprayōgē syāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>atrōcyatē । syāt sarvārthatā yadi hi kāryārthē virōdhō
niyōgasya syāt । na tvatra virōdhō vidyatē । kathaṁ na vidyatē
virōdhaḥ ? kathaṁ vā vidyatē virōdhaḥ । uktaṁ kāryāntaratvāt tuṣakaṇa-
vipramōkasyēti । na ca kāryaṁ kāryāntarē saṁbadhyatē yathā svargaḥ
paśubhiḥ ēvaṁ niyōgaḥ kāryaṁ tuṣakaṇavipramōkaścēti viprati-
ṣiddham । anabhijñō bhavān viṣayaniyōjyānāmityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b652"/>
kathaṁ anabhijñaḥ ? viṣayō hi 1nāmādhikārasaṁbandhī svargakāmō
yajēta iti । tasya ca niyōgasiddhirēva prayōjanam । dr̥ṣṭē'rthē
saṁbhavatyapi yathā gōdōhanēna paśukāmasya praṇayēditi ।</p>
<p>nanu cātrāpi phalasiddhiḥ; niyōgasiddha‍yarthā phalasiddhiḥ
iti ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । ata ēva ca <q>‘karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt’</q>
﻿<pb n="b653"/>
<q>‘phalaṁ ca puruṣārthatvāt’</q> <q>‘puruṣaśca karmārthatvāt’</q> iti viṣaya-
niyōga1 ēva upasaṁhr̥taṁ sakalasya padārthajātasya śēṣatvam ।
niyōjyaḥ idānīṁ kaḥ ? akārakabhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭa iti ṣaṣṭhē
vakṣyāmaḥ । kaḥ punarasau ? adhikr̥taḥ karmaṇi ? kimidaṁ adhikr̥taṁ
iti ? nanu ca kartaivādhikr̥taḥ । yathā na karturadhikārō'dhi-
kr̥tasya kartr̥tvamiti ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । yadyēvaṁ kimāyātaṁ vrīhīn
prōkṣatītyatra । kāryāntarēpi niyōgāvirōdha itīdamēvāyātam ।
﻿<pb n="b654"/>
vrīhīnprōkṣatīti pradhānabhūtaviṣayasaṁsparśānniyōgasya na niyōgāntarā-
vagatiḥ samidādīnāmiva । nanu kāryāntaramityuktam । kāryā-
ntaratvē ca niyōgāntarāvagatiḥ sōmēṣṭīnāmiva । satyaṁ
yadi kāryāntaraṁ syāt । kathaṁ na kāryāntaraṁ ? adhikāra-
niyōgākṣēpāt taṇḍulaniṣpattēḥ svargasiddhivanna kāryāntaram ।
﻿<pb n="b655"/>
tasmādadhikāraniyōga ēvāyaṁ vrīhīn prōkṣati iti prayājādī-
nāmiva । iyān viśēṣaḥ dr̥ṣṭakāryadvārakastvayaṁ sākṣānniyōga-
kārya ēva prayājādiḥ na ca dvāramēva pratibandhakaṁ bhavitumarhati ।
viśēṣatō dr̥ṣṭasākṣānniyōgasaṁbandhānāmapi dvāraṁ kalpyam । idaṁ ca
klr̥ptamiti viśēṣaḥ । tathā ca dvārakalpanāmantarēṇa pradhānēti-
kartavyatāsiddhirna bhavati tathā prakaraṇapramāṇa ēva vakṣyāmaḥ । tadida-
muktaṁ pramāṇābhāvānna sarvārthatēti । na hi dr̥ṣṭē saṁbhavati
saṁbandhahētau kalpyaṁ hētvantaramātmānaṁ labhatē ityarthaḥ ।
nanu ca viniyōgataḥ kāryaṁ, na kāryatō viniyōgaḥ
﻿<pb n="b656"/>
parihr̥tamētat śāstrāntaradr̥ṣṭaviṣayatvāditi । ata ēva bhēdā-
bhēdalakṣaṇaṁ hēturiti । tasmāt sūk‍taṁ phalaṁ tu saha cēṣṭayēti ।
kāryānurōdhī niyōga ityarthaḥ । atō yē yatra śrūyanta
iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">dravyaṁ cōtpattisaṁyōgāt tadarthamēva cōdyēta ।। 11 ।। a. 5 ।।</ab>
<p>idaṁ cintyatē spha‍yaśca kapālāni cēti sannidhāpanavidhayaḥ
saṁyōgatō'viśēṣāt prakaraṇāviśēṣāccēti kiṁ sarvārthatayā'vagamyantē
uta <q>‘spha‍yēnōddhanti’</q> ityēvamādibhiḥ upasaṁhriyanta iti । kiṁ
tāvada‍yuk‍taṁ ? nōpasaṁhriyanta iti । kutaḥ ? aśak‍tēḥ । kathamaśaktiḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b657"/>
sannidhānē hi viniyōgaikyāt dvāramātrānujñānācca dr̥ṣṭadvāra-
katvamēva śakyatē vak‍tum । kalpyapratipakṣatvāt । na punaḥ
dr̥ṣṭaviśēṣadvāramapi । tasmāt śaktitō vyavasthāḥ । atrābhidhīyatē ।
syādētadēvaṁ yadi dvāramātramēvānurudhyatē niyōgēna (tataḥ) saṁbandhānu-
sārī hi niyōgaḥ । (kathaṁ tarhi aruṇād‍yupanyāsēna nirākaraṇaṁ
āsthitē guṇavacanatvē aruṇādivadbhaviṣyati vākyē niyōga
iti ।) uktaṁ śāstrāntaravihitaviṣayatvānniyōgasyēti । ataḥ
sannidhāpanavidhayō na saṁbandhavidhēḥ pratipakṣāḥ bhavitumarhanti tanmūla-
tvāt iti । ataḥ siddhamatrāpi yē yatra śrūyanta iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b658"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">arthaikatvē dravyaguṇayōraikakarmyānniyamaḥ syāta1 ।। 12 ।। a. 6 ।।</ab>
<p>saṁskāradravyavidhayō yē yatra śrūyantē tē tatraivētyuktam । guṇē
idānīṁ cintyatē---kiṁ yē yatra śrūyantē tatraiva uta kr̥ts‍nē prakaraṇē
nivēśa iti । nanu ca anvitapadārthakatvāt padānāṁ naiva kēvalaguṇa-
vacanatā saṁbhavati yathā na kēvalākr̥tivacanatā <q>‘ālabhēta’</q> iti na
kēvalaguṇavacanatā śakyatē vak‍tuṁ yathā <q>‘vāyavyaṁ ś‍vētamālabhēta’</q> iti ।
satyaṁ aparityaktadravyasyaivānvayō yatra dr̥śyatē amūrtasya naiva
tadudāharaṇam । yatra punaḥ parityaktadravyābhiprāyē kēvalaguṇavacana-
syānvayaḥ yathā paṭasya śukla iti bhavati tatra saṁśayaḥ । kāraka-
vibhak‍tau satyāmapi kiṁ kriyānvayī guṇavacana uta kēvaladravyā-
nvayyēvēti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b659"/>
<p>nanu ca kēvalaguṇavacanatā asyāsmin vākyē naiva pratīyatē
paṭasya śukla iti(vat) ṣaṣṭhīnirdēśāt dravyasya tēna saṁbandhāvagatēśca
śuklaśabdasya yuktaṁ kēvalaguṇavacanasyānvayitvam । iha punaḥ
aruṇayēti kārakanirdēśāt kriyāsaṁbandhāvagatiḥ । tadava-
gatēśca guṇamātrasyāśak‍tēḥ aparityaktadravyasyaivānvayō yuktaḥ
ś‍vētamālabhētēti vat । ucyatē । na dravyasambandhā-
vagatirēva tatra guṇavacanatvē hētuḥ dravyāntarānavagatirapi
dravyāntarāvagatau hi paṭasya śuklō bhāga itivat guṇaguṇinōḥ
saṁbandhō na syāt । yadyēvaṁ kimāyātaṁ aruṇayēti ?
﻿<pb n="b660"/>
idamāyātam । atrāpi ēkahāyanyā na dravyāntaraṁ pratīyatē ।
ataḥ ēkahāyanīśabdōpāttatvāt dravyasya nāruṇāśabdaḥ dravyā-
ntarōpaniviṣṭaṁ guṇamabhidhātuṁ śaknōti । ēkahāyanyupanivēśē ca
na krayasambandha ityupariṣṭādvakṣyatē । tasmāt padāntarōpāttadravyakē
vākyē kēvalaguṇavacanānvayitaivēti sthitam । ata upapadyatē
saṁśayaḥ । kiṁ vākyaṁ bhitvā prakaraṇē nivēśō guṇasya dravyayōgitvāt
uta karaṇanirdēśāt krayaṇa ēvēti । kathamēvaṁ sthitē guṇavacanatvē <quote>“1nanu
naivāyaṁ guṇavacanaḥ, kiṁ tarhi ? dravyavacanaḥ</quote> ityākṣēpaḥ upapadyatē । ucyatē---s‍trī-
liṅganirdēśāt, dravyāśritatvāt । prātipadikārthagatatvācca liṅgasya ।
﻿<pb n="b661"/>
kimaruṇayētyēvamādidarśanaṁ nāstyākṣēpavādinaḥ । na nāstidarśanaṁ,
kintu aruṇayētyēvamādiṣu nētyabhiprāyaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi aruṇāda‍yu-
panyāsēna nirākaraṇaṇam ? aruṇādiṣu prayōgasādhutēti । kathamaruṇā-
valliṅgamiti dravyavacanatānirākaraṇam । sthitē guṇavacanatvē
dr̥ḍhatarēṇa kāraṇēna aruṇāvalliṅgaṁ bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ <quote><q>“atha krīṇātinā
na sambadhyēta tasminnēva vākyē ēkahāyanīśabdēna sambhantsyatē na bhaviṣyati vākyabhēda”</q></quote>
iti vadataḥ kō'bhiprāyaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---yadā dvayōḥ kriyā-
sambandhaḥ tadā dravyāntaranirōdhāt kēvalaguṇavacanatā aruṇayēti ।
yadā punaḥ kriyāsambandhō nāsti tadā āśritatvāda‍guṇānāṁ 
dravyāṇāṁ ca tadāśrayatvēna guṇānāṁ kō nāma dravyasaṁbandhaṁ
niruṇāddhi yathā nīlōtpalamiti । atrōttaram---prātipadikāttā-
﻿<pb n="b662"/> 
vata guṇa ēva pratīyatē padāntarasaṁbandhāt‍tu aparityaktadravya-
kō'nvayaḥ । liṅgaṁ ca vākyādbalīyaḥ । kimidaṁ vākyālliṅgaṁ
balīya iti । aidamarthyē hi balābalamuktam na punaranvayayō-
gē'pi । ucyatē । anvayayōgē ca anvayāvagatau satyāṁ kēna
balābalaṁ nivāryatē । uktaṁ cāsmābhiḥ । padāntarēṇa dravyōpādānāt
kriyāsaṁbandhācca padadva‍yasya kēvalaguṇānvayitā na śakyā vākyēna
bādhitum । atrēdānīmuttaram---kriyāyōgitvē'nanvayamālōcya
ananvayādvaraṁ dravyānvayaḥ dravyānvayitvēpi kriyānvayō nātidūraṁ
parityaktō bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b663"/>
<p>avaśyaṁ caitadēvābhyupagantavyam । anyathā hi prakaraṇasaṁbandhō-
'pi na syāt prakaraṇē hi kriyayā dravyēṇa vā anvayaḥ । kriyayā
tāvannasaṁbandha ityuktam । atha liṅgāt dravyēṇāpi na saṁbadhyatē
hanta ananvayitā'bhyupagatābhavati । na ca ananvayitā abhi-
dhānasya dharmō lōkē dr̥ṣṭaḥ । tasmādvaramasminnēva vākyē dravya-
saṁbandhābhyupagamaḥ । ata ēva nīlōtpalādiṣvapyanvayō(na)
dr̥śyatē । anyathā hi saṁbandhābhidhānavibhaktiśūnyānāmapi kathaṁ
vānvayaḥ syāt 1<quote><q>“naitadēvamiti”</q></quote> । satyamēva vaibhaktikō'pi
saṁbandhaḥ abhidhānalakṣaṇō bhavati yadyapratipakṣō bhavēt
ayaṁ tu sapratipakṣaḥ । ataḥ tr̥tīyānuguṇamēvāsyānvayitvaṁ
﻿<pb n="b664"/>
kalpayitavyam, na punaḥ kēvalābhidhānānuguṇam । tasmāt na
nīlōtpalavat saṁbandha upapadyatē । ucyatē । yadi tr̥tīyārthaḥ
prātipadikārthānvayavirōdhī syāt syādētadēvam । sa punaḥ prāptatvānnaiva
virudhyatē । atō yāvadaprāptamēkahāyanyā saṁbadhyata iti na dōṣaḥ ।
bhavēdētadēvaṁ yadyēkahāyanī nānyārthā, sāpi tvanyārthaiva । na ca
dvayōranyārthayōḥ mithaḥ saṁbandhaḥ saṁbhavati । kimarthā punarēkāhayanī ?
krayārthēti brūmaḥ । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ tulyē samabhivyāhārē krayārthā
ēkahāyanī na punaḥ guṇasaṁbandhārthā । atra bhāṣyaṁ <q>“abhihitamapi
punaḥ paryanuyujyata”</q> iti । yadyabhihitaṁ kimiti paryanuyujyatē ।
anyārthasyānyēva saṁbandhaḥ virōdhapradarśanārthaṁ tadarthamēvōttaraṁ tr̥tīyā-
﻿<pb n="b665"/>
saṁbandhāt krayārthatēti । anyārthamapyanyēna saṁbadhyata iti na
dōṣaḥ । śaknōti hi ākāṅkṣāvataḥ anyārthamapi sannihitamā-
kāṅkṣāṁ pūrayitum sannidhānāviśēṣāt । satyaṁ, śak‍nōti na puna
ryadarthaṁ tatsaṁbandhitayaiva । nanu ca tatsaṁbandhinyapi sannidhānama-
viśiṣṭam itarasya cākāṅkṣā । bhavēdētadēvaṁ yadi sannidhānamaviśiṣṭaṁ
iha tu sannidhānamapyanyārtham । na cānyārthaṁ sannidhānamākāṅkṣati
svārthasiddhayē । satyamēvam । tasyāvaśyānvayabhāvitvāt ।
abhidhānasya cānyasyāsannidhānāt anyārthatāmavakr̥ṣya
sannidhānamātraṁ parigr̥hyatē । tathā ca rātrisatrādiṣu dr̥ṣṭam ।
﻿<pb n="b666"/>
yuktamuktam, kintvatra prakaraṇāt sannidhānamananyārthaṁ vidyatē ।
tasmādvākyabhēdādēvānvayō yuktaḥ ananyārthasya saṁbandhinō'vagamāt
ataḥ prakaraṇē sarvasmin‍nivēśa ityēvaṁ prāptē brūmaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">arthaikatvē dravyaguṇayōraikakarmyānniyamaḥ syāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>kraya ēvāruṇimā niviśatē । kathaṁ ? tatsaṁbandhapratipattēḥ tr̥tī-
yātaḥ । nanu kēvalaguṇavacanatvāt na kriyayā saṁbadhyata ityuktam ।
duruktaṁ tat । kathaṁ duruktam ? yasya hi yādr̥śaṁ kriyāsādhanatvaṁ dr̥ṣṭaṁ
﻿<pb n="b667"/>
tasya tathāvidhasyaiva vibhaktayaḥ saṁbandhamāpādayanti । dravyaviśēṣaṇa-
tayā ca guṇaḥ kriyāṁ niṣpādayati । aviśiṣṭasya kāraṇatvānu-
papattēḥ । nanu cānupāttadravyaka ēvāyaṁ prayōgaḥ paṭasya śukla
iti vadityuktam । tatsatyamuktaṁ na punaranupāttadravyatayā kriyā-
saṁbandhō'pahnōtuṁ śakyatē । svavyāpārāpēkṣitvāt kriyāyōgasya ।
na cānupāttadravyatayā vyāpārahāniḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । svavyā-
pārāpēkṣāṇi kārakāṇi kriyayā saṁbadhyantē iti na kārakāntara-
vyāpāramapēkṣantē । nāpyarthāntaragataṁ hānamupādānaṁ vā'bhidhānasya ।
﻿<pb n="b668"/>
tasmādbhinnavyāpārakatvādēkahāyanīdvāraka ēva krayasaṁbandha upapannaḥ ।
ata ēva ca na vikalpaḥ prayōjanavada‍dravyāntara---
saṁbandhārthaṁ kriyāyāḥ prādhānyam । tatprādhānyē tu na pratyēkaṁ
vākyaparisamāptiḥ । tasmādēkavākyatvātsiddhaṁ dravyaguṇayōraikakarmyā-
nniyama iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">ēkatvayuktamēkasya śrutisaṁyōgāt1 ।। 3-4-13 ।। (a. 7)</ab>
<p>uktō dravyaguṇasaṁskārāṇāṁ viniyōgaḥ । idānīṁ viniyōjya-
viṣayagatā cintā kriyatē । ēvaṁ śrūyatē <q>‘grahaṁ saṁmārṣṭi’</q> iti ।
﻿<pb n="b669"/>
tatra saṁśayaḥ---kiṁ śōṣiṇō viśēṣaṇaṁ śōṣitvē ādriyatē śēṣasyēva śēṣa-
tvē uta nēti । kathaṁ punaratra saṁśayaḥ ? yuktaṁ nāvacchēṣaḥ upādīyamāna-
tvāt tadupayōgiviśēṣaṇam । śēṣiṇaḥ punaḥ kāryāntarē nirjñātaśēṣa-
bhāvasyaiva svaśēṣayōgō yukta iti na saṁśayaṁ manyāmahē । ucyatē ।
śrutitaḥ sarvaṁ kalpatē nōpādēyatvāt paśōrēkatvam, kiṁ tarhi ?
śrutēḥ । śrutiścēnnādriyatē dvitvaṁ bahutvaṁ vā kimiti śōṣitayā nōpā-
dīyatē । ataḥ śēṣiṇyapi yathaiva grahaśrutirādriyatē ēvamēkatvaśrutirapi
aviśēṣāt । tadidamuk‍taṁ---<q>‘ēkatvayuktamēkasya śrutisaṁyōgādi’</q>ti ।
﻿<pb n="b670"/>
ata ēva ca <q>‘agnīnādadhīta’</q> iti bahutvasiddhiḥ yūpaṁ chinatti’
iti ca ēkatvam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">sarvēṣāṁ vā lakṣaṇatvādaviśiṣṭaṁ hi lakṣaṇam ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>atrōcyatē---naitadēvaṁ yadēkasya saṁskāra iti । saṁskārō hi nāma
vyāpārāntarayōgyatā । yasya saṁskārō vyāpārāntarayōgyatālakṣaṇaḥ
saṁbhavati sa ēva saṁbandhitāmāpadyatē । nanu ca sasaṅkhyāka
ēva saṁskārēṇa vyāpārāntarayōgyaḥ kriyatē । kutaḥ ? vyāpārāntaraṁ
upādānaśēṣatvāt saṅakhyāyā liṅgasya ca । yathābhūtaścāsau śēṣaḥ
tathābhūtasyaiva saṁskārasaṁbandhaḥ kāryārthatvāt । aindravāyavādi-
﻿<pb n="b671"/>
vākyēṣu ca ēkatvayuktā ēva grahāḥ śēṣatvēna śrūyantē । atō-
'vivakṣitamityayuktam । na ca grahamātraṁ śēṣaḥ ēkaikasya
viniyōgāt ।</p>
<p>nanu viniyuktasyōpādānaśēṣatvaṁ saṅkhyādayaḥ pratipadyantē yathā
ca śēṣabhāvē prādhānyaṁ tathā śēṣibhāvēpi । bhavatu prādhānyaṁ na
kaścidvirōdhaḥ saṅkhyādyaparityāgēna tu yathaiva śēṣatāṁ pratipadyatē tathaiva
saṁskāryatāmapīti vadamāḥ । atrōcyatē---satyaṁ śēṣabhūtasyaiva saṁskāraḥ
tathāpi saṅkhyādayō na saṁbadhyantē । kutaḥ ? sarvatra hi padārthāntara-
saṁbandhaḥ pradhānasyaiva rājapuruṣamānayētivat । tatra hi rājārthaḥ
﻿<pb n="b672"/>
kēvalamupalakṣaṇatayaiva bhāti । ēvamatrāpi dravyamēva pradhānaṁ, yadanyatta-
dupalakṣaṇaṁ jātyādi । na ca upalakṣaṇasya kāryasaṁbandhaḥ । ata
idamuktaṁ aviśiṣṭaṁ hi lakṣaṇamiti । nahyēkatvadīnāṁ vilakṣaṇatvē
grahāntaranivr̥ttau sāmarthyamasti saṁbandhī hi saṁbandhyantaraṁ nivartayati ।
nanu cōktaṁ na saṁbandhimātraṁ(tā) saṁbandhī hētuḥ kastarhi ? śrutyādi-
pratipādyatēti । atra caikatvaviśiṣṭaḥ śrutyā pratipādyatē śēṣī ।
kathaṁ ca śakyatē vak‍tum śrutipramāṇakē vastuni ēkatvamaviva-
kṣitamiti । na cōddiśyamānatvaṁ vidhīyamānatvaṁ vā śrutiṁ vihanti ।
śrutividhātē hi grahēpyaprāptiḥ syāt । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ uddiśya-
mānasya viśēṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti । asyaivārthasyāsminnadhikaraṇē
hēturvaktavyaḥ na cāsāvastītyuktamiti । ucyēta---ayamasti hētuḥ
﻿<pb n="b673"/>
kāryavaduddiśyamānaṁ pradhānībhavati । pradhānasya vidhēyēna saṁbandhō'tra
na pradhānasya guṇānāṁ, yasmāt guṇānāṁ pradhānōpādānanimittaṁ
tadupādānaśēṣatvam ।</p>
<p>kē punaramī guṇāḥ yē vibhaktyabhidhēyāḥ prātipadikārthasya ।
kathaṁ guṇatā vibhaktyarthānāṁ ? prātipadikārthaṁ pratyavacchēdakatvāt ।
vibhaktyarthō hi prātipādikārthamavacchinatti । avacchēdakatayā ca
upādānaśēṣatā । tasmāt siddhaṁ saṅkhyādēḥ dravyaṁ prati guṇatvaṁ
vibhaktyabhidhēyasya । na ca guṇānāṁ guṇaiḥ saha saṁbandhō
vidyatē guṇaścāyaṁ saṁskārō nāma । uk‍taṁ ca guṇānāṁ ca
parārthatvāt” iti । athāpi nāma prātipādikābhidhēya
ēvāyamarthō jātyādiḥ viniyōjyaśca । tathāpyanuddiśyamānō
naiva pradhānatāṁ śaknōti pratipat‍tum । kimiti ? uddēśōhi nāma
﻿<pb n="b674"/>
kāryāvacchinnasya vastunō bhavati na padārthamātrāvacchinnasya । atō
jātyādibhiḥ dravyamēvōpalakṣayitavyam । na hi dravyaviśēṣādr̥tē
kāryaviśēṣaparyavasānaṁ bhavati । tasmādupalakṣaṇatayaiva tatra jātyā-
dēranvayaḥ na punaḥ kārakatayā । nanu caivaṁ sati upādēyatvēpi kārya-
viśēṣānavagāt jātyādīnāmupalakṣaṇataiva । na caivamiṣyatē jātirēvāṅga-
miti mīmāṁsakāḥ । anabhijñō bhavān upāttōpādēyayōḥ upātta-
dravyalakṣaṇaṁ hyuddiśyamānapadārthō bhavati । vidhēyaṁ punaḥ kamupalakṣa-
yati ? vihitatvāddhi kāryasidhyarthaṁ svāśrayaṁ dravyamākṣipati nōpalakṣa-
yati । ata uddiśyamānasya upalakṣaṇatvāt dravyē saṁpratyayō bhavati
﻿<pb n="b675"/>
na punaḥ svasaṁbandhinyabhidhēyē । tasmāt kāryamātramēvāpēkṣatē'vacchē-
dakatayā na punaḥ śrutyā'bhihitamēkatvādikam । (tarhi) upāttataiva
tatra viśēṣāvagamē hētuḥ । yatpunarupādēyaṁ tat śrutita ēva viśiṣṭa-
mavagantavyam, nānyata iti viśēṣaḥ । sō'yamuktō hētuḥ uddiśya-
mānasya viśēṣaṇamavivakṣitamityatrārthē । upāttatvādityuk‍tō hētuḥ ।
kā vārtā agnīnādadhīta yūpaṁ cchinattīti ? vivakṣitā saṅkhyā, atra
hīdamēvōpādānavākyam । nanu cāgnipadabhuddēśakam । pradhānabhūtāścā-
gnayaḥ । satyaṁ yathā bhavānāha । kintu dvividhō hyuddēśaḥ upāttasyānu-
pāttasya ca । grahaṁ saṁmārṣṭītyupāttōddēśaḥ ag‍nīnādadhītētyanupāttōddēśaḥ
﻿<pb n="b676"/>
anupāttañcōddiśyata iti kathamidaṁ ? vidhēyaviṣayō hyuddēśa ityucyatē,
nōpāttatvamanupāttatvaṁ ca uddēśyatvē hētuḥ । ataḥ pramāṇāntarasiddha-
viśēṣaṇaṁ uddiśyamānamavivakṣitaviśēṣaṇaṁ bhavati । yatpunaravijñāta-
viśēṣaṇamēvōddiṣṭaṁ tat vidhēyavat śrutita ēva viśiṣṭamavagantavyam ।
tasmāt suṣṭhūcyatē upāttōddēśē'vivakṣitaṁ viśēṣaṇamiti । nanu
ca grahaṁ saṁmārṣṭīti dvitīyēyaṁ kārakavibhaktiḥ kārakaṁ
ca kriyārthaṁ bhavatīti śābdāḥ । nanu īpsitatamē dvitīyē-
yam । satyaṁ, sā tu kārakē । nanu ca vipratiṣiddhaṁ
﻿<pb n="b677"/>
īpsitatamaṁ kārakaṁ cēti ? kathaṁ vipratiṣiddhaṁ ? kimidaṁ
īpsitatamaṁ nāma ? yadi tāvat yataḥ kriyāsiddhiḥ
tadīpsitatamaṁ ēvaṁ tarhi kārakamātrē prasaṅgaḥ tataśca viśēṣā-
bhidhānamanarthakamidaṁ karma idaṁ karaṇamiti । atha yatkriyayā āpyatē
utpādyatē saṁskriyatē vā tatkarmētyucyatē । na tarhi kārakaṁ kriyā-
paryavasānāpēkṣō hyāptyādikō guṇaḥ । paryavasitē hi vyāpārē phalaṁ
niṣpadyatē na punaḥ phala[sya]sādhyaiva kriyā bhavati । ataḥ īpsitaṁ
kārakaṁ cēti vipratiṣiddham । atrābhidhīyatē---na viprati-
ṣiddham । āptyādikō guṇaḥ kārakasthaścākārakasthaśca yadā kārakasthaḥ
﻿<pb n="b678"/>
tadā kārakamēva phalam । kimidaṁ kārakamēva phalamiti ? ।
yadā hi kārakamēva kayācidvikārāpattyā vyāpyamutpādyaṁ
saṁskāryaṁ vikāryaṁ cēṣṭaṁ tadā tadēva phalamityucyatē tāmēvāvasthā-
maṅgīkr̥tya īpsitatamavyapadēśaṁ labhata iti । kriyāsiddha‍yarthaṁ
phalasiddha‍yarthaṁ vā । ataḥ kārakamīpsitatamamiti na viruddham ।
vidyatē hi kārakaṁ na phalasamavāyi yathā karaṇādi । vidyatē
ca phalaṁ na kārakasamavāyi yathā svargādi । nanu
svargādyapi kārakasamavāyyēva kartr̥gāmi kriyāphalamiti vaca-
nāt । na kārakatayā phalasamavāyō vidyata iti ।
adhikāralakṣaṇavyāpārō'yaṁ adhikāralakṣaṇē uktaḥ । kathaṁ
tarhi bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ sūtraṁ kartrabhiprāyē kriyāphalē
﻿<pb n="b679"/>
iti ? asyāpi tatraivārthō nirūpyatē । atō grahaṁ
saṁmārṣṭīti yadyapi grahaḥ saṁmārgaṁ niṣpādayati tathāpi na tasyāṁ-
śasya vācikā vibhaktiḥ īpsitatamatvabhācaṣṭē phalāṁśaṁmityarthaḥ kriyā-
niṣpādyamiti yāvat । tasmāt śrutitō viśēṣāvagama iti
siddham । ataḥ upāttaviṣayaḥ saṁskāra iti sthitam । nanu ca
vyabhicāryētaddarśanam । anīpsitatamē'pi dvitīyā bhavatyēva । tataḥ
kim ? idaṁ tatō bhavati kārakāṁśābhidhāyinī na phalāṁśābhidhā-
yinī । ēvaṁ grahamityapi kārakamēvācaṣṭē । tataścaikatvamaviva-
kṣitamimi na śakyatē vak‍tum । kathaṁ tarhi grahārthaḥ saṁmārgaḥ
pramāṇābhāvāt । prayōjanavatvāt yathā paśupurōḍāśō'g‍nīṣōma-
dēvatārthaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---karmēpsitatamatvaṁ tāvat dvitīyā'bhidhattē ।
tathā yuk‍taṁ cānīpsitamiti tu kriyānirbāhyamēvētyarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b680"/>
iyān viśēṣaḥ kriyāntarasaṁbandhitayā ēkasyōpādānaṁ ēkasya nēti ।
ēvaṁ tarhi gāṁ dadātītyavivakṣitatvaṁ saṅkhyāyāḥ । bhavatviti cēnna;
prayōjanāntarakalpanāprasaṅgāt । kimiti kalpanā nēṣyatē ? pramāṇā-
bhāvāt । nanu ca dvitīyaiva pramāṇaṁ; satyaṁ, kāryāpēkṣāyāṁ viśēṣaṁ
samarpayāti na punaḥ kāryāntaramavagamayituṁ kṣamā, viniyōgaparyava-
sāyinyō hi vibhakta‍yaḥ na kāryaparyavasāyinyaḥ navā'dhikāra-
śūnyō niyōgō'stīti <q>‘phalavatsannidhau’</q> ityatra vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b681"/>
saṁskāravidhayastūktāḥ tēṣāmarthēna ityatra । uktōttaramapi kimiti
bhavatā paricōditaṁ ? (bhāvikārya)vismaraṇāparādhāditi manyāmahē
tadidaṁ smāryatē anupātaviṣayamidaṁ prādhānyamiti yūpavat siddhaṁ
vivakṣitatvaṁ saṅkhyāyāḥ । amunā ca viśēṣēṇa sūtrāntarapraṇayanaṁ
bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ akathitamiti । tatrāpi tathāyuktamityanuvartatē
tasmāt dvitīyāprādhānyaṁ na vyabhicaratīti sthitam । upāttē tu
viṣayē viśēṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti siddham । 1<quote>grahādiṣvēkatvaṁ
brūyāt na dvitīyādīn pratiṣēdhēt”</quote> iti । upāttaviṣayatvāt tu grahaśrutēḥ
upādēyē hyēkatvādayō viśēṣaṇam । iha punaḥ upāttataiva viśēṣā-
vargatau hēturityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b682"/>
<p>nanu ca <q>‘parisañcaṣṭa’</q> iti kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ---ēka-
tvamananvitaṁ syāt nānanvitānāmabhidhānamastītyuk‍taṁ tadbhūtā-
dhikaraṇē । naitadasti satyamananvitābhidhānamēkavacanasya prāpnōti na
punaḥ parisaṅkhyā saṁbhavati aprāptatvāt । grahasaṁbhārgādēḥ saṁbandhasya
prāptau satyāmanyanivr̥ttau niyōgaḥ prabhavati । aprāptē punaḥ yathā
ś‍vēti śrutiḥ na kākādīn nivartayituṁ kṣamā । na cānanvitā-
bhidhānam tasyāpi prāp‍tyavagamāt । nanu ca yuktaṁ śvādiṣu । ēkatvaṁ
punaḥ bahuṣūpādīyamānēṣu pakṣēpi na prāp‍nōti । atō'nanvitā-
bhidhānaṁ duṣpariharamiti । parihr̥tamidaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa na vibhak‍tērva-
canamēvaikaṁ prayōjanamiti । kathaṁ punaranēna parihr̥tamidaṁ bhavati ?
itthamanēna parihr̥taṁ bhavati-saṅkhyāyā ananvayē'pi karmamātrē prayōga-
darśanāt yathā brāhmaṇō na hantavya iti । atrāpi sādhyamiti cēt,
﻿<pb n="b683"/>
na nañarthē vadhēna saṁbadhyamānē ēkatvamanvētuṁ kṣamam । anyataḥ
pravr̥ttyavagamāt । tasmādēkatvābhidhānaṁ karmamātrē sādhviti
draṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p>1<quote>ayaṁ cāparō dōṣaḥ iti</quote> । ēkatvānvitābhidhānē āśrīyamāṇē
grahatvaṁ nōpāttaviṣayaṁ syāt anupāttaviṣayatvē ca grahatvasyānanvayaḥ
prāp‍nōti । ananvīyamānē ca saṁsargavidhānaṁ nirviṣayatvādanarthakam ।
﻿<pb n="b684"/>
<q>“athaikatvasaṁmārgasaṁbandhō vidhīyēta”</q> tatrāpi dvayī gatiḥ syāt anēna
guṇaphalasaṁbandhavadvidhānaṁ na saṁbhavatīti darśayati । anyatra syāditi
kathaṁ ? ēkatvaṁ tāvannōpāttasyōpalakṣaṇāya alaṁ bhavati ।
sammārgēṇa hi saṁbadhyamānaṁ pradhānaṁ vā bhavati guṇō vā
nānyaḥ saṁbandhō'sti । kathaṁ nāsti ? prātipadikāśritaṁ hi
saṅkhyābhidhānaṁ vibhak‍tīnāmityuktam । kasmānna viṣayatayā
uddēśyatayā vidhēyatayā vā saṁbandhaḥ saṁbhavati paratantratvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b685"/>
abhyupagamyāpyaruṇāvanna saṁbhavatītyuktaṁ grahasya pradhānatvāt ।
nanu ca pradhānēpi saṁbhavatyēva viśēṣaṇaṁ nimittabhūtaṁ kārakatva-
māśritya । kēna cōk‍taṁ na saṁbhavatīti ? iha punarvidhānāsaṁbhavaḥ
pradarśita pradhānatvāda‍grahasya । athōcyēta grahādi lakṣayitvā tasyaika-
tvasaṁbandhō vidhīyatē na saṁmārgasaṁbandha iti । kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhi-
prāyaḥ---kaḥ punaḥ pakṣapātaḥ saṁmārgō'nvayī na punarēkatvamiti ।
uttaraṁ---kriyāśūnyō'pyanvayō na saṅkhyādēḥ saṁbhavati । asati
tu vidhēyē saṁbhavatyapi na ca śrutyānvayaḥ ēkatvasyāstītyuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b686"/>
yadyavivakṣitamēkatvamiti1 lakṣaṇavirōdhaṁ darśayati । bahuṣu bahuvacana-
miti śābdāḥ । na vayamētadvicārayāmaḥ2 iti pramāṇataḥ sthitē lakṣyē
kiṁ lakṣaṇaṁ kariṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ । na cātra lakṣaṇavirōdhaḥ na
vibhak‍tērvacanamēvaikaṁ prayōjanamiti vyākhyātam । api ca grahaḥ
prātipadikārthaḥ ēkatvaṁ vibhaktyarthaḥ । kimatō yadyēvam ? ētadatō bhavati
prātipadikārthagataṁ hi vibhaktiḥ svamarthaṁ śrutyaiva vadatīti vibhaktya-
bhihitasya pāratantryaṁ darśayati । tacca vyākhyātam । atha yaduktaṁ
paśumālabhētēti upādēyānāṁ śrutitō viśēṣa ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">3saṁskārādvā guṇānāmavyavasthā syāt ।। 3-1.16 ।। a. 8.</ab>
<p>yadi kāryata upādānāṁ upāttasya ca lakṣaṇaṁ
﻿<pb n="b687"/>
śēṣitayaivēti tatō grahaśrutirapi hi sōmarasādhārē pātrē lakṣaṇaiva ।
ēkakāryatvāt । saṁmārgasya ca sōmarasāvasēkanirharaṇamēva prayō-
janamityupapannaṁ camasānāmapi saṁmārjanam । darśitaṁ caitadbhāṣya-
kārēṇa । sāmarthyataśca kāryasiddhau kēvalasammārgavidhānalābhaḥ
prakaraṇē mantrōpadēśavat । uktaṁ caitadbhāṣyakārēṇa ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">1vyavasthā vā'rthasya śrutisaṁyōgāt tasya śabdapramāṇatvāt ।। 3-1.17 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---śrutitaḥ upāttaparijñānaṁ nōpādā-
nāt śrutiḥ । śrutiśca grahaṁ saṁmārṣṭīti । nanu ca
sōmāvasiktaparimārjanaṁ tulyaṁ kāryamityuktam । satyamuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b688"/>
na śrutibādhē tatsamarthamityuktamasmābhiḥ । śrutē yadēva kāryaṁ tadēva
cēt kāryaṁ kimityaśrutē'pi na bhavati । na hi kāryaṁ śrūyatē ।
śrūyatē hi kāryamityuktam । kāryaṁ cēnna kriyatē kathaṁ yavēṣu prōkṣaṇam ?
yathā tat tathā navamē vakṣyāmaḥ । yaduk‍taṁ saṁsargamātra-
vidhānaṁ lābhō labhyata iti । tadayuktam । niyōgaviṣayatvāta
niyōgasya darśitaṁ ca bhāṣyakārēṇa । viniyōgē sati na
﻿<pb n="b688"/>
kaścidvirōdhō niyōgasya syāt sannikarṣasyāpi viśēṣāt । sa ca
virōdhē । iha tu virōdhābhāvādatantraṁ viprakarṣa iti siddham ।
ēkatvaṁ punaryathā nānvēti tathōktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">1ānarthakyāttadaṅgēṣu ।। 3-1-18 ।। a. 9</ab>
<p><q>‘saptadaśāratnirvājapēyasya yūpō bhavati’</q> ityatrōddēśakaṁ padaṁ kiṁ
vājapēyasya saptadaśēti uta yūpasya saptadaśēti । pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhi-
prāyaḥ । yadi yūpa ityuddēśakaṁ padaṁ vājapēyasyētyananvitābhidhānaṁ
﻿<pb n="b690"/>
prāp‍nōti yūpēna vājapēyasyāsaṁbandhāt । tasmāt vājapēyasaṁbandhini
yūpaśabdō draṣṭavyaḥ । ēvamanvitapadārthakō vākyārthaḥ samarthitō bhavati ।
atrābhidhīyatē । yadi yūpaśabdē śrautānvayini vājapēyasyētyananvitaṁ
syāt syādētadēvam । atra punaḥ saptadaśārat‍niryūpa ityapi saṁbandhē
vājapēyaśabdō'nvita ēva । kathaṁ ? saṁbandhasaṁbandhinyapi ṣaṣṭhyantasyā-
nvayadarśanāt dēvadattasya nap‍tētyēvamādiṣu । tasmādyūpaśabdasya
lākṣaṇikatvē nāsti pramāṇamiti yūpēnaiva saṁbandhaḥ । kimiti punaratra
vājapēyasyētyanēna kr̥tam ? kimasmākamanēna kr̥taṁ na kr̥tamiti ?
﻿<pb n="b691"/> 
anvayastāvadvidyatē । vidyamānānvayē tu vākyārthē kiñcitkāryayōgi
bhavati kiñcit prāptārthaṁ sadanūdyata iti na dōṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">1kartr̥guṇē tu karmasamavāyādvākyabhēdaḥ syāt ।। 3-1-19 ।। a. 10</ab>
<p>abhikrāmaṁ juhōtīti kiṁ karmaṇaḥ karmānvayō vidyatē uta nēti
cintyatē । kathaṁ punaranvayō vidyatē kathaṁ vā na ? tatra pūrvapakṣavādinō-
'bhiprāyaḥ na karma karmasādhyaṁ bhavati । tasmādyaḥ prakaraṇē kartā'bhi-
krāmatītyanvayaḥ । nanu ca prayājēṣvapi yaḥ kartā tatrāpyanvayō bhavatyēva ।
﻿<pb n="b692"/>
satyaṁ bhavati yadi juhōtītyabhidhāyakaḥ syāt । anabhidhāya-
katvē tasmin na karturuddēśyatvaṁ saṁbhavati nānr̥taṁ vadēditivat ।
tasmāt saṁyōgatō'viśēṣāt prakaraṇāviśēṣācca vākyabhēdaḥ । juhōti-
rōdānīṁ kimarthaḥ ? yadarthastadarthō bhaviṣyatīti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">1sākāṅkṣaṁ tvēkavākyaṁ syādasamāptaṁ hi pūrvēṇa ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>satyamananvayaḥ karmaṇaḥ karmaṇā । kartr̥saṁbandhāt tu
aruṇāvat saṁbhavatīti । nanu ca karturupādānaṁ
nāsti yathā ēkahāyanyāḥ, juhōtītyasyānabhidhāyakatvādi-
﻿<pb n="b693"/>
tyuktam । na brūmaḥ karturuddēśō'stīti । tannimittakastu karmōddē-
śē'pyanvayō na virudhyata iti, tatra tasya saṁbhavāt aruṇādhikaraṇa-
vaiṣamyam । tatra dvayōrapyanvayinōrupādānaṁ iha tu saṁbhavamātrēṇaivēti
viśēṣaḥ । yaduk‍taṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa pūrvapakṣē saṁbandhamātraparijñānāt
prayōgavacanāt kartavyatāsiddhiḥ iti tatraiva karturuddēśyatvaṁ na
virudhyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu saṁbhavamātrēṇānvaya-
siddhērna karturuddēśēna prayōjanamastīti manyatē । ataḥ siddhaṁ karmāpi
karmaṇāmuddēśyatāṁ pratipadyata iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b694"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">1sandigdhē tu vyavāyādvākyabhēdaḥ syāt ।। 3-1-21 ।। a. 11</ab>
<p>upavyayata ityatra sandihyatē---kiṁ sāmidhēnyanuvacanasya kartā
upavyānēna saṁbadhyatē uta kr̥ts‍nē prakaraṇa iti । nanu naivātrōddēśyaṁ
padaṁ kiñcicchrūyatē । anuddiṣṭapadārthaṁ ca yattat prakaraṇēnaiva saṁbadhyatē
saṁyōgatō'viśēṣāt prakaraṇāviśēṣāccētyuktam । ucyatē---ādhastyē
tāvadadhikaraṇē anuddiṣṭēnāpi kartrā'nvayō'pi na virudhyata
ityuktam । ēvamatrāpi sāmidhēnīnāṁ kartuḥ sannidhānāt
kriyāntarasādhanatayā upavyānasya lōkē'vagatatvāt anuddi-
ṣṭō'pi kartā sannihitaḥ kāryaparipūraṇāyālaṁ bhavitumarhati ।
﻿<pb n="b695"/> 
<quote>1nanu darśapūrṇamāsayōrēva prakaraṇamidam । paraprakaraṇē sāmidhēnyaḥ śrūyanta
iti ।</quote> kō'sya bhāṣyasyārthaḥ ? varṇitō'smābhiruddēśyapadā-
bhāvāt prakaraṇāviśēṣaḥ । <quote><q>“satyaṁ, paraprakaraṇē śrūyantē । tathāpi
tāsāmavāntaraprakaraṇamasti”</q></quote> iti । kimidamavāntaraprakaraṇam । ēkasya
hi adhikāravidhēḥ prakaraṇam । na hi aṅgavidhīnāmapi prakaraṇamasti ।
pradhānavidhyabhēdāt । pradhānavidhīnāṁ ca abhēdaṁ caturthē vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b696"/>
saṁskāravidhīnāṁ ca tēṣāmarthēna saṁbandha ityatrānuvādaḥ pradarśitaḥ ।
tasmādavāntaraprakaraṇaṁ grāhakaviniyōjakatayā nōpapadyatē ।
ataḥ sannidhānamātramavaśiṣvatē । ucyatē---sannidhāna ēvāyaṁ
prakaraṇaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ । kathamavagamyatē । yēna tatsannidhā-
vabhidhīyamānaṁ tasyēti jñāyatē iti vacanāt । nanu ca
viniyōjakē'pi prakaraṇē sannidhānaśrutiśabdaḥ upapadyatē ।
kēna cōk‍taṁ nōpapadyata iti । kintu tanna saṁbhavatī-
tyuktam । vākyabhēdaśravaṇācca, vyavadhānaṁ ca darśayati ।
﻿<pb n="b697"/>
parārthēna vyavadhānamānantaryaṁ vihantiṁ na punaḥ viniyōgam । anyathā
svāhākārasyāviniyōgaḥ syāt samidādibhirvyavadhānāt । atha
nivitpadānāmanyārthatvāt grāhakasyāpi vyavadhānamiti dvādaśāhīna-
syētyapi vyavadhānaṁ syāt । kiñca kāmyairavyavadhānaṁ nivitpadānāṁ
syāt । tataśca nividarthatā prāpnōti । satyaṁ yadyanuvacanavyavadhāna-
mabhiprētam । iha tu sannihitakartr̥vyavadhānamabhiprētaṁ tacca guṇaphala-
saṁbandhābhidhānē sati karmaṇō vyavadhānādupapannaṁ karturvyavadhānam ।
﻿<pb n="b698"/>
ēvaṁ sthitē pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ---guṇaphalasaṁbandhēpyanuvacana-
śrutau kartā sannihita ēvēti sāmidhēnyarthaṁ upavyānam
rāddhāntavādī tu nāvidhīyamānaṁ sannihitaṁ bhavati svasthānasthitamanu-
vadanīyamanūdyatē, na punaḥ sannidhāpyatē । anūdyamānavaśavartitvā-
danuvādānām । ataḥ sannidhānāviśēṣāt kr̥ts‍nē prakaraṇē nivēśa
iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="22">guṇānāṁ ca parārthatvādasaṁbandhaḥ samatvāt syāta1 ।। (3, 1. 22. a. 12) ।।</ab>
<p>vāraṇō yajñāvacara iti yajñasaṁbandhitvēna pātraṁ śrūyatē ānartha-
kyāttadaṅgōṣviti sthitō nyāyaḥ । tadidānīṁ pavamāna-
﻿<pb n="b699"/>
haviṣāṁ yadyādhānāṅgatā tataḥ pavamānahaviṣṣvēva pātravidhānamētat ।
yadi nāṅgatā tadā sarvayajñārthamiti । kiṁ tāvad‍yuktam ? pavamāna-
haviṣṣu vidhānam । ādhānāṅgaṁ hi pavamānahavīṁṣi prakaraṇē caitacchrūyatē
pradhānē cāsaṁbhavat dharmaḥ aṅgēṣu vidhēya ityuktam । nanu ca
pavamānahavīṁṣi agnyarthāni yadāhavanīyē juhōtīti vacanāt ।
anārabhyavādō'yaṁ sarvahōmānāṁ guṇatvēnāhavanīyaṁ vidadhāti na
prādhānyaṁ saṁbhavati । tasmādānarthakyāttadaṅgēṣviti pavamānahaviṣṣu
vidhānam । atrābhidhīyatē---naivādhānaprakaraṇē pavamānahavīṁṣi śrūyantē
nāpyagnyarthānyēva । kathaṁ ? yadāhavanīyē juhōtīti vacanāt ।
﻿<pb n="b700"/>
nanu ca guṇatayā vidadhātyanārabhyavādō'yamityuktam । na brūmō na guṇa-
tayā vidadhātīti । kintvatra prakr̥titaḥ prāptipradarśanārthaṁ ēvaṁ vacana-
mupanyastaṁ nōpadēśārtham । kathaṁ punaḥ prakr̥tiprīptau prādhānyaṁ bhavatīti
nanu ca guṇatayaiva prakr̥titō'pi prāp‍nōti । satyamēvam । ādhānō-
pakārakatvamagniniṣpattyā bhavati । agniniṣpattiścētprayōjanaṁ kimi-
tyādhānōpakārakatayā na punaḥ sākṣātprakr̥titaḥ saṁbandhāt । nanu ca
guṇatayā prāptirityuktam । satyamuktaṁ sā punarādhānāṅgatvē na saṁbhavati
aniṣpannatvādag‍nēḥ । niṣpādayatīti cēt tarhi sākṣānniṣpādakatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b701"/>
na hi sākṣātsaṁbandhē saṁbhavati parapr̥ṣṭhēna saṁbandhō yuktaḥ ।
tasmātsarvārthatā vāraṇādēḥ yuk‍tēti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">mithaścānarthasaṁbandhāt ।।3-1-23 a. 13 ।।</ab>
<p>tadēva punarudāharaṇāntarē cintyatē kēnacit viśēṣēṇāna-
rthakyāttadaṅgēṣviti । kaḥ punarasau viśēṣaḥ । ayamasau viśēṣaḥ ।
tatra yūpaśabdaḥ śrūyatē । iha punaḥ nājyabhāgābhidhānam । ataḥ
pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । yuk‍taṁ vājapēyē yūpaśabdābhidhānāt vyava-
dhānē'pi vājapēyētyanvayaḥ । iha punaḥ saṁbandhisaṁbandhyanvayē na
kiñcit pramāṇamasti । katha tarhi dvivacanam । dvayōrdvivacanam । nanu
caikatvāt prādhānyasyaikaivānuvākyā । kimidaṁ ēkatvātpradhānasyēti ।
﻿<pb n="b702"/>
nanu caikaikatra pradhānatrayamasti । na brūmaḥ ēkamēva pradhānamiti । ēkai-
kasyētikartavyatāsaṁbandha iti vadāmaḥ tataḥ kiṁ dvayōrasaṁbandhaḥ ।
nanu cājyabhāgayōrēkēna saṁbandhaḥ । satyamēva, śrutyā tu dvayōtpattēḥ
dvandvābhidhānamaviruddham । iha punaḥ pradhānē svataḥ ēkatvāt anu-
vākyāyā ēkaikasyāścōtpattēḥ pradhānānāṁ dvandvavirōdhaḥ । ucyatē---na
virōdhaḥ । kimiva vacanaṁ na kuryāt nāstivacanasyātibhāra iti ।
tatra dvitvamayathārthatvaṁ ca mantrasya bhaviṣyati, vyavadhānē pramāṇā-
bhāvādityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b703"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---tadidamayuktamabhihitamiti vadāmaḥ । kasmāt ? na
tatrāpi yūpaśabdābhidhānaṁ hētuḥ । kiṁ tarhi vidhēyasya yōgyatā ।
saṁbhavati ca yōgyatayāpyanvayō vājapēyasyētyuktam । ēvamatrāpi
saṁbhavati yathāyōgyavidhānē yathārthatvadvitvayōḥ pramāṇamasti ।
tasmādājyabhāgayōrēva mantravidhānamiti siddham ।</p>
<p>yatpunaridamuktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa1 nanu pradhānagāmitvēpi dvayōḥ
pradhānayōrdvē anuvākyē āgnēyasya ag‍nīṣōmīyasya cēti tatkathaṁ ?
dvitvōtpattērvirōdhāt । abhyupagamyāpi yuktyantaravirōdhapradarśa-
nārtham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b704"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">ānantaryamacōdanā ।।1 3. 1. 24-a. 14 ।।</ab>
<p>yadi yōgyatā niyamahētuḥ ihāpi tarhi staraṇē dīkṣitāvēdanē ca
parisamāptā yōgyatā ityatraivaidamarthyaparisamāptiḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---satyaṁ yadyatraiva yōgyatā kr̥ts‍nēpi prakaraṇē sā ।
tathaiva yadi paramēkavākyatāṁ niyantuṁ kṣamā । sā ca nāsti dvayō-
rākhyātayōrasaṁbandhāta kriyāyāṁ kriyārthāyāṁ tumun‌ṇvulauḥ tau ca
na staḥ ataḥ kr̥ts‍nē prakaraṇē nivēśaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">śēṣastu guṇasaṁyuktaḥ ।। 3-1-25-a. 15 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ āgnēyēpi
saṁbhavati aindrāgnēpi saṁbhavatīti । ayamabhi-
﻿<pb n="b705"/>
prāyaḥ---uddēśyē hi padārthamātrarayaiva upalakṣaṇatvam । saṁbandhimātra-
tayaiva siddhērna viśēṣō'pēkṣaṇīyaḥ । vidhēyē punaḥ viśēṣaniṣṭhatvātkāryasya
yuktaṁ viśēṣāpēkṣaṇam । tasmādāgnēyavidhau naindrāgnavidhiḥ upalakṣaṇē
punaḥ padārthānugamānna virōdhaḥ । ata ēva cāvyāsajyasaṁbandhi-
ḍitthaḍavitthadarśanam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">vyavasthā vā'pyarthasaṁyōgāt ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---yathā bhavānāha tathāpi tu yathā'bhidhēyaṁ
lakṣaṇāsaṁbhavē nāyathārthatvaṁ bhavati । pūrvaprasiddhaṁ hi lakṣaṇatvē(na)
hētuḥ । atō nāprasiddhalakṣaṇā bhavitumarhati yathāprasiddhāsaṁbhavē ca
﻿<pb n="b706"/>
aprasiddhanimittatāpi gr̥hyatē । tasmādāgnēyasyaiva caturdhākaraṇamiti
sthitam । ḍitthaḍabitthādīnāṁ tu pratyēkamēva siddhiḥ āgnēyastu
pratyuktaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b707"/>
<head>atha tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">arthābhidhānasaṁyōgānmantrēṣu śēṣabhāvaḥ syāt tasmādutpatti-
saṁbandhō'rthēna nityasaṁyōgāt1 ।। 3-2-1 a. 1 ।।</ab>
<p>yuktaṁ tāvat 2 kiṁ mukhya ēvābhidhēyē mantrāṇāṁ viniyōgaḥ
uta gauṇē'pīti । idantvayuk‍taṁ kaḥ punarmukhyaḥ kō vā gauṇa iti ।
kathamivāyuktam ? yaḥ paraśabdaḥ paratra vartatē sa gauṇa iti sthitam
tathā ca darśitam---3kathaṁ punaḥ paraśabdaḥ paratra vartatē ? svārthābhi-
dhānēnēti । tasmādayuktō'yaṁ praśnaḥ ।</p>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ, lakṣaṇāyāmapi paraśabdaḥ paratra vartatē
tadva‍yāvr̥ttyarthō'yaṁ praśnaḥ iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b708"/>
<p>tannōpapadyatē । yadēva gauṇatvē lakṣaṇaṁ vakṣyati---1anā-
dr̥tyaiva māṇavakapratyayaṁ jvalanaṁ agniśabdāt pratiyantō
dr̥śyantē na tvanādr̥tya jvalanapratyayaṁ māṇavakaṁ pratiyanti iti ।
lakṣaṇāyāmapyēvamēva । nahyanādr̥tya gaṅgāpratyayaṁ gaṅgāsamīpaṁ pratiyanti
tasmānna tannivr̥ttyarthamiti śakyatē vak‍tum ।</p>
<p>atha mataṁ lakṣaṇāyāmanvēti lakṣaṇāpadaṁ gauṇē punaḥ nānvēti
iti । tadayuktam । pratītau tāvat dvayamapyanvēti । kāryē punarnaikamapi ।
atō'nēnāpi viśēṣaṇēna na viśēṣaḥ । atha vākyārthanivr̥ttayē yatnaḥ,
﻿<pb n="b709"/>
tanna; naivārthāntarē vākyaṁ vartatē anvitābhidhāyīni padā-
nyēva hi vākyam । anvitāśca padārthāḥ vākyārthaḥ । na
cānanvitābhidhānamasti iti pradarśitam । ēvaṁ tarhi praśnārthō-
vyākhyēyaḥ । ēvaṁ ca sōpapada---suṣṭhuprasiddha bahuśaḥ prayōgāśca
pratyuktā bhāṣyē atastannirākaraṇārthō'pyayaṁ praśnaḥ nōpapadyata ēva ।
﻿<pb n="b710"/>
ucyatē । ayaṁ praśnasya arthaḥ vākyārthavagamāddhi nimittatayā
padārthavibhāgō'vagamyatē । sa cāyaṁ māṇavakē'gnau ca tulyaḥ
agnirmāṇavaka ityuk‍tē māṇavakaḥ piṅgalatā ca nimittam । agnirjva-
latītyuk‍tē jvalanō jvalanakriyā ca । tasmānna viśēṣaṁ paśyāmaḥ
asya śābdō nimittabhāvō'sya gauṇō nimittabhāva iti । nanu
cāgnipratyayapurassarā māṇavakē pratītiḥ paiṅgalyasya; naivaṁ śakyatē
﻿<pb n="b711"/>
vak‍tum । uktamidaṁ vākyānnimittabhāvāvagatiriti । agnirmāṇa-
vaka iti piṅgalataiva kēvalaṁ nimittatayā'vagamyatē yathā piṅgalō
māṇavaka iti । tasmād‌durnirūpamidaṁ gauṇō'yaṁ mukhyō'yamiti manvā-
nasya praśnaḥ । na cōpapadādibhiḥ saṁbhavatīti pradarśidaṁ bhāṣyē । agni-
rivāyaṁ māṇavaka ityatra yuktamagnisādr̥śyam ivādīnāṁ sādr̥śyē prayōga-
﻿<pb n="b712"/>
darśanāt । ag‍nirmāṇavaka iti tu ivārthaśūnyō'rthaḥ vākyārthaḥ
yathā piṅgalō māṇavaka iti ca tulyō nimittabhāvaḥ । atō niṣprayō-
janamēvēdamadhikaraṇaṁ manyāmahē । kathaṁ tarhi gaṅgāyāṁ ghōṣaḥ kūpē garga-
kulamiti । yuktaṁ prativasatītyasya sāmarthyaṁ na bhavatīti samīpānva-
yitā । ag‍nirmāṇavaka iti tu piṅgalaguṇāvagamō na kathañcinnōpa-
padyatē । tasmāt bhavatu lakṣaṇā । gauṇatvē punaḥ na kiñcit
pramāṇamasti । kathaṁ cāg‍nipratyayō lōkē paiṅgalyādapyupapadyatē
﻿<pb n="b713"/>
pūrvādivāparapratyayaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---ivārthanibandhana ēvāyaṁ pratyayaḥ
kutaḥ ? tathā'vagatēḥ । kathaṁ punarivaśabdamantarēṇēvārthaḥ pratīyatē । iva-
śabdō'pi tāvadivārthaḥ kimiti kalpyatē । prayōgadarśanāditi cēt
atrāpi tulyam । nanu ca paiṅgalyē'vagatē jvalanasādr̥śyamavagamyatē apara-
śabdavadityuktam । naitadupapadyatē । māṇavakasadr̥śō'g‍nirityapi pratyayaḥ
﻿<pb n="b714"/>
syāt । iha punarviparītamiti । atipaiṅgalyāt jvala-
nasyōpamānamiti cēt nāsyāṁ kalpanāyāṁ pramāṇamasti । yathāvagamaṁ
nimittakalpanā nyāyyā tanmūlatvāt nimittāvagatēḥ । atō yadyapi
viparītaḥ saṁbhavati tathāpi prasiddhapratipakṣatvāt nātmānaṁ labhatē ।
apratipakṣō hi saṁbhavaḥ saṁbhavaḥ । tasmādupapannaṁ prayōgapratyayābhyāṁ
gauṇamukhyābhidhānam । kiṁ mukhya ēvābhidhēyē mantrāṇāṁ viniyōgaḥ,
uta gauṇē'pīti । tasmāta yuktō vicāraḥ ।</p>
<p>kiṁ tāvatprāptaṁ ? aviśēṣādubhayābhidhānaṁ; ag‍nirjvalatītyapi
prayōgō dr̥ṣṭaḥ ag‍nirmāṇavaka iti ca । tasmānna vinigamanāyāṁ
﻿<pb n="b715"/>
hēturasti । atrābhidhīyatē---ayamasti mukhyābhidhānaśūnyaṁ nāsti
gauṇābhidhānamiti pradarśitam । tasmānmukhya ēva śabdasya
vyāpāraḥ । abhidhānēna mantrā upakurvanti mukhyē cābhidhānaṁ
na gauṇē । kutastarhi gauṇapratyayaḥ ? sādr̥śyāditi । satya-
muktam, tat‍tu upāyātvēna na punarnimittanirākaraṇatayāpi ।
kēna cōk‍taṁ nimittatā nirākriyata iti । mukhyē saṁbhavati
na gauṇē viniyōgaḥ kṣama iti ētāvaducyatē । yatra puna-
rmukhyē na saṁbhavati tatra gauṇē'bhyupāyatvamiṣyata ēva । na tarhi
pūṣādyanumantraṇādīnāṁ utkarṣaḥ । samākhyayā viniyuktānāṁ
﻿<pb n="b716"/>
mukhya ēva saṁbhavatītyutkarṣaḥ । tasmāt mukhyē yatra saṁpratyayō na tatra
gauṇē'pi mantraniyamē pramāṇamasti । kimarthaṁ mukhyaṁ pratyāyayatītyēva-
mādinā pradarśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1vacanāttvayathārthamaindrī syāt ।।3-2-3 a. 2 ।।</ab>
<p>aindna‍yā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhatē ityatra saṁśayaḥ kimaindrēṇa mantrēṇa
gārhapatyasyābhidhānaṁ utēndrasyēti । kathaṁ punaḥ gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata
iti spaṣṭāyāṁ śrutau saṁśayaḥ ? mukhyē'rthē mantrō viniyujyata iti
sthitamādhastyē'dhikaraṇē । nanu ca mukhyāsaṁbhavē gauṇēpi ca vini-
yujyata ēva । ētadēva na vijānīmaḥ saṁbhavō vidyatē nēti । [nanu]
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti spaṣṭaiva śrutiḥ । viniyōjyasāmarthyānu-
sārī viniyōga iti anīpsitārthā dvitīyā bhavatīti brūmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b717"/>
tathā ca smaryatē <q>‘tathā yuk‍taṁ cānīpsitaṁ’</q> iti । ayamēva cāsya viṣayaḥ
viniyōjyavaśāt kārakaparyavasāyyēva । yadvā gārhapatyamupētyābhi-
dhatta iti dvitīyōpapadyata ēva । tasmādindrābhidhānam । yuk‍taṁ caitadēvaṁ
anyathā alaukikī abhidhānaśaktiḥ kalpanīyā । nanu gauṇamabhidhānaṁ
bhaviṣyati । nāsti gauṇamabhidhānam । siddhē hi prayōgē gōṇamabhidhānaṁ,
na punargauṇāt prayōgasiddhiḥ । na cātra gārhapatyē indraśabdaprayōgō-
'nyataḥ siddhiḥ kartavyatōpadēśāt । atō yathābhidhānaṁ viniyōgaḥ
atrābhidhīyatē । gārhapatyābhidhānaṁ mantrēṇa kartavyam । kutaḥ ?
yathōpadēśaṁ hi kāryaṁ na yathākāryamupadēśaḥ । atidēśō hi saḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b718"/>
nanu ca yathākāryamupadēśō'pīti saptamādyē uktam । niyōgārthaḥ
tatra kāryaśabdēnōktaḥ na punarāp‍tyādayaḥ । nanu ca viniyōgē ēva
sandihyata ityuktam । kimiti na niścita iti cēt । anīpsitē-
'pi dvitīyādarśanāt । kimidamanīpsitamiti ? tathā yuk‍taṁ cānī-
psitamiti । sutarāṁ tarhi dhātvarthaṁ prati prādhānyam । anyathā hi
tathāyōgō na syāt । tarabarthaḥ idānīṁ kimarthaḥ ? anīpsitamapi
pradhānamiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b719"/>
<p>nanu cōk‍taṁ nādr̥ṣṭā śabdaśaktiḥ kalpayituṁ śakyata iti ?
kimatrādr̥ṣṭaṁ vacanād dr̥śyata ēva । na vacanāt padārthānāṁ
śaktiḥ śakyā avagantum । kathaṁ tarhi yōgādēḥ niyōgārthasiddhau
śaktiḥ ? kāryāvagamyatvāt । iha tu viparītam । yadyatrāpi
pratipattavyamiti vacanaṁ syāt bhavēt kāryadarśanam । idantvanya-
paramēva vacanaṁ ēndra‏‍yā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti । tadidamuk‍taṁ-saṁbandha-
syāśāstrahētutvāt1 iti । gauṇaṁ tarhyabhidhānaṁ bhaviṣyati ।
nanu prayōgasiddhē gauṇamabhidhānamityuktam । atrāpi kārya-
﻿<pb n="b720"/>
tayā siddha ityaviśēṣaḥ । guṇaśravaṇaṁ pradarśanārthaṁ sūtra iti matvā
yōgāccētyuktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">tathōhvānamapīti cēt1 ।। 3-2-5 a. 3 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi <q>‘avaghnannāhvayati’</q> ityāhvānēna avaghātaṁ kuryādityarthaḥ
guṇādvā'bhidhānaṁ bhaviṣyati yōgādvā āhnayatītyanuvādaḥ । yō hyē-
hīti brūtē sa āhvayatyēva । tririti kathaṁ ? śākhāntarē pāṭhāt
﻿<pb n="b721"/>
trirityapyayamanuvāda ēva । atrābhidhīyatē---trirityētāvadvidhīyatē ।
anyat sarvamanūdyatē । nanu ca trirityapi prāptaṁ, na, aniyamāt
kvacit dviḥ paṭhyatē । tasmādavaghnanniti lakṣaṇaiṣā । nāyaṁ dōṣaḥ, anyataḥ
prāptēḥ । nanu ca pravr̥ttāvaghātasya naiṣa mantraḥ prāpnōti । idamapyanyataḥ
pnāptatvādēvācōdyam । tasmānna gauṇē viniyōgē pramāṇamasti ।
﻿<pb n="b722"/>
yadi punarayaṁ mantrō'vaghātē mukhyārthaḥ syāt nāvaghātē lakṣaṇā kalpitā
bhavēt । śakyatē ca haviṣkr̥cchabdēnāvaghātō vak‍tuṁ patnīvat । satyam
śakyatē, āhvānantu ananvitārthaṁ prāp‍nōti । tribhiriti
ca aniyataṁ syāt । tasmādvaraṁ lakṣaṇaiva । tayā ca liṅgamai-
kāntikam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">1 tathōtthānavisarjanē ।। 3-2-10, a. 4 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cōdāharaṇamēvēdaṁ, kimatrātidiśyatē । na hi anyatvā-
dr̥tē sādr̥śyamupapadyata ēva । idamastyanyatvaṁ pūrvasminnadhikaraṇē
﻿<pb n="b723"/>
trirityēvadvidhīyatē । anyatsarvamanūdyatē । iha punaḥ kālasaṁyōgō
vidhātavyaḥ aprāptē sayōgavidhānē lakṣaṇā na nyāyyēti pūrvapakṣavādī
adhikaraṇavaiṣamyaṁ manyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu praiṣārthānanvayatulyatvāt
tathētyuktavān ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">1sūktavākē ca kālavidhiḥ parārthatvāt ।। 3-2-11 a. 5 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b724"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē, nēyaṁ kālakṣaṇā । kiṁ tarhi ? mantrōpadē-
śō'yam । nanu cānyārthō mantra ityuktam na haratērabhidhātēti ।
mābhūt haratērvācakaḥ haratidēvatāvācakō bhaviṣyati । nanu ca
nirvr̥ttayāgadēvatāvacanō'yam । na ca haratiryajatiḥ । ucyatē-nirvr̥tta-
dēvatāvacanatvē'pi tatsaṁskārō yāgō bhaviṣyati । paśupurōḍāśavat ।
nanu cāyaṁ haratirna yajatirityuktam । haratiryajatiḥ mantrasaṁbandhāt ।
﻿<pb n="b725"/>
nanu caivaṁ sati saiva lakṣaṇā prāp‍nōti । na lakṣaṇā, yāgē
sati haratyarthasya prāptatvāt । ālabhētētivat । anyathā hi vr̥tta-
midamā nirdēśyaṁ syāt । āśāsta iti ca bhūtanirdēśaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b726"/>
tasmātsuṣṭūcyatē haratiryajatiriti । yaduk‍taṁ pratipattau sabhavantyāṁ
nārthakarma nyāyyamiti । sviṣṭakr̥dvadavirōdhō bhaviṣyatītyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">1kr̥tsnōpadēśādubhayatra sarvavacanam ।। 3-2-16 a. 6 ।।</ab>
<p>haratiryajatiḥ sūktavākamantrasthēti sthitam । idamidānīṁ
cintyatē । kiṁ sakalasya sūktavākasya paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāyāṁ ca
prayōga uta dēvatāpadavibhāgēnēti ।</p>
<p>nanu cintaivēyaṁ nōpapadyatē । sthitamarthaikatvādēka-
vākyatvam । śliṣṭapaṭhitānāṁ pradhānadēvatāpadānāṁ na cātrai-
kārthatvaṁ saṁbhavati । nāpi vibhajyamānasākāṅkṣatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b727"/>
tasmādbhinnānyētāni । bhinnānāṁ tvēkavacananirdēśē sati kathaṁ
kr̥ts‍naprayōga āśaṅkyatē । yathā āg‍nēyyētyuk‍tē na kr̥ts‍nā āgnēyyaḥ
prayōktavyā ityāśaṅkā bhavati । mukhyē ca saṁbhavati na gauṇē
viniyōga ityapi sthitam । ucyatē । yathā bhavānāha । kintu
pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē sūk‍tavākō vartata iti vākyasamūhē ēka-
vacanamidaṁ, ēvamatrāpi sūktavākēnēti samūhagatamēvēdamēkavacanaṁ,
ataḥ samudāya ēvātra karaṇam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b728"/>
<p>nanu samūhasyaikārthatā na saṁbhavati । vacanāt kalpyatē
yathā uttamaprayājē । imāmāśaṅkāṁ nivartayituṁ idamadhikaraṇam । kr̥taḥ
pūrvapakṣaḥ । idānīṁ rāddhāntō'bhidhīyatē---nātra samūhaviniyōgē
pramāṇamasti sūktavākō vartata iti anyathāpyēkavacanōpapattēḥ । ēkā-
bhidhānāddhi pāṭhakānāṁ sūktavākō vartata iti yujyatē'bhidhānam । iha
punaḥ sūktavākēna prastaraṁ praharatīti na liṅgabādhēnaikavākyatvaṁ śakyatē
kalpayitum, yathāliṅgaṁ viniyōgōpapattēḥ । tasmādviśēṣāgrahaṇāt yēna
﻿<pb n="b729"/>
kēnacit sūktavākēna prahr̥tē prahr̥taṁ bhavati sūktavākēna prastaraṁ
praharatīti । samudāyābhiprāyastu hēyatayōpanyastaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">1liṅgakramasamākhyānāt kāmyayuktaṁ samāmnānam ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>ādhastyē'dhikaraṇē uk‍taṁ prakaraṇāt pratyēkaṁ śēṣatvē prāptē liṅgā-
dvibhāga iti । ihēdānīṁ prakaraṇādyat balīyaḥ tatkramasamākhyābhyāṁ
nitarāṁ balīya iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । liṅgācchēṣatvē atantrē
kramasamākhyē ।</p>
<p>nanu naiva liṅgaṁ kēvalaṁ viniyōjakaṁ rāddhāntē vakṣyati viniyō-
jakatvē tu balābalam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b730"/>
<p>kimarthaṁ vā prāk śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇāt balābalacintā ।
atrābhidhīyatē । naivēyaṁ balābalacintā । sāpēkṣaṁ liṅgaṁ
viniyōjakamityatra pratipādyatē । kathaṁ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ?
liṅgamapi śrutyādivat pramāṇāntaranirapēkṣamiti balābalasūtrē
anukramaṇāt pūrvapakṣō'yam । rāddhāntastu---sāmānyasaṁbandhē sati
śēṣiviśēṣē liṅgaṁ viniyōjakamiti । yathā liṅgaṁ na kēvalaṁ
viniyōjakaṁ tathā śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇē nipuṇataramupapāda-
yiṣyāmaḥ । ataḥ kramasahitaṁ ca liṅgaṁ viniyōjakam ।
﻿<pb n="b731"/>
ubhayaliṅgapramāṇasāhityē ca prayōjanamuk‍taṁ bhāṣyē ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1adhikārē ca mantravidhiratadōkhyātēṣu śiṣṭatvāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b732"/>
<p>āgnēyyā''gnīdhramupatiṣṭhata ityēvamādiṣu liṅganirdēśēṣu kiṁ
yāvalliṅgā grahītavyāḥ uta prakr̥tānāṁ grahaṇamātramiti । pūrvapakṣavādī
tu vidhēyasya prakr̥tābhidhānasāmarthyaṁ na saṁbhavati iti manvānō
yāvalliṅgaṁ grahaṇamityāha । uddēśyapadaṁ hi prakr̥tāpēkṣaṁ bhavati na
punarvidhēyārthasamarpakamapi । uddēśyatvaṁ hi nāma prayōjanavadarthatā । na ca
sāmānyaṁ prayōjanavadbhavati upāttaviṣayatvāt prayōjanavattāyāḥ । nanu
ca sāmānyamēvōpādīyatē । nāparimitasyōpādānaṁ saṁbhavati । tasmā-
llakṣaṇatayaiva tatra sāmānyam । yathōk‍taṁ grahādhikaraṇē vidhēyaṁ punaḥ sapa
rimāṇaṁ śabdādēvāvagantavyam । anyatō'navagamāditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b733"/>
prakr̥tamaprakr̥taṁ vā yāvalliṅgaṁ vidhēyam । kiṁ prakr̥tābhirliṅgavatī-
bhirupasthātavyaṁ uta dāśatayībhya ēvaṁliṅgā āgamayitavyā
iti dāśatayīgrahaṇaṁ na prakr̥tapratipakṣatayā । ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati ।
kiṁ yāvalliṅgā grahītavyā uta prakr̥tā ēvaivaṁliṅgā āgamayitavyā
iti ।</p>
<p><q>‘kimidaṁ 1upadiṣṭōpadēśō na nyāyyaḥ’</q> ? idamidam । upadiṣṭa-
taiva hi tasya viśēṣaḥ । na cāsau vidhēyāṅgamityuktam । prakr̥tvaṁ
punarabhidhānāt‍tulyam । atrāha-2virōdhē sati liṅgēna prakaraṇaṁ bādhyatē
﻿<pb n="b734"/>
na caitayōrvirōdha" iti । kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ prakr̥tē'pi
gr̥hyamāṇē'bhihita ēvārthō gr̥hītō bhavati । yathaikasyāmapi gavyupā-
dīyamānē caritārthaiva gāmālabhētēti śratiḥ । naitadēvamiti । nātra
liṅgavattā śabdārtha iti manyatē । ucyatē, talliṅgavattā'nēnēti
hēyatayā'sya pakṣasyōpanyāsaḥ । dāśatayyāṁ punaḥ mantravyaktāviti
prakr̥ta ēva saṁpannē liṅgārthē niṣpramāṇakaḥ prakr̥tabādha iti
manyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b735"/>
<p><quote>1liṅgajanitastu pratyayaḥ kaścinmithyēti</quote> । liṅgārthasaṁpattau satyāṁ kō'yaṁ
mithyābhāvaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---nāyaṁ sāmānyōpasaṁhāraḥ śabdārtha
iti । <q>‘svargakāmō yajēta’</q> iti na sampatyā anyaprayōgārhōpi
śāstrārthaḥ paryavasita iti śakyatē vak‍tum । nanu ca vyaktirapadārtha
iti sāmānyōpasaṁhr̥tirēvōpanyastā1 । ētadēva na vijānīma
iti pratyayārthapradhānatvāt taddhitāntānāṁ na tadvattā'ṅgamiti
﻿<pb n="b736"/>
manyatē । tasmānna sāmānyōpasaṁhārārthamidaṁ śāstram । nanvētataduk‍taṁ
kāryāntarē prakr̥tasyōpadēśō nāsāvarthāntara upadēkṣyata iti
upadiṣṭōpadēśaparihārāyāyamupanyāsaḥ । kimiti ? liṅgavanmātra-
grahaṇāditi darśitam । nātrōpadiṣṭatā hētuḥ । nanu caivaṁ
sati prakr̥tabādhaḥ । bhavatvabhidhānāt prakr̥tabādhō na dōṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b737"/>
api ca na liṅgaṁ prakaraṇaṁ vā'nugrahītavyamiti nānugrahārthā
śāstrārthōpasaṁhr̥tiriti yaduk‍taṁ tadidam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">1tadākhyō vā prakaraṇōpapattibhyām ।। 3-1-22 a. 8 ।।</ab>
<p>atrōcyatē---rāddhāntī tu prakr̥tē'pi vidhēyapratyayō naiva na ghaṭata
iti manvānaḥ prakr̥tasyaiva grahaṇamityuktavān । kathaṁ ? uddēśyatvaṁ hi
nāma prayōjanavatō bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b738"/>
<p>prakr̥tatvaṁ punaḥ vidhēyēpi prakr̥tapratyayaṁ naiva bādhatē । na hi
sannihitē viśēṣē sāmānyaśabdaḥ tamativartatē । nīlōtpalamitivat
gāmānayētivadvā । tasmāt prakr̥tapratyarthī na sāmānyaśabdō bhavitu-
marhati । prakr̥tā ēvaivaṁ liṅgavyaktayaḥ parigr̥hyanta iti siddham । sarvēṣāṁ
cōpadiṣṭatvāditi । yaduktaṁ tadidam । yadyupadēśamātraṁ sarvatrāsti
prakr̥tagrahaṇē'pyupadēśō na viśēṣaṇamityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b739"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1liṅgasamākhyābhyāṁ bhakṣārthatānuvākasya ।। 3-1-25 a. 9 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē---yathā prakr̥tatayā liṅgamupasaṁhr̥taṁ kimēvaṁ
samākhyāpi svanimitta ēvōpasaṁharati uta yathāliṅgaṁ viniyōga
iti । kiṁ tāvad‌yuktam ? samākhyāpi prakr̥tavanniyamayatyēva
viśēṣē liṅgam । nanu liṅgāntaravirōdhaḥ prāpnōti । na, viśēṣaṇa-
tayāpi liṅgāntarasyāvirōdhāt । yataḥ svārthē parārthē vā'bhidhāna-
maviśiṣṭam । nanu ca pārārthyē lakṣaṇā prāpnōti । tathāpya-
bhidhānamaviśiṣṭaṁ idaṁparatāviśēṣō'yaṁ nābhidhānaviśēṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b740"/>
tasmānniyantumarhati samākhyā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1tasya rūpōpadēśābhyāmapakarṣō'rthasya cōditvāt ।। 3-2-16 ।।</ab>
<p>satyamavirōdhi liṅgāntaram---kintu anidaṁparatāyāḥ pramāṇaṁ
na vidyatē । bhakṣaṇavalliṅgāntaraviṣayasyāpi smaraṇārha-
tvāt । prayōgō hi smaraṇīyaḥ । grahaṇādyapi ca prayōgaṁ ēva ।
tasmādyathāliṅgaṁ vyavasthā । nanu ca samākhyāśūnyaṁ liṅgaṁ
viniyōjakatāmēva na pratipadyatē । naiva samākhyā-
śūnyaṁ bhakṣanimittāpi samākhyā kratusaṁbandhitāmāpādayatyēva ।
﻿<pb n="b741"/>
laukikī lakṣaṇētyasyōktaḥ parihāraḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">1guṇābhidhānānmandrādirēkamantraḥ syāt tayōrēkārthasaṁyōgāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvādhikaraṇāpavādō'yam । aprayōgābhidhānō mantraḥ prayō-
gābhidhānēna saha ēkavākyataṁ nīyatē samākhyayā । liṅgaṁ hi
dr̥ṣṭārthatayā samākhyāyōpasaṁhr̥tam । yatra punaḥ dr̥ṣṭārthatā nāsti
tatrādr̥ṣṭakalpanāyāṁ pramāṇaṁ nāsti iti samākhyaiva viniyōktrī ।
sā ca svanimittaivēti siddhaṁ lakṣaṇēnaikavākyatvamityēkamantratvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b742"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">1liṅgaviśēṣanirdēśāt samānavidhānēṣvanaindrāṇāmamantratvam ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>iha pānōpalakṣaṇaprakaraṇē samānavidhānē sthitē <q>‘anuṣṭu-
p‌chandasa’</q> iti namanadarśanāt <q>‘‘aindraḥ sōmō
﻿<pb n="b743"/>
gr̥hyatē mīyatē ca”</q> iti prakr̥tivikāraśaṅkāyāṁ kr̥tvācintā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1punarabhyannītēṣu sarvēṣāmupalakṣaṇaṁ dviśēṣatvāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>atra āśrāvaṇādapanayaḥ prasthitadēvatāyā iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
agrahaṇānnēti siddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><quote>2pāt‍nīvatē tu pūrvavat । 3tvaṣṭāraṁ tūpalakṣayēt । triṁśacca ।।</quote></p>
<p>āgrayaṇāt punaranāgrayaṇasyāpi taduddēśēna grahaṇamityayanaya
ēva । tvaṣṭari sahavacanāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nācōditatvāditi rāddhāntaḥ
﻿<pb n="b744"/>
trayastriṁśati tvag‍nēḥ mādayitr̥tvadarśanāt punarāśaṅkā । mādayitr̥taiva
tatprādhānyāt dēvatābhāvamāpādayati iti rāddhāntaḥ । ēvamanuva-
ṣaṭkāradēvatāpi taduddēśēnāgrahaṇānnōpalakṣyā ।</p>
<p>sthitāduttaram---ēkayāgatvāttu samānavidhānam । tasmādaindra-
mēva samantrakam itaradanāmnānādamantrakamēva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b745"/>
<p>aindrāgnē punaḥ pānamēvōpalakṣyatē na dēvatēti । āg‍nēyaṁ
caturdhā karōtīti sthitē pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ dēvataivōpalakṣaṇaṁ pānābhāvāditi
rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">1chandaśca dēvatāvat ।। 3-2-42 a. 18 ।।</ab>
<p>dēvatayā tulyaṁ cchanda iti manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ
ēkachandasō na vidyata iti rāddhāntaḥ । anuṣ‍ṭup‌chandasa iti chandō-
ntaravidhānāt namatītyasya parihāraḥ । aindraḥ sōmō mīyatē gr̥hyatē
ca iti samānavidhānē sthitē yathāliṅgaṁ mantra iti sthitam ।
tasmādidamapyakāraṇaṁ prakr̥tivikārabhāvasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b746"/>
<p>idānīmindrapītasya iti sthitē savanasāmānādhikaraṇyāt
sarvē mantravanta iti rāddhānta ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b747"/>
<head>atha tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1śrutērjātādhikāraḥ syāt ।। 3-3-1 a. 1 ।।</ab>
<p>1<quote>śrutērjātādhikāraḥ syāt</quote> । <q>‘uccairr̥cā kriyatē’</q> iti kimayaṁ vēdadharmaḥ
uta r̥gdharma iti saṁśayaḥ । kō'yaṁ vēdō nāma ? nanu cargapi vēda
ēvēti । ucyatē---vidhāyakaṁ vēdaśabdēnōcyatē । ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati
---yadr̥gvēdaśabdavācyaṁ vidhāyakaṁ tadvidhēyadharmaḥ uta yatra pādavyavasthā
tasmin mantra iti ।</p>
﻿<page n="b748"/>
<p>kiṁ tāvad‍yuktam---uccaiḥ r̥cā kriyata iti vacanādr̥gdharmō'ya-
miti । nanu vēdōpakramamētadvākyam । kō dōṣaḥ ? r̥kṣvapyayaṁ vēda-
śabdō vartata ēva । ēvaṁ ca na vikalpō bhaviṣyati vēdāntarapaṭhi-
tasya r̥gjātasya ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1vēdō vā prāyadarśanāt ।। 3-3-2 ।।</ab>
<p>atrōcyatē---vēdadharmō'yam । kutaḥ ? vēdaśabdōpakrama-
tvādvākyasya । nanu ca upakramōpasaṁhāravaśāt r̥kṣu vartata
ityuktam । satyamuktam । tattu nōpapadyatē । kathaṁ nōpa-
padyatē ? ēvaṁ nōpapadyatē । upakramē yaḥ padārthaḥ parijñātō
﻿<pb n="b749"/>
bhavati tadviśēṣapratipattirēva kēvalamupasaṁhārādapēkṣyatē । na
punastadvirōdhyarthāntaram । atō'virōdhidharmavidhānamēva kēvalaṁ
vēdēna saṁbadhyatē । r̥k‌cchabdastadānuguṇyādanuvādaḥ । kathaṁ
punarnargvēdaśabdēnōcyatē ? kēna cōk‍taṁ nōcyata iti ?
kintu vidhēyatayā na vidhāyakavat । dr̥ṣṭaścāyaṁ r̥k-
śabdō vēdē---r̥gbhiḥ prātardivi dēva rhayatē’ iti । kuta
ētat ? yajurvēdē tiṣṭhati madhyē ahna iti sahayōgāt ।
﻿<pb n="b750"/>
dharmōpadēśaśca sāmnāṁ pr̥thaktvēnaivamēvēdamupapadyatē । anyathā hi
r̥gvidhānātsiddhēḥ pr̥thagvacanamanarthakam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1trayīvidyākhyā ca tadvidi-iti ।।</ab>
<p>trayīvidyaśabdaśca vēdatrayavidi vartatē । tataḥ kiṁ ? idaṁ tatō
bhavati । vēdē r̥gādiśabdānāṁ prayōgō dr̥ṣṭa iti । yatpunarvēdāntarōktasya
svarāntarāpattiriti । vidhānānna dōṣaḥ । prakaraṇabādhaśca vākyādiṣyata
ēva । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ vēdasaṁyōgēpi prakaraṇaṁ nānugr̥hyatē, r̥g‌dharma-
vidhānavat । ucyatē-r̥cāmaṅgatvāttaddharmaḥ prakaraṇēna gr̥hyata iti yuk‍taṁ;
﻿<pb n="b751"/>
vēdadharmatvē punaḥ vidhānamupalakṣaṇam । na ca tadaṅgamiti yāva-
dvidhānaṁ dharmavidhiḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1guṇamukhyavyatikramē tadarthatvānmukhyēna vēdasaṁyōgaḥ ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p><q>“ya ēvaṁ vidvānagnimādhattē”</q> iti yājurvaidikō vidhiḥ । <q>“ya 
ēvaṁ vidvān vāravantīyaṁ gāyati”</q> iti ādhānaprakaraṇē sāmavaidika
iti kr̥tvā cintyatē । yājurvaidikē bhavatūpāṁśutvaṁ, sāmavaidikē
cōccaiṣṭvaṁ, satyamēvaṁ yadyaṅgapradhānavidhī bhidyētē yathātvabhēdaḥ tathā
phalavatsannidhau aphalaṁ tadaṅgamityatra vakṣyati । abhēdē cōbhayavēda-
vidhānāt bhavati saṁśayaḥ । ubhayavēdavidhānāt vikalpō
bhavatu । na vikalpaḥ saṁbhavati । ēvaṁ sati aṅgavidhiranuvāda
﻿<pb n="b752"/>
ityaṅgavidhēḥ pradhānavidhitantratvaṁ darśayati । tathāpi kaḥ saṁśayaḥ ? aya-
masti saṁśayaḥ kimaṅgavidhirākṣiptasvavidhēya ēva pradhānavidhitantrō
bhavati, uta pradhānēnaikībhūtō vidhēyaṁ vidhatta iti । pūrvapakṣavādī
manyatē । svārthaṁ vidhāya prayōjanavaśāt pradhānēnaikībhavati vāravantīya
gāyatītyasya yaḥ svārthaḥ । ataḥ sāmavaidikasvarayuktasyaivāṅgabhāvaḥ ।
atrābhidhīyatē---vihitasvārtha ēva pradhānēnaikībhavati । na punaraṅga-
tāmapi vidhāya । pradhānavidhiraṅgatāṁ vidhatta iti saptamādyē vakṣyāmaḥ
﻿<pb n="b753"/>
aṅgatayā ca vāravantīyasya prayōgaḥ na vāravantīyaṁ gāyatītyasya
vidhērviṣayatayā । atō na svārthavidhiḥ pradhānavidhiṁ bādhitumarhati
svārthasya prayōgārthatvāt । tadidamuktam---<q>“1guṇasyānuṣṭhānēna mukhyaḥ
saguṇaḥ kathaṁ syāditi guṇē pravartatē । guṇapravr̥ttyā cēnmukhyayya
guṇahānirbhavati guṇapravr̥ttau phalamēva nāvāptaṁ bhavati । atha pradhānaṁ
saguṇaṁ kariṣyāmīti guṇē pravartamānō guṇasya guṇaṁ vinipātayati nāsya
svārthō hīyatē nāsau guṇaṁ saguṇaṁ kartuṁ pravartata”</q> iti na guṇavidhau
svārthē pravr̥ttirītyuk‍taṁ bhavati । prayōgāṅgatvācca guṇavidhēḥ pradhāna-
guṇēna bhavitavyamityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">2bhūyastvēnōmayaśruti ।। 3-3-10 a. 3 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitaṁ tāvat pradhānavidhinibandhanō guṇaḥ guṇavidhi-
﻿<pb n="b754"/>
nibandhanaṁ guṇaṁ bādhata iti । idamidānīṁ cintyatē---yatrōbhayatra
pradhānaśrutiḥ tatra kva pradhānacōdanēti । yatra pradhānacōdanā
tannibandhanēna guṇēna bhavitavyam । tatsidhyarthēṣācintā tatrā-
gr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatvādubhayatrētyuktvā bhūyastvēnaikatra nirūpitaṁ
vālavyajanādinā bahupu rājapratimēṣūpaviṣṭēṣu rājā'vagamyata iti
dr̥ṣṭāntābhidhānam । tadidamubhayamayuktam । kva bhūyastvēna pradhānasya
prayōgābhidhānaṁ dr̥ṣṭam । na ca bālavyajanaṁ ś‍vētacchatraṁ vā bhūyastvēnā-
vagamayati । kiṁ tarhi ? asādhāraṇatayā । tasmādasaṁbaddhamēvēdaṁ
bhāṣyaṁ manyāmahē ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---nēdamasaṁbaddham । bhūyastvēna hi prayōgā-
vagamassūcyatē sakalaprayōgō'vagamyata ityarthaḥ । alpāṅgā-
﻿<pb n="b755"/>
bhidhānē punaḥ na sakalaprayōgāvagatirbhavati । sakalē ca prayōgē'vagamya-
mānē prayōgābhidhānamatirbhavati । prayēyāddhi pramāṇānumānamiti
sthitam । yadapi ca vālavyajanamupanyastaṁ tadgamakasāmānyatayā
bhūyastvēnēti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">asaṁyuk‍taṁ prakaraṇāt iti kartavyatārthatvāt ।। a. 4 ।।</ab>
<p>1 kimētāvantyēva pramāṇāni ? kē'yaṁ praśnaḥ ? yadi tāvata
sūtrārtha ēva na śakyatē vyākhyātuṁ praś‍nēna vinētyabhiprāyaḥ । tada-
yuktam । praś‍nēna kimatra; yadasaṁyuk‍taṁ tatprakaraṇēna viniyujyata iti
﻿<pb n="b756"/>
nanu kēnāsaṁyuktamiti na vidmaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi ētadēva
praṣṭavyam । kēnāsaṁyuktamiti । k‍vēdamupayujyatē kimētāvantyēva
pramāṇānīti ? athāyamabhiprāyaḥ । kimiti śrutyā liṅgēna
vākyēna vā yadasaṁyuktēṁ tatprakaraṇēna viniyujyata iti । kimētā-
cantyēva pramāṇātīti, tathāpyuttaraṁ tāvadasaṁbaddhaṁ anyadapyastīti ।
yadyanyadapyasti kimiti tarhi śrutyā liṅgēna vākyēna vā'saṁyukta-
mityucyatē । athājñānamēva naiva śrutiliṅgavākyēbhyaḥ pramāṇamanya-
dvijñāyata iti tathāpi svarūpaṁ vaktavyam । nāsaṁyuktaṁ prakaraṇāditi
yujyatē kartavyasya itikartavyatākāṅkṣasyēti vakṣyamāṇavadvaktavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b757"/>
ataḥ praś‍nō'rthē'naupayika iva dr̥śyatē । atrābhidhīyatē---ayamabhi-
prāyō bhāṣyakārasya । lakṣaṇādāvuk‍taṁ <q>“1śēṣalakṣaṇamucyatē ।
śrutyādīni viniyōgē kāraṇāni”</q> iti । tatra tāvat śrutiliṅga-
vākyaiḥ viniyōjyaṁ śēṣatvamuktaṁ prakaraṇēna viniyōjyaṁ punaḥ kimatra
bhaviṣyati । nanu ca prayājādayaḥ santyēva kimiti praśnaḥ ।
bāḍhaṁ praśnārthaḥ vidyatē prayājādīnāṁ hi ēkaniyōgalakṣaṇasaṁbandhaṁ
caturthē vakṣyati darśapūrṇamāsādibhiḥ kimatrānyatsaṁbandhē pramāṇaṁ
mr̥gyatē । ēvaṁ ca tadbhūtādhikaraṇa ēvōktaḥ saṁbandhaḥ anvitā-
midhāyibhiḥ padaiḥ sarvatra śabdārthāvagamē hēturiti vyāpakaṁ
bhavati । pramāṇāntarē punaranviṣyamāṇē nānvitābhidhānanibandhanaḥ
﻿<pb n="b758"/>
śakyatē pradarśayitum । prakaraṇādibhirhi vākyārthānāṁ saṁbandhāvagatiḥ ।
na ca vākyārthasya vākyārthasya ca saṁbandhē padābhidhānalakṣaṇaḥ saṁbandha
upapadyatē । anvitaṁ hi padārthāntarēṇa padārthamācaṣṭē padaṁ, na
vākyārthaṁ vākyārthāntarēṇa । atō darśapūrṇamāsārthatayā prayājādi-
vākyārthānvayaṁ aśābdaṁ manyamānasya praśnaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu caitānyēva pramāṇātīti aśābdaṁ manvānasya praś‍nēnaiva
bhavitavyam na punaḥ kimētāvantyēva pramāṇānīva । ucyatē---ēta-
dēvōk‍taṁ yadyasaṁyuk‍taṁ na tarhi viniyōjyam । atō'saṁyuktamiti
vadatā ētāvantyēva pramāṇānītyuk‍taṁ bhavati । tasmāt yuktō'yaṁ praśnaḥ
﻿<pb n="b759"/>
---kimētāvantyēva pramāṇānīti । itarastu nāvaśyaṁ padārthā-
ntarānvitamēva śābdam । aidamarthyēnāpi śabdaḥ saṁbandhaṁ
pratipādayatyēvēti manvānō nētyuktavān । itarastu pr̥cchati 1kimaparaṁ
kāraṇamiti praśnēnaivōpakramaḥ pūrvapakṣa iti, pūrvōktapraśnārthavivaraṇaṁ
﻿<pb n="b760"/>
kā nāmēyaṁ nadīti ca । na cānirjñātanadyarthasyaivōpapadyatē praśna iti 
prakaṭīkr̥taḥ praśnārthaḥ <q>‘kathaṁ punarasaṁyuktasyaiva viniyōgaḥ’</q> । tadi-
damaidamarthyailakṣaṇaṁ kathayati iti kartavyatārthitvāditi । aidamarthyēnāpi
śabdaḥ sabandhaṁ pratipādayatyēvēti ।</p>
<p>nanu caikaniyōgalakṣaṇasaṁbandhō'yamityuktam । kimidamiti-
kartavyatārthitvaṁ nāma ? ucyatē---ēkaniyōgalakṣaṇa ēva saṁbandhō
nōpapadyatē yadītikartavyatā lakṣaṇaḥ saṁbandhō na syāt । na
hyasaṁbandhavidhēyasya ēkaniyōgatā upapadyatē vidhēyanānātvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b761"/>
upapadyatē ca karaṇētikartavyatayā saṁbandhaḥ । anyatrāpi sādhyē
darśanāt । sādhyaścāyaṁ niyōgārthaḥ । tasmādupapannaṁ itikartavya-
tārthitvāditi vidhēyasaṁbandhakāraṇam । kimiti tadbhūtādhikaraṇē
vākyasyaivārthēnautpattikaḥ saṁbandhō darśitaḥ । ucyatē---asūtrārthajñō
bhavān । kriyārthēnēti vadatā sarvasyaivāsya prāmāṇyaṁ darśitam ।
tasmādaidamarthyalakṣaṇamēva saṁbandhaṁ vēdē vēdavidō manyantē । tatsidhyarthaṁ
tu padārthānāmapi anvitābhidhānaṁ darśitam । aidamarthyamēva hi
﻿<pb n="b762"/>
pramāṇāntaratvē hētuḥ । anvitābhidhānaṁ tu pramāṇāntarapūrvakēṣvapi
tulyam dēvadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmōdanaṁ pacatītyēvamādiṣu laukikēṣu
vākyēṣu । ataḥ prakaraṇaviniyōjyamapi śēṣatvamastīti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">1kramaśca dēśasāmānyāt ।। sū. 12. a. 5 ।।</ab>
<p>atrēdānīṁ kaḥ praśnārthaḥ aidamarthyalakṣaṇamēva hi saṁbandhaṁ vēdavidō
manyanta ityuktam । nanu caitāvantyēva pramāṇānītyākṣēpēṇa bhavitavyaṁ
kimidaṁ <q>‘kimētāvantyēva pramāṇānī’</q>ti । atrōcyatē-atrāpyasaṁyukta-
﻿<pb n="b763"/>
grahaṇaṁ viṣayāntarapradarśanārtham । satyamaidamarthyavyatirēkēṇa saṁbandhō
nāsti, tathāpi pramāṇāntaramasti aidamarthyaviśēṣāvagatau sthāna-
sāmānyaṁ nāma tadidamuk‍taṁ---kramaśca dēśasāmānyāditi । prayōjanaṁ tu
darśitamēva ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">1ākhyā caivaṁ tadarthatvāta ।। sū. 13. a. 6 ।।</ab>
<p>atrēdānīṁ praśnārthō nōpapadyatē aidamarthyē sati sthānavat
viśēṣāvagamē hētutvāt samākhyāyāḥ । ucyatē---astyatra
viśēṣaḥ yuk‍taṁ tāvatsthānasya viśēṣāvagahētutvaṁ vaidikatvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b764"/>
samākhyā punaḥ laukikī । na ca laukikamabhidhānaṁ vēdārthāvagamē
hēturbhavati । yathā <q>‘pacati’</q> ityēvamādipu । ata idaṁ kimētāvantyēva
pramāṇānīti । atrōcyatē । samākhyāyā laukikatvēpi vaidi-
kasyārthasya viśēṣāvagamē hētutvaṁ pratipadyatē । kutaḥ ? abhidhānaṁ
hi kr̥ttaddhitasamāsānāṁ saṁbandhini prasiddhaṁ vaidikasyārthasya cēdama-
bhidhānaṁ yadyapi svayaṁ laukikam । atō viśēṣamavagamayati । na
cēdaṁ smr̥tivat pramāṇāntarāpēkṣaṁ autpattikatvāt śabdārtha-

﻿<pb n="b765"/>
saṁbandhasya । tasmādyuktaṁ ākhyā caivaṁ tadarthatvāta iti yatō
viśēṣāvagamē hētuḥ । prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<p>śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṁ samavāyē pāradaurbalyamartha-
viprakarṣāt ।। 7 ।।</p>
<p><quote>1kā punaratra śrutiḥ ? kiṁ liṅgamiti</quote> । nanu cāyaṁ praśnō nōpapadyatē ।
kimiti nōpapadyatē ? yasmāt uktāni viniyōgē kāraṇāni
iyuktam । na cānirjñātasya uktatā saṁbhavati । tasmādvipratiṣiddhaṁ
<q>“uktāni viniyōgē kāraṇānīti । kā punaratra śrutiḥ rkiṁ liṅgaṁ”</q>
iti ca ।</p>

﻿<pb n="b766"/>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ viniyōga ēva śrutyādibhiruk‍tō, na
punaḥ śrutyādīnāṁ svarūpamiti । yadyēvaṁ tarhi vaktavyaṁ uk‍taḥ
śrutyādibhirviniyōga iti । na viniyōgē kāraṇānyuktānīti ।
kiñca viniyōgōktyā viniyōgakāraṇānyuktāni bhavantyēva । kāryataḥ
kāraṇaparijñānāt । arthāvacchēdyamēva hi śābdaṁ viśēṣatō bhavati ।
svarūpatō varṇamātragrahaṇāt । atō viniyōgōktyāpi1 naiva praśnō
na ghaṭatē । śrutiliṅgayōśca svarūpamabhidhāya punarvākyapraśnē kō'bhi-
prāyō na vidmaḥ । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ saṁhatyārthamabhidhati padāni vākyaṁ

﻿<pb n="b767"/>
miti spaṣṭamēvānyatvamupalabhāmahē । tasmādasaṁbaddhamēvēdaṁ bhāṣyamiti
arthajñānamāninō manyatē ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---satyamarthāt pramāṇāvagatistathāpi upapadyata
ēvāyaṁ praśnaḥ kā punaratra śrutiriti । kathamupapadyatē ? satyaṁ gārhapatya-
śravaṇaṁ śrutiḥ satyaṁ ca indrābhidhānasāmarthyaṁ liṅgaṁ tathāpi padāntara-
nirapēkṣaṁ naivōbhayaṁ śakyatē'vagantum । aindrayā gārhapatyaḥ upasthā-
tavya iti । nāpīndraparatā mantrasya । tulyē padāntarasavyapēkṣatvē
﻿<pb n="b768"/>
viśēṣaṁ ajānan pr̥cchati---<quote>kā punaratra śrutiḥ kiṁ liṅgamiti</quote> । atha
kimityādāvēva ētanna nirūpitaṁ <quote>śrutyādīni viniyōgē kāraṇānī</quote>tyāsmin bhāṣya
ēva । atrōcyatē---tatrāpyētat utsūtramēva vaktavyam । iyāṁstu atra
viśēṣaḥ <q>‘śrutiliṅga’</q> ityasya sūtrasya vyākhyātavyatayā aupōddhāti-
katayā saṁbaddhamabhidhānaṁ bhavati । kathaṁ punaridānīṁ tulyē padāntara-
saṁbandhē gārhapatyaśabdasya śrutitōcyatē ? iyamucyatē padāntara-
saṁbandhastu indrābhidhānē gārhapatyābhidhānē vā aviśiṣṭaḥ । gārhaṁ-
patyaśravaṇamēva gārhapatyābhidhānē vyāpriyatē । nanu dvitīyā vyāpriyata
ityuktam । satyamuktam gārhapatyaśravaṇē sati । ataḥ padasyaiva
﻿<pb n="b769"/>
nidarśitaṁ na prātipadikamātrasya । ēvamindrābhidhānēpi mantrē
padāntaramudāstē । ēvaṁ ca sati vākyē praśnōttaramētadvivēkāyē-
tyupapannamēva । atō'sādhāraṇapratipattinimittatayā saṁhatyārthā-
bhidhānē satyapi śrutirliṅgamiti cōcyatē । tasmādupapannaṁ śruti-
liṅga‍yōrvirōdhē kimubhayaṁ viniyōjakaṁ uta śrutirēvēti । prakaraṇa-
praśnābhiprāyaṁ tu svasthānē vakṣyāmaḥ, kramasamākhyayōśca ।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṁ sati vaktavyaṁ śrutiḥ liṅgaṁ cōbhayaṁ pramāṇaṁ ata śruti-
rbalīyasīti । iha punaḥ śrutiliṅagayōḥ kiṁ śrutirbalīyasī āhō-
svit liṅgamiti na ghaṭatē । yasmādidamapi kāraṇaṁ śrutiḥ liṅgamapīti ।
﻿<pb n="b770"/>
tasmādyathaivōpanyastamasmābhiḥ tathaivōpanyasanīyam, na tu kiṁ
śrutirbalīyasī āhōsvit liṅgamiti । tulyabalē ētē
kāraṇē iti ca pūrvaṣakṣahētudarśanāt । tasmādanyathaivōpanyā-
sō'nyathaivōpasaṁhāra iti । viruddhaṁ phalamapyēvamēvōpanyastam
kimindrasya gārhapatyasya cōpasthānaṁ kartavyaṁ, uta gārhapatyasyaivēti ।
tasmādupakramōpasaṁhārayōḥ sāmyaṁ vaktavyam ।</p>
<p>yadapi ca ēvaṁ tarhi liṅgavākyē virudhyamānē iha saṁpradhāryētē na
śrutiliṅgē iti tadapyayuktamiva, sarvatra samavētaṁ vivik‍taṁ ca dr̥śyata
ityuktatvāt vivēkasya । yā śrutiḥ sā liṅgēna viruddha‍yata iti vākyaṁ
punaḥ lakṣaṇayāpyupapadyata ēvētyuktvā athavēti śrutyantarōpanyāsaḥ
kimaparitōṣāt uta vikalpārtha ityētadapi naiva jñāyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b771"/>
<p>ucyatē---yastāvadupanyāsaḥ kiṁ balīyasī śrutiḥ āhō---
svilliṅgamiti tatrāyabhiprāyaḥ । kiṁ liṅgōnmardanēnaiva yathā śrutiḥ pramāṇa
tathā liṅgamapi । yadi ca ubhayamubhayōpamardanēnaiva pramāṇaṁ tadōpapadyata
ēvāyamupanyāsaḥ kiṁ balīyasī śrutiḥ āhōsvilliṅgamiti ।</p>
<p>ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati---na vidmaḥ kiṁ balīya iti । tasmādubhayaṁ
pramāṇaṁ ubhayaprāmāṇyē cōbhayōrabhidhānam । ata ēva cāniyama
ityuktam <q>“yadi tulyabalē ētē kāraṇē”</q> iti ca viśēṣāgrahaṇāt ।
<q>“tatō vikalpa”</q>1 iti । kō'yaṁ vikalpaḥ ? nanu cāsmin pakṣē
samuccaya ēva । abhidhānavikalpamaṅgīkr̥tyaitaduktaṁ na prayōgavikalpam
﻿<pb n="b772"/>
yadi tu liṅgaṁ balīyaḥ’ ityētadapi bhāṣyamupanyāsavat draṣṭavyam ।
ēvaṁ tarhōtyuk‍tē viśēṣē punaḥ praśnaḥ kēnābhiprāyēṇa ? na kēvalāt
gārhapatyaśravaṇāta tadupasthānāvagatiḥ । tāvanmātrasya ca śratitva-
mupadarśitam । tadidānīṁ rāddhāntavādyabhiprāyaṁ vivr̥ṇōti---satyaṁ
vākyādr̥tē nāyamavagamaḥ gārhapatyaśravaṇāt tadupasthānāvagatiriti ।
yā'tra śrutirityuktam indrābhidhānēpi tulyatvāt । kathaṁ ? balīya-
syapi hi liṅgē aindrayōpatiṣṭhata ityētat gārhapatyaśabdēna sahaika-
vākyatāmupētyaiva । yadi hi nōpēyāt tatō liṅgēna virudhyēta
tasmāt śrutiliṅgayōrvirōdhaḥ । atha vā nātra ēkavākyatvāditi
﻿<pb n="b773"/>
pakṣāntarōpanyāsaḥ sakalapadapradarśanārtha iti vyākhyātam । kiṁ
punaratra yuktam ? ubhayatra svārthāvagamāt । liṅgādapi liṅgārthō'vagamyatē
śrutērapi hi śrutyarthaḥ । vākyasya caudāsīnyāt ubhayatrābhidhānamātraṁ
virudhyatē । na cābhidhānē kaścidviśēṣō'vagaṁmyata ityataḥ tulyabalē ētē
kāraṇē ityuktam । 1<quote><q>“nanu liṅgasya bhaṅgurasyēva rūpaṁ savicikitsō hi liṅgātpratyaya”</q></quote> iti ।
kēyaṁ vicikitsā nāma ? asamyak pratyayaḥ । kimatrāsamyaktvam ।
nahīndrābhidhānāt indrō'bhidhātavya iti pratyayō bhavatītyarthaḥ ।
bhavati tu gārhapatyaśravaṇāt vidhāyakavākyagatatvāta gārhapatya-
śabdasya । nanu cāvidhāyakatvāt liṅgasya prāmāṇyamēva nāsti, kathaṁ
﻿<pb n="b774"/>
virōdha iti । satyaṁ---abhidhānasāmarthyamātraṁ naiva pramāṇam-iti-
kartavyatāvagamē satyanyatō viśēṣāvagamē pramāṇaṁ, kartavyatāvagamāt
prakaraṇādibhiḥ । karmavyatāvagamē cābhidhānamātramavaśiṣyata ityuktam ।
tasmāta tulyabalē ētē kāraṇē iti । <q>“1balīyānapi hi hētuḥ”</q> iti
na ca tāvat balīyān, anvāruhyāpi na virōdhō'stīti manyatē ।
<quote>nanvayamēva virōdhaḥ sakr̥t upasthānaṁ cōditam asakr̥dabhinirvartyata iti । naivam---upasthēya-
bhēdāt pratipradhānamāvartantē guṇā iti nyāya ēvaiṣaḥ na virōdhō'rthaḥ</quote> । nanu cēdaṁ avi-
rōdhōttaraṁ na ghaṭatē । nahyatrōpasthēyadvayaṁ śrūyatē aindrayā
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭata iti gārhapatya ēvaikaḥ upasthēyatayā
śrūyatē nēndrō'pīti । tasmādanuttaramidam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b775"/>
<p>ucyatē---prakaraṇāt kartavyatāvagamāt indrapadāt indrā-
bhidhānaṁ pratīyata iti manvānēna <q>‘upasthēyabhēdāt’</q> ityuktam ।
vākyasāmānyāt । ēvaṁ tarhi gauṇamukhyatā nōpapadyata iti
punarvirōdhōpanyāsaḥ । nanu ca pratipradhānaṁ guṇāvr̥ttau satyāṁ
