naivāsau virōdhō ghaṭatē । aviniyuktamantrāpēkṣō'yaṁ virōdhaḥ ।
viniyōgē tvavirōdhaḥ iti siddhō'tra pūrvapakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---<quote>śrutiliṅgayōrvirōdhē śrutirbalīyasī iti । kutaḥ ? arthaviprakarṣāt ।
kimidaṁ arthaviprakarṣāditi arthasya viprakarṣaḥ arthaviprakarṣaḥ । kaḥ punararthaḥ ? śrutyarthaḥ
﻿<pb n="b776"/>
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti sannikr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutyarthaḥ । indraḥ upasthēya iti viprakr̥ṣṭaḥ । kathaṁ ?
<q>‘kadācana starī:’</q> ityanēna mantrēṇēndra upasthātavya iti na śrūyatē । satyapīndrābhidhānasāmarthyē
vacanābhāvat anupasthānīyaḥ indra ityavagamyatē</quote> । nanu pūrvamēvōktaṁ satyāṁ kartavya-
tāyāṁ indrābhidhānaṁ pramāṇaṁ, tataścōbhayatrābhidhānē tulyataiva । atō
dvayōḥ prāmāṇyamiti । kimidaṁ punarākṣiptam samāhitaṁ ca ?
<quote><q>“dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapēkṣaṁ syāt iti । yadētat prakaraṇaṁ liṅgaṁ ca ubhyamapyēta-
daśābdam । na cātikrāntapratyakṣa ēva ēvaṁlakṣaṇakē'rthē śabdamantarēṇa paricchēdō'vakalpatē ।
atō manyāmahē viprakr̥ṣṭaṁ śrutyarthālliṅgamiti”</q></quote> ucyatē---aśābdamētaditi viśēṣaṁ
pradarśayitum । nanu caivaṁ sati prāmāṇyamēvāsya hīyatē । kutō
﻿<pb n="b777"/>
virōdhaḥ । adhāyamabhiprāyaḥ asati virōdhē smr̥tivalliṅgasya prāmāṇya-
miti । tadayuktam । kutaḥ ? smr̥tērhi arthamavagamya virōdhādviparyayaḥ
kalpyatē । iha punaḥ upasthānaṁ naivāvagamyata ityuktam । kathamana-
vagamyamānē'rthē'numānam । tasmāddurgr̥hītastēnasaṁbhāṣitavadasaṁbandhaṁ
pratibhāti । punarapi kartavyatāpēkṣālliṅgādēvārthāvagatiṁ darśayati ।
śrutisaṁbhavē vā avagativākyasādhāraṇyē sati kathamayaṁ viśēṣa
iti vaktavyam । atrābhidhīyatē---kartavyasyētikartavyatākāṅkṣasya
vacanaṁ prakaraṇamiti prakaraṇādaidamarthyalakṣaṇa ēva saṁbandhaḥ na punaḥ
anvitapadārthalakṣaṇa ityuktam । tataḥ kim ? anvitapadārtha-
﻿<pb n="b778"/>
lakṣaṇaḥ saṁbandhaḥ padārthēbhya ēvāvasīyatē । aidamarthyalakṣaṇastu kēvalaṁ
kāryata ēvēti na padārthānvayē vyāpārō'vagamyatē । ēvamapi kō
viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśēṣaḥ---1padārthānvitalakṣaṇaḥ tasmin
sati paścātkāryayōgaḥ pada rthānvayalakṣaṇastu prathamata ēva । sō'yamartha-
viprakarṣaḥ । anvayapradarśanārthaṁ ca tārtīyaṁ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṁ śēṣaśēṣividō
manyantē । sa cānvayaḥ śrutau prathamataramavagamyata iti na kāryataḥ
pāścātyāyāṁ padārthānvayāvagatau pramāṇamasti । nahyanvitasyānvayō
dr̥śyatē yataḥ । tasyāt sūktaṁ liṅgāt śrutirbalīyasīti ।
ānumānikamabhidhānaṁ ca padārthānvayāpēkṣamēva draṣṭavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b779"/>
1vikalpasya cānyāyyatvāditi mantravākyāpēkṣam । nēndraśabdasyā-
bhidhānadvayaṁ nyāyyamityabhiprāyaḥ । atō na viniyuktasya viniyōgō
ghaṭata iti pradarśitō hētuḥ । yaduktamavirōdha iti; ēvamuk‍tō virōdhaḥ
yadutēndraśabdasya mantravākyāpēkṣayā nābhidhānadvayamupapadyata
iti । aidamarthyasyānvayalabhyatvāt śrutāvuparatā kartavyatāpēkṣēti
nākāṅkṣādvayamupapadyata iti virōdhaḥ । tadidamakr̥tasāmarthyatvaṁ
mantravākyasya niyōgasya cōktaṁ vākyaprakaraṇaśabdābhyām ।
﻿<pb n="b780"/>
ata upapannō'rthaviprakarṣaḥ । 1<q>“liṅgavākyayōrvirōdhē kimudāharaṇam ?
syōnaṁ tē sadanaṁ kr̥ṇōmi ghr̥tasya dhārayā suśēvaṁ kalpayāmi
tasmin sīda amr̥tē pratitiṣṭha vrīhīṇāṁ mēdha sumanasyamānaḥ iti”</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu cārthaviprakarṣādityuktō hētuḥ sāpēkṣanirapēkṣatvaṁ ca liṅga-
vākyayōḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b781"/>
<p>ataḥ prakaṭa ēvārthaviprakarṣaḥ kimityadhikaraṇāntaramāra-
bhyatē । na kēvalamidamadhikaraṇaṁ, sarvādhikaraṇākṣēpa ēvāyam ।
sujñānō hyarthaviprakarṣaḥ । kathaṁ? liṅgaṁ tāvaduktaṁ nirapēkṣatvāditi ।
vākyamapi padārthānvayāvagamyamānasaṁbandhaṁ aidamarthyalakṣaṇāt balīya
iti pradarśitam । prakaraṇamapi tadapēkṣitvāt kramasya kramādūlīyaḥ।
ēvaṁ kramō'pi saṁbandhakr̥ttayā vēdāvagamyatvācca samākhyāyā balīyā-
nēva । atō nārambhaṇīyānyēvaitāni adhikaraṇānītyarthaviprakarṣajñānā-
bhimāninō manyatē । atrōcyatē---yattāvadidamuktaṁ nirapēkṣatvālliṅgaṁ
balīya iti । tadayuktam । kasmāt ? sakalasya hi mantrasya kartavya-
tāvagamāt na kēvalāt padāt kartavyatāvagamō bhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b782"/>
atō vākyamēva prathamataraṁ padānāṁ parasparasaṁbandhāvagamē hētuḥ । saṁba-
ndhasya ca kāryāvagatiḥ । tasmādvākyamēva balīya iti bhavati matiḥ ।
avaśyaṁ caitadēvamabhyupagantavyam । anyathā hi avirōdhisyōnādi-
padāntarasaṁbandhō'pi nirapēkṣatvālliṅgasya viniyōgē na syāt ।
atō durjñānō'yaṁ vākyaliṅgayōḥ viprakarṣa iti prārabdhamidamadhikaraṇam ।
ayamēva ca pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ padāntarasavyapēkṣaṁ liṅgaṁ viniyō-
jakamityubhayatra viniyōgaḥ । yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ1 liṅgasya śrutyāpi bādhi-
tatvāditi । kō'yaṁ hētuḥ ? na hi śrutyā bādhitasyānyēnāpi bādhyatā ।
﻿<pb n="b783"/>
tasmāt bāliśabhāṣitamēvēdaṁ pratibhāti । nēdaṁ bāliśabhāṣitam ।
anyō'bhiprāyaścōdakasya । yathaiva śrutyā padārthānvayasaṁbandhajñānakāraṇa-
tvēna liṅgaṁ bādhitaṁ kāryaikyaviniyōjyatvādēvaṁ vākyēnāpīti pūrvapakṣi-
tam । atrābhidhīyatē---yajuṣastāvadviniyōgaḥ pratipadam । kāryataḥ
punaraikyaṁ padānāṁ, yāvadēkaṁ kāryaṁ tāvadaviruddhaḥ padāntarasaṁbandhaḥ ।
kāryāntarē tu pratyarthini na kāryāntarasaṁbandhitā śakyatē pratipat‍tuṁ
pratipadavidhānādēva । atra hi kāryatō mantratvam । na mantrataḥ kāryaṁ
<pb n="b784"/>
yathā r̥kṣu sāmasu ca । ataḥ kāryanirapēkṣakēvalapadārthānvaya-
saṁbandhitāṁ vākyanibandhinīṁ bādhatē liṅgam ।</p>
<p>nanu ca śrutāvapyēvamēva prāpnōti । satyaṁ prāpnōti yadīdaṁ yajuḥ
syāt tat‍tu śrutiviniyōjyatvaṁ r̥kṣu pradarśitam । r̥cāṁ tu
mantrataḥ kāryamityuktam । yajuṣāṁ punaḥ yatrāpi iṣē tvēti viniyōgaḥ
tatrāpyupādānavaśādvicchēdaḥ na punaḥ kāryōpādānābhyāṁ anyō
yajuṣṭvē hēturasti । tasmādyuktō vākyabhēdaḥ । yatpunaridaṁ bhāṣya-
kārēṇa pradarśitaṁ---1<q>“nanu caikavākyatvēpi liṅgamēva vyāpriyata”</q> iti ।
tadayuktamiva pratibhāti । kimiti, kāryatō'trārthanirṇayaḥ । kutaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b785"/>
na sāmarthyamātrāt, kāryasavyapēkṣaṁ hi sāmarthyaṁ liṅgamiti
nirūpitam । yadapi ca parihr̥taṁ---<q>“arthaviprakarṣō'tra bādhyatvē hētuḥ ।
asti caikavākyabhūtasya liṅgasyābhidhānālliṅgāt viprakarṣaḥ”</q>
iti । tadapyayuktamiva । ēkavākyatāhētōrliṅgasyāliṅgatvā-
dityuk‍tam । atrōcyatē---pratipadaṁ viniyōgāt ēkavākya-
tayāpi ca kāryōpapattēḥ yuktā liṅgatāśaṅkā । parihāraścārtha-
viprakarṣāt । tasmānnātra śrutirliṅgaṁ vākyamiti tantraṁ, viprakr̥ṣṭaṁ
aprāpakamiti sūtrārthaḥ । ataḥ siddhaṁ kāryabhēdādvākyabhēda iti । tarhi
tasmin sīdēti kimālambanamidaṁ ? pūrvaprakr̥tālambanamēvēvati brūmaḥ ।
nanu caivaṁ sati parārthataiva pūrvasya prāpnōti tataśca vākyaṁ
balavadityuktaṁ bhavati । nāvaśyaṁ parāmarśē tādarthyamēva
﻿<pb n="b786"/>
bhavati । anyārthamapyanyārthēnāvamr̥śyatē ēva sarvanām‍nētyadōṣaḥ । yathā
tatprayōjakō hēturiti, yathā ca vēdē ētasyaiva rēvatīṣviti ।
tasmādvalīyō'bhidhānamiti siddham । aya 1vākyaprakaraṇayōḥ
kathamiti । kiṁ punaḥ prakaraṇaṁ nāmēti । kō'yaṁ praśnaḥ ? itikartavya-
tārthitvādityēvaṁ nirjñātē prakaraṇē na vidmaḥ kimarthō'yaṁ praśna iti ।
atrōcyatē---iti kartavyatārthitvādityuktam । na vidmaḥ kasyēyamiti
kartavyatārthitēti । yasyēyamitikartavyatākāṅkṣā tadatrōcyatē
---kartavyasyēti niyōgārthasyētyarthaḥ । tasyētikartavyatākāṅkṣasya
yēyaṁ tr̥tīyākāṅkṣā tatprakaraṇaṁ tēna biniyōgaḥ । tadviniyōgē kāraṇaṁ
na kartavyatāmātraṁ nāpyanyat । ta smādupapannaḥpraśnārthaḥ, uttaraṁ ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b787"/>
<p>idānīṁ vākyaprakaraṇayōḥvirōdhē <q>“1tulyabalē ētē kāraṇē”</q> iti
kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? kāryārthatvādanvayasya ubhayaṁ kāryēṇa viniyujyata
iti । yadvā kāryādr̥tē'nvayasya bādhitatvāt prakaraṇamēva balīyaḥ ।
tatpratyayatvādvākyasya । ēvaṁ manyānēnōktaṁ vākyasya bādhitatvāditi ।
﻿<pb n="b788"/>
atrōcyatē---atrāpyarthaviprakarṣādityuktō hētuḥ । kathamartha-
viprakarṣaḥ uktaḥ? kāryārthatayānvayaḥ kalpyaḥ । na ca klr̥ptānva-
yasya kāryārthatvē siddhē'nvayāntaraṁ viniyuktaviniyōgavirōdhāt
liṅgavacchakyatē pratipat‍tum । tasmādvākyaṁ balīyaḥ । durjñānaviprakarṣa-
jñāpanāyādhikaraṇaprapañcō'yaṁ liṅgavat sarvatra draṣṭavyaḥ । udāharaṇa-
muktam । <q>“1 atha prakaraṇasya kramasya ca virōdhē kimudāharam”</q> iti ।
atrāpi pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē kramaprakaraṇayōstulyabalatvamiti ।
﻿<pb n="b789"/>
kathaṁ ? bhāṣyakārastāvat ajñānamēva vyapadiśati1 । kimajñānāt‍tulya-
balatvaṁ sidhyati ? jñānasya hi tulyabalatvaṁ atulyabalatvaṁ vā viṣayaḥ
nājñānasya । nanu cājñānamapi pramāṇatayōpanyastamēva । na, vyavahāra-
mātraṁ tadityuk‍tam । pramāṇāntarapramēyābhāvamātraṁ pramēyam । iha
tulyabalatvaṁ atulyabalatvaṁ ca na pramāṇāntarapramēyabhāvamātraṁ
śakyatē vak‍tum । kathaṁ tarhyētadbhāṣyaṁ <q>“na tāvadviśēṣamupalabhāmaha”</q>
iti । bhāṣyakāra ēvātra praṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---durvidagdhavacanamātramidam । ayamabhi-
prāyō bhāṣyakārasya । nātrānayōrviśēṣō jñāyata iti
﻿<pb n="b790"/>
sarvatra prakaraṇānusyūtēḥ kramō'pi kāryavānavagamyatē ēva । kāryataśca
sannidhiranvitamavagamayatīti । pratyuta prakaraṇamēvātra bādhyatayāva-
gamyatē । viśēṣōpasaṁhārāt sannidhēḥ । na hi klr̥ptasya sannidhēḥ
kalpanā śakyatē vak‍tum । anvayasyēva । tatpunaridamanvāruhya-
vacanamityuktamādhastyē'dhikaraṇē । sarvatra caivaṁ draṣṭavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b791"/>
atrōcyatē---kramātprakaraṇaṁ balīyaḥ । kutaḥ ? na hyanā-
kāṅkṣitasya kramaḥ saṁbandhē hētuḥ । sannidhimātraṁ hi kramaḥ ।
na ca sannidhimātrāt saṁbandhō bhāryā rājñaḥ puruṣō dēvadattasyētivata ।
ākāṅkṣā ca prakaraṇavatāṁ tulyēti sarvapradhānasaṁbandhō vidēvanādīnām
kramāddhi ākāṅkṣā, ākāṅkṣātō'nvayaḥ anvayācca tādarthyamiti ।
sō'yamarthaviprakarṣaḥ । yaduktaṁ kramādākāṅkṣōpasaṁhāra iti tadayuktam ।
sarvārthatvēpi kasyacitsannidhānabhavaśyaṁbhāvīti pāṭhārthamēva tat ।
﻿<pb n="b792"/>
bādhitasya hyanugrahō nyāyya ityuktam । “prakaraṇavataḥ sākāṅkṣatvāt
sannidhānē cāmnātēna paripūrṇēnāpyavakalpata ēkavākyatvaṁ iti । kimidaṁ
paripūrṇēnāpi iti ? ētaduktaṁ bhavati---na cētkramaḥ prakaraṇaṁ
ēkavākyataiva nāsti । nanu ākāṅkṣā sannidhiryōgyatvamiti
caikavākyatvē hētuḥ । satyaṁ vākyārthāvagatau, iha punarvā-
kyārthasya vākyārthasya ca saṁbandhaḥ । sa cētikartavyatārthitayaiva
saṁbadhyata ityuktam । kramaḥ punaḥ vākyārthasya ca sannidhāna-
mityuktam । yathā bhāryārājñaḥ puruṣō dēvadattasyētyatra pradarśitam ।
﻿<pb n="b793"/>
<q>“atha kramasamākhyayōḥ kathaṁ ?”</q> kramō hyākāṅkṣāvataḥ sannidhaubhavati
viśēṣāvagatau hētuḥ । samākhyā punaḥ viśēṣanimittaivēti tulyabalē
ētē kāraṇē iti । tasmādubhayaṁ viniyōjakam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b794"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---kramō balīyān vaidikō hyasau sannidhiḥ ।
samākhyāpunarlaukikī । nanu caivaṁ vadatā samākhyā naiva pramāṇamityuktaṁ
bhavati । maibaṁ vōcaḥ arthaviprakarṣa ēvānēna prakārēṇōcyatē । kathaṁ ?
samākhyā hi saṁbandhanimittā satī sannidhānādyavagamayati ।
kramaḥ punaḥ svayamēva sannidhiḥ । na ca pratyakṣasya sannidhēḥ punaḥ
sannidhānāntarakalpanāṁ ghaṭatē iti sō'yamarthaviprakarṣaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi
samākhyā ? samavāyādibhiḥ upapadyatē brāhmaṇagrāmavat ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b795"/>
<p>1<q>“atha yat tatra tatrābhidhīyatē idamanēna bādhyaṁ idamanēna
bādhyamiti tatra yadbādhyatē kiṁ tadbādhakaviṣayaṁ prāptaṁ utāprāptamiti”</q> ।
kasya vyākhyānamētat ? na kasyacidapīti brūmaḥ । kiṁ tarhi anēna
atra kriyatē । bhāṣyakāra ēvātra praṣṭavyaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē
---śrutyādīnāṁ balābalacintāśēṣabhūtamidaṁ bhāṣyam । kathaṁ kr̥tvā ?
balābalacintā hi bādhyāpēkṣiṇī । tadidānīṁ bādhyaṁ kiṁ
bādhakaviṣayaṁ prāptaṁ sat bādhyatē utāprāptamiti । ubhayathā'bhi-
hitō dōṣaḥ । nanu ca prāptabādhō daśamē darśita ēva । kimiti
prāptau satyāṁ virōdhō darśitaḥ । ucyatē---kāryataḥ prāptau na dōṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b796"/>
<p>ihōpadēśaścintyatē । upadēśēna ca prāptiḥ durbādhēti tatraiva
daśamē pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ । iha kasmāttanna pradarśyatē ? pradarśita-
mēva <q>“pratipradhānamāvartantē guṇā”</q> iti । kathaṁ pratipradhānāvr̥ttyabhidhānē-
nābādhaḥ pradarśitō bhavati । dvayōḥ prāmāṇyābhyupagamēna
pratipradhānābhidhānāt । prāptēścāviśēṣāt । tasmāt ayuktamida-
manēna bādhyamiti aprāptē'pi । atrēdānīmupadēśabādhavidō
'bhidadhati । sāmānyataḥ prāptiṁ manvānā viśēṣamapaśyantaḥ smr̥ti---
pramōṣanimittaṁ prāptijñānaṁ vyapadiśanti śuktikāyāmiva rajata-
jñānam । viśēṣāvagamāt‍tu tattēṣāṁ nivartata iti bādhaśabdaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b797"/>
nanu cāyamuk‍tō bādhaḥ prathamapāda ēva <q>‘yasya ca duṣṭaṁ
karaṇaṁ’</q> ityatra kimiti punarupanyastaḥ ? ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b798"/>
<p>astyatra viśēṣaḥ tatra hi śuk‍tikārthasyāgrahaṇāt rajatē
ca smarāmīti pramōṣāt vyapadēśasiddhiḥ । iha punarāga-
mikatvēna dvayasyāpi tulyatāpattirbhavatyēvēti punarārabdham ।
kiṁ punarāgamikatvē dvayasyāpi tulyatāpattiḥ । tulyatāpattau
vā bādhaḥ । atrōcyatē---svatō viparyayābhāvāt । na śuk‍tikādi-
ṣviva svayamēva viyarpayō bhavati aparīkṣitakāraṇasvabhāvasyāpi ।
<pb n="b799"/>
iha punaḥ kāraṇaparīkṣādvārakō viparyaya iti prārabdhamidama-
dhikaraṇam । tadviśudhyarthaṁ cēdaṁ bhāṣyam । sō'yaṁ aprāptabādha
iti sūktam ।। 8 ।।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 6 ।। ahīnō vā prakaraṇādnauṇaḥ ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē---kiṁ niyōgasannidhirbalīyān
﻿<pb n="b800"/>
uta viniyōgasannidhiriti । pūrvapakṣavādī kāryārthatvādviniyōgasya
prakr̥takāryasaṁbhavē prakr̥takāryasaṁbandhō yukta iti manyatē । kathaṁ tarhi
viniyōgaḥ ? kāryārthatvāt, tadanuguṇō vyākhyāyatē । ēvaṁ tarhi prakara-
ṇādvākyaṁ durbalamityuk‍tam, na, san‍nidhānāviśēṣē hi vākyaṁ balīyaḥ ।
yatra punaḥ kāryasan‍nidhirēva nāsti kiṁ tatra vākyaṁ kariṣyati ।
﻿<pb n="b801"/>
tasmāt kāryānuguṇaiva padārthavyākhyēti yuk‍taṁ na hīyata
ityahīnaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">1asaṁyōgāt‍tu mukhyasya tasmādapakr̥ṣyatē ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>atra bhaṇyatē---uk‍tamasmābhiḥ padārthānvayaḥ saṁbandhakāraṇaṁ
kāryatō'pyanvaya ēvāvagamyatē । na cānvayāvagamē pratītānvayatyāgō
yuktaḥ । na ca dr̥ṣṭē hastini tatpādēnānumānaṁ saṁbhavati । tasmāda-
pratipakṣamēva padārthavyākhyānaṁ yuktam । padārtha ēva hi padārthaprati-
pakṣō bhavati na punaḥ kāryam । anyathā hi arthavādapadānāmapi
kartavyatābhidhānataiva syāt । tasmādahīnasyēti kratvantarārthataiva
nyāyyā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b802"/>
<p>nanu ca tulyamēvātra śrautatvaṁ ēkatra na hīyata ityahītaḥ anya---
trānhāṁ samūha iti । kimasmākamanayā cintayā । ēkatra śrautō'nyatra
gauṇa iti kr̥tvā cintitam । na cēdatra saṁbhavati udāharaṇāntaraṁ
saṁbhaviṣyati । yadvā rūḍhiṁ manyatē bhāṣyakāraḥ satrēṣvadarśanāt ।
﻿<pb n="b803"/>
vyutpattimātraṁ taddhitavidhiḥ śunaśśēpādiṣu samāsavidhiriva ।
tasyādidamapyupapadyata ēvōdāharaṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 9 ।। dvibahutvayuktaṁ cōdanāttasya ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu caiva pūrvēṇaivādhikaraṇēna gatamidam । na hi pratīyamānānva-
yatyāgō yuktaḥ kāryānurōdhēnēti । satyam---kintu astyatrādhikā-
śaṅkā । yathāśaktiprayōgē nityē karmaṇi yajamānāntarapravēśamapi
manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । pat‍nyabhiprāyaṁ caikaśēṣābhidhānam
tasmādanutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b804"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">na prakr̥tērēkasaṁyōgāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---yajamānāntarapravēśastāvanna saṁbhavati । kutaḥ ?
yajamānasya hi yathā śak‍nuyādityucyatē । tatra yanna saṁbhavati
tasyaiva gauṇārthatā, tyāgō vā, na punaryajamānāntarōpādānēna saṁpat ।
sati caivaṁ na yajamānādvitvaṁ bahutvaṁ vā bhavati prakr̥tau । yadapyuk‍taṁ
pat‍nyabhiprāyā dvayōryajamānayōḥ bahubhya iti cābhidhānōpapattiriti ।
tadapyayuktam । tasmānna pat‍nyabhiprāya iti itarētarayōgō ghaṭatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b805"/>
<p>ādhānē tu lakṣaṇayā, asaṁbhavāt śrautasya yathā ca pat‍nyā
sahētarētarayōgō nāsti yāgē tathā ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । satriṇāmēva
hi saḥ । tasmādatrāpi pūrvavadutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">।। 10 ।। jāghanī caikadēśatvāt ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>kēna punaḥ prasaṅgēnēdamadhikaraṇamāyātam ? anēna prasaṅgēna ।
sthitaṁ tāvat prakaraṇāt vākyaṁ balīyaḥ sannidhānē
﻿<pb n="b806"/>
cāsannidhānē ca kāryasya । atrēdaṁ sandihyatē---kimayaṁ vākyārtha
utāyaṁ iti vākyārtha ēva saṁśayaḥ । kiṁ jāghanyuddēśēna pat‍nīsaṁyājā
vidhīyantē uta viparītamiti । pūrvapakṣī tāvat jāghanyuddēśēna
pat‍nīsaṁyājavidhānaṁ manyatē । kutaḥ ? ēvaṁ śrautō'rthō-
vihitō bhavati । anyathā hi vākyārthavidhānaṁ syāt ।
nanu cāsmin pakṣē vākyārtha ēva vihitō bhavati anyadanya-
smin‍nucyatē । anabhijñō bhavān vacanavyaktīnām । na brūmō
vākyārthasya vidhisaṁbandhō nāsti iti kiṁ tu vidhēyō vākyārthaḥ ।
ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati---na sannikr̥ṣṭatyāgēna viprakr̥ṣṭārthavidhānaṁ yuktamiti ।
ayaṁ cāparō lābhaḥ jāghanyā paśupādānakalpanā na kr̥tā bhavati ।
tasmādatrāpyutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b807"/>
<p>cōdanā vā'pūrvatvāt ।।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---jāghanyēvātra pat‍nīsaṁyājēṣu vidhīyatē ।
kutaḥ ? yāgavidhānē hi pat‍nyarthō vidhātavyō bhavati । nanu cātra
pat‍nīsaṁyājāścōdakēna saṁnihitā ēva । satyam---vidhīyamānatvēna tu
prakaraṇāntarē prayōjanānyatvamiti karmāntarāpattiḥ । nanu cāsannidhānaṁ
tatra karmāntaratvē hētuḥ na vidhīyamānatā, na cānanyārthatvamatra, jāgha-
nīyasaṁbandhārthatvādvākyasya । tasmānnāyaṁ vākyabhēdaparihāra upa-
labhyatē । ucyatē---anabhijñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ śāstra-
bhēdasya । vidhānasannidhirhi vihitavidhānē bhēdamuparuṇaddhi,
﻿<pb n="b808"/>
na padārthamātrasannidhiḥ । uddēśyatvē hi bhavati padārthamātrasannidhirapya-
vagamahētuḥ, padārthamātrasavyapēkṣatvāt uddēśya bhāvasya । tasmāda‍yuktō
vākyabhēdaḥ । yatpunaridaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇōbhayathā saṁbandhividhāna-
mupanyastaṁ tatkimartham ? ucyatē । nāntarīyakasākṣādvidhānavivēka-
pradarśanārtham । pradarśanamidānīṁ kimarthaṁ ? anyatarāprāp‍tyarthaṁ
nēha prakaraṇē ubhayasyāvāptirupapadyatē । tasmāt anyatara-
dvidhēyam । sā ca jāghanyēva, pat‍nīsaṁyājānāṁ prāptatvāttasmādanutkarṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b809"/>
yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ na paśuṁ prayuṅk‍ta iti asmadīyēpi pakṣē laukikyāḥ
prayuk‍tērvidyamānatvāt‍tulyam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="24">।। 11 ।। 1santardanaṁ prakr̥tau krayaṇavadanarthalōpāt syāt ।। 24 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpyutkarṣāśaṅkā dīrghaśacdasyānanvayāt । dhr̥tyā ityartha-
vādānupapattēśca । anutkarṣavādī tu latādairdhyēṇāpyanuvādaṁ manvānaḥ
dīrghasya vā sōmasya iti prakr̥tāvēvaitadvidhānamiti manyatē । rāddhānta-
vādī punaḥ sōmāpēkṣaivātra dīrghatā mantavyā na latāpēkṣēti
ca nātirēkādvinā'rthavādōpapattiḥ iti saṁsthāsvityuktavān ।
nanu cāsminnapi pakṣē prakaraṇādutkarṣa ēva । saṁsthā hi vikārāḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b810"/>
yāgābhiprāyō'yamutkarṣaḥ kāryāpēkṣayā tūtkarṣa ēvētyadōṣaḥ । yatpuna-
ridamuk‍taṁ sīsēna krīṇātītivadvikalpa iti । nanu ca tatra
samuccayō'nayōḥ na vikalpaḥ daśabhirēva krīṇātīti । bidhānavikalpa-
maṅgīkr̥tyaitannidarśanam, na prayōgavikalpam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 12 ।। 1saṅkhyāyuk‍taṁ kratōḥ prakaraṇāt syāt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>vākyārthasamavāyāpēkṣiṇī prakaraṇādutkarṣacintā gatā, idānī-
mabhidhānavipratipattirvākya ēva cintyatē---kimayaṁ prathama-
śabdō jyōtiṣṭōma ēva vartatē uta jyōtiṣṭōmaprayōga iti ।
﻿<pb n="b811"/>
<q>‘ēṣa vāva prathamō yajñō yajñānāṁ’</q> iti śravaṇāddhi spaṣṭaiva yajñavacanatā
gamyatē <q>“1ēvaṁ ca prakaraṇamanugrahīṣyatē”</q> iti pratiṣēdhavidhyabhiprāyaṁ
tat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="33">2naimittikaṁ vā kartr̥saṁyōgāt liṅgasya tannimittatvāt ।। 33 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---satyamasmāt prayōgāt avagamyatē kintu
ya ētēnāniṣ‍ṭvā'thānyēna yajētēti prayōgādapi prāthamyamavagamyatē
﻿<pb n="b812"/>
nāniṣ‍ṭvā'thānyēna yajētēti । kathaṁ ? kartr̥saṁbandhitayā śrūya-
māṇatvāt । kartuśca prayōgēṇa saṁbandhō na prayōjyēna । prayōgaparē
ca vākyē ēṣa vāva prathamō yajñō yajñānāṁ yajjyōtiṣṭōma iti śrutiḥ
na punaḥ prayōjyaniṣṭhā । kvacidasya prayōgō'vagamyatē jyōtiṣṭōma-
śabdasyaiva । ataḥ prayōga ēvāyaṁ iti na prathamē prayōgē pravr̥ñj‍yā-
dityarthaḥ । yajñaśabdaśca prayōjyaviṣayatvāt prayōgē'pyupapadyata ēva ।
﻿<pb n="b813"/>
prathamaprayōjyō yajñānāmityarthaḥ । ēvaṁ ca prakaraṇa ēva pravargya-
vidhirupapannō bhavati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 12 ।। 1pauṣṇaṁ pēṣaṇaṁ vikr̥tau pratīyētācōdanātprakr̥tau ।। 34 ।।</ab>
<p>pauṣṇaṁ pēṣaṇaṁ uttaravivakṣayētyuk‍tam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="35">।। 13 ।। 2tatsarvārthamaviśēṣāt ।। 35 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē kiṁ yāvatpauṣṇaṁ tatsarvaṁ prapiṣṭaṁ kartavyaṁ uta
carurēvēti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī viśēṣāgrahaṇāt sarvārthamiti manyatē ।
nanu ca purōḍāśē prāptatvāt na śakyatē vidhātuṁ; na, pauṣṇatayā aprāptēḥ
﻿<pb n="b814"/>
tasmāt sarvārtham । nanu hr̥dayādyākr̥tivināśaḥ paśau bhavatu,
vacanāt । kimiva vacanaṁ na kuryāt । atrōcyatē---purōḍāśē
tāvat prāptatvānna vidhiḥ । nanu pauṣṇatayā'prāptirityuktam । kāryata
ēva prāptiriṣyatē na saṁbandhitayā anyathā hyarthavādapadānāmapi
kāryārthataiva syādityuktam । nanu caivaṁ sati prakaraṇādvākyaṁ durbala-
mityuktam । kāryē satyanvayakalpanā atō balavattā uktā vākyasya ।
﻿<pb n="b815"/>
tasmānna vidhānaṁ purōḍāśē saṁbhavati । paśau tarhi saṁbhavati । na
hi । tarhi sāpēkṣatvaprasaṅgāt śāstrasya । na ca nirapēkṣē saṁbhavati
sāpēkṣāśrayaṇaṁ yuktamityuktaṁ śabdavidbhiḥ । tasmāt carāvēva pēṣaṇaṁ
śabdāt pratīmaḥ । yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ 1yadyapītyēvamādinā bhāṣya-
kārēṇa ēvamapi sāpēkṣatvaṁ naiva parihartuṁ śakyata ityabhiprāyaḥ ।
anvārōhamātraṁ caitata । pūrvamēva hyuktō hētuḥ । nanu ca carāvapi
carutaiva hīyēta viśadasiddhaudanē prayōgadarśanāt । na, piṣṭakacarāvapi
pak‍tisāmānyāt ityabhihitaḥ caruśabdaprayōga iti carāvēva
pēṣaṇamiti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b816"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 15 ।। 1ēkasminnēkasaṁyōgāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>atra bhāṣyakārēṇa indrapītāgnēyaśabdābhyāṁ viśēṣō darśitaḥ
pūṣā prapiṣṭabhāgō bhavatīti । tathā adantakō hīti hētuvacanaṁ sōmā-
pauṣṇē nēmapiṣṭaścaruriti । sōmāpauṣṇē nēmapiṣṭa ityanuvādō yuktaḥ ।
nēmapiṣṭavidhānē hi pauṣṇōpalakṣaṇāt carurityavivakṣitaṁ syādityēva-
mādyadhikāśaṅkānirākaraṇārthamidamadhikaraṇam । atrōcyatē---katha-
māsāmāśaṅkānāṁ nirākaraṇaṁ ? kāryaprayuktatvāddharmāṇāmityuk‍tō
hētuḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ kāryēṇa saṁbandhō dēvatāpadayuktānāṁ bhavatīti
﻿<pb n="b817"/>
niṣprayōjanatvāddēvatāyāḥ kāryārthatvācca yāgasyēti lakṣaṇōpapadyatē ।
dēvatā cēdupalakṣaṇaṁ na dvidēvatākēṣūpalakṣayituṁ kṣamaḥ । adēvatā hi
sā tatra । adantakatvādīnāṁ tu hētuvannigadatvēnārthavādatvamuktam ।
arthavādāśca guṇavādēna vyākhyēyāḥ । nēmapiṣṭaśabdasya nyāyā-
pētatvāt dvidēvatākēṣu viśiṣṭavidhānaṁ bhaviṣyati । tasmādēka-
dēvatākēṣu pēṣaṇamiti siddham ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b818"/>
<head>tr̥tīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1nivītamiti manuṣyadharmaḥ śabdasya tatpradhānatvāt 3-4-1 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaḥ vidhinā tvēkavākyatvāditi sthitē'rthavādatvē puna-
rvidhānāśaṅkā । ēkavākyatvē hi na vidhidvayamavakalpata iti na nivī-
tatvādividhisaṁbhavaḥ । pākṣikīṁ prāptiṁ manvānō vidhiṁ manyata iti cēt ।
tadapyayuktam । tasyāpi vacanāntarēṇa prāptatvāt upapadyata ēvārtha-
vādaḥ । ucyatē---prakaraṇāṅgatayā'prāptiṁ manvānēnēdamadhikaraṇaṁ cinti-
tam । vidhānēpi prakaraṇāṅgatā na saṁbhavatīti sthitamarthavādatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b819"/>
nanu cātithyādāvaprāptirvidyata iti yuk‍tam । na । tadanvayāna-
vagamāt । manuṣyamātrasaṁbandhitāyāṁ tu prāyādibhirupapannatvāt
arthavādataivēti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 2 ।। 1digvibhāgaśca tadvatsambandhasyārthahētutvāt ।। 3-4-10 ।।</ab>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">।। 3 ।। paruṣiditadhr̥tapūrṇavidagdhaṁ ca tadvat ।। 3-4-11 ।।</ab>
<p>tadvadityayamatidēśaḥ kimabhyadhikaṁ paśyataḥ ? anyathā
hyupavītē prāptiḥ, anyathā dikṣu, anyathā paruṣi dinādiṣviti
viśēṣapradarśanārthō'yamatidēśaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b820"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 4 ।। 1akarmakratusaṁyuktaṁ saṁyōgānnityānuvādaḥ syāt ।। 3-4-12 ।।</ab>
<p>uk‍taṁ nivītādhikaraṇēna kratudharmatayā nivītādi pratīyatē manu-
ṣyaśravaṇāditi । prāyēṇa ca prāptatvādanuvāda iti । atrāpīdānīṁ
tadvadēvānuvādaṁ manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nanu ca tatra manuṣyaśabda-
śravaṇādyuk‍tō'nuvādaḥ prāyikīṁ ca prāptimāśritya arthavādaḥ । ucyatē ।
atrāpi pūrvaprāptapratiṣēdhāt gamyata ēva pumān yasyāsau pratiṣēdhaḥ ।
pratiṣēdhaśās‍trē hi sarvatra pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturēvādhikāraḥ
﻿<pb n="b821"/>
ataḥ pūrvaprāptasyaivāyamanuvādaḥ । vidyatē ca prāptiḥ arthataḥ ।
prāptimātratayā ca pratiṣēdhōpapattēḥ na prakaraṇārthatā । nanu cāyamanu-
vādaḥ kasya vidhēḥ śēṣaḥ ? na kasyacidapīti brūmaḥ । prāp‍tiranuvādatvē
hētuḥ nārthavādatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b822"/>
<p>ēkavākyatvēna hi arthavādō bhavati na prāp‍timapēkṣatē
yathā jārtilayavāgvā juhuyāditi । tasmānnānuvādaḥ । nanu cēdaṁ
śrutivākyaṁ tasyāḥ smr̥tērmūlaṁ bhaviṣyati । na bhavitu-
marhati । atra hi śrūyamāṇasya prakaraṇārthatā'vasīyatē na puruṣārthatā
anuvādapakṣē punaḥ puruṣārthatayaiva prāp‍tēḥ siddhā puruṣārthatā । nanu ca
﻿<pb n="b823"/>
kratvarthatayāvagamyamānasya kathaṁ puruṣārthatayā'nuvādō yuktaḥ kalpa-
yitum । ucyatē---kraturapi hi puruṣārtha ēva । atastatsaṁbandhi-
tayāpi puruṣasyēcchātaḥ prāpnōtyēvānr̥tavadanamiti na dōṣaḥ tatsaṁbandhā-
vagatēḥ । upanayōttarakālabhāvitvācca kratūnāṁ siddhō'nuvādaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">1vidhirvā saṁyōgāntarāt ।। 3-4-13 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । āyuṣmataivōk‍taṁ na smr̥tivākyasyēdaṁ mūlatāṁ
pratipadyata iti । ēvaṁ cēt tvayaivēdaṁ saṁyōgāntaramabhyupagataṁ saṁyōgā-
﻿<pb n="b824"/>
ntaratvē ca nānuvādaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । nanu ca pratiṣēdhē
pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturēvādhikāra ityuktam । satyamuktam । na tu
tat prakaraṇē śakyatē vak‍tum । kimiti ? padārthamātra ēva
pratiṣēdhōpapattēḥ laukikēṣu punaḥ puruṣēcchāta ēva pravr̥ttirviṣayatāṁ
pratipadyatē pratiṣēdhasyēti tatkriyākarturēvādhikārō yuktaḥ । iha
punaḥ kratvarthatayaiva pravr̥ttirgamyatē padārthasyēti na tasya karturadhikāraḥ
śakyatē vak‍tum । nanu ca kartaivākhyātēṣu pradhānatayāvagamyatē ।</p>
<pb n="b825"/>
niyōgābhēdāt‍tu prayājādīnāmaṅgatvabhavagamyatē । savēṣāmēkaphalānu-
bandhatvāt । saṁskārakarmaṇāmapi kratvarthasya saṁskāryatayā'vagatēḥ
yuk‍taivāṅgatā । pratiṣēdhē punaḥ pratiṣēdhyasya akratvarthatvāt
ākhyātēna ca kartrabhidhānāt karturēva pratīyatē । na ca tatsaṁbandhā-
vagatirviruddhā । kratōrapi puruṣārthatvāt upanayanōttarakālabhāvi-
tvācca tadarthapratipattēḥ siddhō'nuvāda ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b826"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---syādētadēvaṁ yadyākhyātānāṁ kartā'bhidhēyaḥ syāt,
na punarākhyātānāṁ kartrabhidhānaśaktiḥ śakyatē kalpayitum ।
kriyābhidhānādēva sarvakārakāvagatēḥ । kathaṁ tarhi bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ
sūtraṁ laḥ karmaṇi ca bhāvē cākarmakabhyaḥ cakārāt kartari cēti । saṅkhyā-
vidhānārthamētaditi pradarśitam । saṅkhyāviśēṣavidhānāśrayaṁ ca yak
śabiti ca । anyakārakasaṅkhyābhidhānamidānīṁ kimiti na bhavati ?
tulyē'vagamyamānatvē । na lōkaḥ paryanuyōk‍tuṁ śakyatē । durjayō
hi mahājanaḥ; laukikaprayōgamūlaṁ cēdaṁ śāstraṁ bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ
﻿<pb n="b827"/>
prayuktasya hi niyamamācaṣṭē । nāprayuktasyābhidhānam । tasmāda-
paryanuyōgō'yam । ataḥ kratvarthapadārthamātrapravr̥ttyāśrayamēvēdaṁ pratiṣēdha-
śāstram । nanu ca pratiṣēdhyagatā pravr̥ttiḥ na kratvarthatyuktam । acō-
ditatvāt । naiva tādarthyēna cōditatvaṁ saṁbandhahētuḥ upakārakatayāpi
saṁbandhitōpapadyata ēva । saṁbandhini ca vidhiḥ kratvarthō bhavatītyuktaṁ
payō brataṁ brāhmaṇasyētyēvamādiṣu । nanu cōpakārakaviṣayatayā
pratiṣēdhasya kratvarthapuruṣārthayōrna kaścidviśēṣaḥ । yathāsti viśēṣa-
stathōktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b828"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 5 ।। 1ahīnavatpuruṣadharmastadarthatvāt ।।3-4-14 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaḥ nivītaṁ manuṣyāṇāmityanēna viśēṣaḥ jañjabhyamānasya ?
ayamasti viśēṣaḥ nārthavādāt parihāraḥ saṁbhavati । avākya-
śēṣatvāt । nāpyanuvādō nānr̥taṁ vadēditivat । nāpyatrārthaprāptasya
viṣayatvasaṁbhavō nānr̥taṁ vadēditivat । na hi jañjabhyamānatāṁ
kadācidapi prāp‍nōti anr̥tavadanavat । tasmājjañjabhyamāna-
mātrasya mantravidhānamidaṁ na prakaraṇē'vasthāpayituṁ śakyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b829"/>
nanu caivaṁ sati phalakalpanā syāt । bhavatu vacanāt, kō dōṣaḥ ?
atō vākyāt prakaraṇabādhaḥ siddhō yathā dvādaśāhīna-
syēti । atrābhidhīyatē---na phalakalpanāmarhatyētadvacanam । kutaḥ ?
vākyaṁ hi padārthasaṁbandhamātrē prabhavati na kāryē । kāryaṁ hi
niyōgasamadhigamyamēva prakr̥taścāyaṁ dārśapaurṇamāsikō niyōgaḥ ।
sarvamēvēdaṁ viniyōgakāraṇam । na ca kāryāntarakalpanā
﻿<pb n="b830"/>
klr̥ptē sati saṁbhavati iti prakaraṇa ēva nivēśaḥ । nanu ca jañjabhya-
mānatā na kratvarthatayā'nr̥tavadanavat saṁbhavati । mābhūt jañjabhya-
mānatā kratvarthā । kartustu kratvarthatā prakaraṇasaṁbandhē hēturbhaviṣyati ।
tasmāt kratōḥ kartuḥ dharmō'yamiti siddham । ahīnē punaḥ
kāryatvād‍yuktaḥ utkarṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 6 ।। 1śaṁyau ca sarvaparīdānāt ।। 3-4-17 ।।</ab>
<p>śaṁyau punaḥ śatēna yātayāditi phalaśrutēḥ na prakaraṇa-
kalpanā nyāyyā । svavākyasthā hi kāryāvagatiḥ balīyasī
﻿<pb n="b831"/>
tasmāt puruṣamātradharmau'yaṁ na brāhmaṇāyāvagurēditivat । nanu
jañjabhyamānēpi <q>‘prāṇāpānāvēvātman dhatta’</q> iti phalaśravaṇabhastyēva ।
na । dhatta iti vartamānōpadēśāt na sādhyatayāvagamyatē । iha punaḥ
yātayāta iti bhaviṣyadarthatāṁ liṅavagamayatīti viśēṣaḥ ।
tasmānmūlasmr̥tēḥ prāptasyānuvāda iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b832"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 7 ।। prāgaparōdhānmalavadvāsasaḥ1 ।। 3-4-18 ।।</ab>
<p>malavadvāsasā saha saṁvādapratiṣēdhē sandēhaḥ kiṁ kratvarthaḥ saṁvādaḥ
uta puruṣārtha iti । kiṁ prāptaṁ ? nānr̥taṁ vadēditivat kratau saṁbhavāt
kratvartha iti prāptē । ucyatē---na prāptatvāt । kratvarthatayā hi
<q>“tāmaparudhya yajēta”</q> । iti prāpta ēvāyamasaṁvādaḥ। tasmāt
puruṣārthaḥ vākyaṁ ca prakaraṇādvalīya ityuktamēva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b833"/>
<p>nanu puruṣārthatayāpi prāpta ēvāyamasaṁvādaḥ <q>“nākalyāṁ
nārīmabhiramayēnna rajasvalāṁ”</q> iti । asyāḥ smr̥tēridamēva mūlaṁ
bhaviṣyatīti । anuvādō vā sarvathā tāvat kratvarthatā
nāsti । nanu ca saṁvādamātrapratiṣēdhō'yam । ucyatē--<q>‘nāsyā
annamadyāt abhyañjanaṁ vāva striyā annaṁ”</q> ityupagamanapratiṣēdha
ēvāyamiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b834"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 8 ।। aprakaraṇē tu taddharmastatō viśēṣāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘hiraṇyaṁ bhāryaṁ’</q> ityanārabhyavādāt puruṣārthō'yam । na hyatra
kratussannihitō'vagamyatē । tasmātpuruṣārthaḥ । nanu ca prayōjanavataḥ
saṁskārō, na niṣprayōjanasya saṁskāryatā yuktā dvitīyānirdēśācca
hiraṇyasaṁskāra ēvāyaṁ yuktaḥ saṁskr̥taṁ kratōrupakariṣyatīti ।
atrābhidhīyatē---syādētadēvaṁ yadi saṁskr̥tasya hiraṇyasya karmārthatā
upapadyatē---na tāvat prakr̥taṁ karmāsti । na cēha karmacōdanā, dravya-
dēvatāsaṁyōgābhāvāt । tasmāt dravyasaṁskārānarthakyāt puruṣa-
dharmē'yam । nanu cātra phalaṁ kalpayitavyam ? niyōgānāṁ
kāryārthatvāt prakr̥tasya kāryāsyāvidyamānatvāt na dōṣaḥ kalpanāyām ।
﻿<pb n="b835"/>
tasmāddhiraṇyadhāraṇaṁ karturdharmaścōdyata iti sthitam । yadi kartr̥-
saṁskāratvēna phalaṁ kalpyatē kimiti dravyasaṁskāratayā kratūpakārō na
kalpyatē । ayamasti viśēṣaḥ ēkavākyāvagatēna hyarthavādēna
kartr̥sambandhē phalakalpanā upapadyatē na punaraprakr̥tēna kratunā artha-
viprakarṣāt । ayaṁ cāparō viśēṣaḥ sarvatra draṣṭavyaḥ kartr̥sambandhē
hyadhikārasiddhiḥ adhikr̥tasya ca phalakalpanā nyāyyā । na punaḥ
dravyasambandhē prayōjanakalpanēti sak‍tuṣu darśitam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b836"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 9 ।। śēṣō'prakaraṇē'viśēṣāt sarvakarmaṇāt ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>yēna karmaṇērtsēt iti aviśēṣāt sarvakarmārthatēti pūrvapakṣavādī
manyatē । nanu cānāhitāg‍nērāhavanīyābhāvāt nāyaṁ hōmaḥ
saṁbhavati anāhavanīya ēvāyaṁ bhaviṣyati pradhānānurōdhāt । na
guṇānurōdhēna pradhānasyāṅtyāgō yuktaḥ । guṇa ēva hi tattyāgaḥ
﻿<pb n="b837"/>
pradhānānurōdhēnētyaṅgavidō manyantē । satyamēvaitat । kintvatra ayaṁ
nyāyō na saṁbhavati । kasmāt ? vaidikē tāvadāhavanīyabādhō
nōpapadyatē । na ca laukikasyaivāṅgamiti śakyatē vak‍tuṁ tvayaivōktama-
viśēṣāditi । atō bhāvābhāvayōrvirōdhāt bhāvata ēva viśēṣā-
vadhāraṇaṁ yuktam na punaḥ abhāvataḥ । anavagamē hētuḥ asau । na punaḥ
viśēṣāvagamē hētuḥ । tasmādvaidika ēva jayāhōma iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 10 ।। dōṣāttviṣṭirlaukikē syāt śāsrāddhi vaidikē na dōṣaḥ syāt1 ।। 34 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b838"/>
<p>pauṇḍarīkē śrūyatē---yāvatō'śvān pratigr̥hṇīyāt iti । kiṁ
laukikē'śvapratigrahē iyamiṣṭiḥ uta vaidika iti saṁśayaḥ । laukikē
dōśadarśanāt śūdrādanyasmādvā pāpakarmaṇaḥ kr̥tē dōṣō bhavatīti ।
<q>“1na dōṣasaṅkīrtanaṁ prāyaścittaviṣayaviśēṣaṇam । kintu prāyaścittastu-
tyarthēna”</q> iti । kimidaṁ prāyaścittaviṣayaviśēṣaṇaṁ kiṁ vā stutyarthēnēti़
idamidam । asyārthasyāpanuttayē yadā prāyaścittaṁ tadā viṣaya-
viśēṣaṇam । yadā tu kāryāntarārthaṁ tadā stutyarthēna dōṣa-
nirghātārthaṁ cēdam । tasmāt laukikē bhavitumarhati । <q>“2nanu
vaidikēpi apratigrāhyāt pratigr̥hṇatō dōṣō'styēva । ucyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b839"/>
bhavēdētadēnaṁ yadi pratigrahasya karturiṣṭirbhavēt । sā khalu
yathā hētukartuḥ tathā uttarē'dhikaraṇē vakṣyāmaḥ”</q> । asambandha-
midaṁ bhāṣyam । yadi laukikē pratigrahīturiṣṭiḥ na bhavati tataśca
vaidikē'pi aśvaṁ apratigrāhyāt pratigr̥hṇatō dōṣō'stīti satyapi
dōṣanirghātārthē prāyaścittē kasmāllaukika ēva pratigrahītuḥ prāyaścittā-
śaṅkā । atha upakramāvagatārthavādadarśanāt dāturiṣṭirityucyatē
laukikē'pi tulyam । atha laukikē pratigrahapakṣēpi dāturēvētyabhiprāyaḥ
śūdrādanyasmādvā pāpakarmaṇaḥ iti bhāṣyaṁ asambaddham । kathaṁ vōparitanē-
'dhikaraṇē pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । vēdō vā prāyadarśanādityupakramēṇōpasaṁhārāva-
dhr̥ttēḥ । atrābhidhīyatē-nēdamasaṁbaddham । ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b840"/>
laukikē'śvapratigrahē dōṣaśravaṇaṁ viṣayaviśēṣaṇatayaivōpapattēḥ । yasmā-
dasmin pakṣē pratigrahīturēvēṣṭiḥ । dāturyadīyamiṣṭiḥ syāt tatō
dānasyāṅgaṁ vā kalpayitavyaṁ phalāntaraṁ vā । dānāṅgatā tāvanna saṁbhavati
nimittatvēnāsyōpakṣayāddānasya । atha viparivr̥ttyā punaraṅgitvaṁ
dānasya tadā idamēvāyuktam । guṇavādēnāpyarthavādōpapattēḥ । pāpa-
pramōcanasya phalatayā vā vākyēnāvagatēḥ । na ca dātuḥ pāpaṁ
śakyatē kalpayitumiti । tasmālaukikē pakṣē pratigrahīturēvēṣṭiḥ
﻿<pb n="b841"/>
cōditatvāllōkē vēdē ca dānasya । rāddhāntavādī tu yathāśrutasya
pāpasyāśvapratigrahō na nidānatayā pramāṇāntarēṇa prasiddhaḥ । nāpi
vacanāt । vākyabhēdaprasaṅgāt । tasmāt pāpamātravacanamidaṁ
vaidikēpyupapadyata ēva, rakṣaṇapōṣaṇādinā duḥ khadarśanāt । phalaṁ
ca na kalpayitavyaṁ bhavati karmāṅgatayōpapattēḥ । prakaraṇaviniyōjyatayā
karturvā bhavatu pratigrahīturvā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b842"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 11 ।। acōditaṁ ca karmabhēdāta1 ।। 30।।</ab>
<p>yuktaṁ tāvat yadā kartuḥ tadā karmāṅgaṁ; yadā pratigrahītuḥ tadā
kathaṁ ? upakramōpasaṁhāravaśāt pratigrāhayēditivat vipariṇāmāt
kalpyatām । r̥tvijō yājanīyāḥ upavāsavat ।</p>
<p>yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ---kathaṁ punaḥ vēdō vā prāyadarśanāditi
sthitē'dhikaraṇē uparitanē'dhikaraṇē pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । dōṣapradarśanādēvēti
manyatē । arthavādabhūtō'pi dōṣaḥ pratigrahīturēvāñjasyēnōpapadyatē ।
upakramō'pi laukikapakṣavata dāturapi tāvat aśvapratigrahē dōṣaḥ
kiṁ punaḥ pratigrahīturiti vyākhyāyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu avaśyaṁ
﻿<pb n="b843"/>
tāvat nirvāpayēditi vipariṇāmaḥ kalpyaḥ । tasmādvaramupakrama-
darśanāt pratigrāhayēdityēvaṁ manyatē । atō nēdaṁ punaruktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 12 ।। pānavyāpacca tadvat1 ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>tadvadityātidēśikō'pi viśēṣaḥ । ayaṁ viśēṣaḥ dōṣadarśanam ।
nanu ca pūrvasminnadhikaraṇē dōṣadarśanādēva laukika ityuktam ।
satyamanupapattistatrōktā dōṣasya । iha tu glānirvamanādupapadyata
ēvēndriyāṇāmityadhikāśaṅkā । ata ēva vamanārthaṁ taditi parihr̥tam ।
﻿<pb n="b844"/>
glānyarthamēva yat na tasya glānirdōṣatvēna śakyatē kalpayitumiti ।
tasmāt pūrvavadēvēdaṁ karmaphalakalpanābhayāt cōditasōmapānavamana-
nimittakamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 13।। tatsarvatrāviśēṣāt1 ।। 34 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṁ yāvantassōmavāminaḥ tāvatāṁ vamanē ētatprāyaścittaṁ uta
svāmina ēvēti । aviśēṣāt sarvārthamiti prāptē । ucyatē
---svāmina ēvēdaṁ prāyaścittam । kutaḥ ? na yajamānasya r̥tvijāṁ
caikā cōdanā saṁbhavati । ēkatra yajētēti cōdanā anyatra yājayēditi
﻿<pb n="b845"/>
na caikasmin vākyē ubhayamētat bhavati । kasmāt ? avipariṇatā ēṣā
cōdanā । sā ca svābhivamana ēvāvagamyatē । tasmāt phalavatsanni-
dhāvaphalaṁ tadaṅgamiti bhavati tadidamuktam । nānyadīyō yāgō'nyasyō-
pakarōtīti । tasmānna r̥tvigvamananimittamiti । na hyanyasya
cōditamanyasyōpakārōtītyarthaḥ । ataḥ svāmivamananimittamēvēti
siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 14 ।। 1sarvapradānaṁ haviṣastadarthatvāt ।। 3-4-37 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b846"/>
<p>ihēdānīṁ sandihyatē । <q>‘āg‍nēyō'ṣṭākapāla’</q> iti kiṁ kr̥ts‍nasya
haviṣastyāgaḥ uta dvirhaviṣō'vadyatīti tāvanmātrasyaiva tyāga iti ।
nanu cātra sandēha ēva nōpapadyatē āg‍nēyō'ṣṭākapāla iti pari-
samāptā cōdanā । dvirhaviṣō'vadyatīti saṁskāracōdanā haviṣaḥ
agnēstr̥ṇānyapacinōtītivat । nanu ca juhōtītyapi śrūyatē
haviṣō'panītasya pratipattirbhaviṣyati । yathā yāgōttarakālaṁ
sviṣṭakr̥dādayaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---naitadēvam । juhōtiḥ yāgāśca
saṁbandhidravyasādhyāḥ । sakalasya ca parityāgē hōmō
yāgāśca sviṣṭakr̥dādayaḥ nōpapadyantē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b847"/>
<p>aṣṭākapālaviṣayāścōdanāḥ । ata upapadyatē saṁśayaḥ ।
asmiṁśca saṁśayē kasya pakṣasyādhyavasānaṁ yuk‍taṁ ? pūrvapakṣavādī
tāvanmanyatē---apratipakṣatvādāgrēyacōdanāyāḥ tatsavyapēkṣatvāccōtta-
rāsāṁ pūrvaiva balīyasīti । tadidamuktam । <q>“sarvapradānaṁ haviṣasta-
darthatvāt”</q>। kathaṁ tarhi caturavattaṁ juhōtīti sviṣṭakr̥tē sama-
vadyatīti । gauṇō vā yajyarthō juhōtyarthaśca grahītavyaḥ, taddharmakaṁ vā
dravyāntaramutpādyam । dvirhaviṣō'vadyati havirdharmakādavadyatītyarthaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">kr̥tatvāt‍tu karmaṇaḥ sakr̥tsyāt dravyasya guṇabhūtatvāt।। 3-4-40।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---satyamēvaṁ yathā bhavānāha। yadi
āgnēyō'ṣṭākapāla iti tyāgaparyantastaddhitaḥ syāt।
﻿<pb n="b848"/>
sāsya dēvatēti saṁbandhimātratayā'vagatēḥ ēkadēśatyāgādapyupapadyata
ēva saṁbandhitā । tadidamuktam---<q>“akr̥ts‍nasaṁbandhēpi taddhitasaṁbandha-
syōpapattiḥ darśitastatō grahītavyamiti saṁbandhaḥ"</q>। sati caivamāgnēya-
cōdanāyāmupapannāyāṁ na caturavattaṁ juhōti sviṣṭakr̥tē samavadyati iti
gauṇī vr̥ttiḥ śakyatē kalpayitum । havirdharmakasya vā dravya-
syōtpādaḥ । tathā caturavattēnaiva kr̥taḥ śāstrārthaḥ āg‍nēyō'ṣṭāka-
pāla iti sviṣṭakr̥dādidarśanaṁ cōpapannam । yatpunaridamāśaṅkitaṁ
dva‍yavadānasya saṁskāratvānna sarvaparityāgē virōdha iti tadidamāśaṅkā-
mātramēva haviṣō yāgārthatvādityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b849"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 15 ।। aprayōjakatvādēkasmātkriṁyēran śēṣasya guṇabhūtatvāt ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>iha śēṣakarmāṇyudāharaṇaṁ---kiṁ sakr̥t kr̥tvōparantavyam uta
yāvacchēṣamāvr̥ttiḥ iti । pūrvapakṣavādī kr̥tatvācchāstrārthasya sakr̥-
tkaraṇaṁ manyatē । nanu pratipradhānaṁ guṇā āvartanta iti śēṣasyā-
prādhānyādāvr̥ttikēvātrāvagamyatē । ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ
---pradhānōpakārāya hi śēṣasya saṁskāraḥ, sakr̥t kr̥tēna ca kr̥taṁ kāryamiti
nāvr̥t‍tiṁ manyatē । na hi śēṣatvāt saṁskāryatvam । nanu ca
grahādāvapyēvamēva prāpnōti । prāpnōtyēva yadyatra na samādhīyatē । tatra
tarhi kā cintā ? ēkatvasyāvivakṣētyuktam । atrābhidhīyatē
---yāvacchēṣamāvr̥t‍tiḥ । nanu ca kr̥tatvācchāstrārthasya sakr̥t ityuktam
﻿<pb n="b850"/>
ucyatē । śēṣasaṁskāradvāraṁ hi pradhānasyōpakāryatvamuktam । na ca
śēṣē viśēṣō'vagamyatē । ayamayaṁ ayaṁ vēti । atō'guhyamāṇa-
viśēṣāt, pratipradhānamāvr̥t‍tiḥ liṅgāni darśitāni ca bhāṣyē ।
yatpunaraprayōjakatvāt śēṣāṇāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tadēvēdaṁ na śēṣatvāt
saṁskāryatvamiti yaduk‍taṁ, na punarguṇabhāvaṁ śēṣasya manyatē । na hi
śēṣasya prayōjakatvamaprayōjakatvaṁ cōpapadyatē । tasmāt sa ēva pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="46">।। 16 ।। ēkasmāccēdyārthākāmyamaviśēṣāt ।। 46।।</ab>
<p>pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣē anuṣṭhānacintēyam । atrāviśēṣādyataḥ
kutaściṁditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b851"/>
<p>mukhya ēva nimit‍tē saṁbhavati na naimit‍tikōpaghātaḥ śakyatē
kartumiti rāddhāntaḥ । jaghanyānāṁ tu kr̥tatvāt naimit‍tikasya
(nimittāvagatiḥ) yuk‍taivākriyā śēṣakāryāṇām । iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="48">।। 17 ।। bhakṣāśravaṇāddānaśabdaḥ parikrayē ।। 48 ।।</ab>
<p>idaṁ brahmaṇa iti dvyavadānōpasaṁhārādyāgasya śēṣēṇa parikrayaṁ
manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu tasyāvadēyayōgyatayaivōtpat‍tēḥ
yāgārthataivēti nārthāntarē viniyōgamarhatīti । kathaṁ tarhi
sviṣṭakr̥dādiyāgaḥ ? atyaktatvācchēṣasya vacanāccōpapadyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b852"/>
nanu ca dānamapi vacanādbhaviṣyati । satyam---yadi vacanamasti ।
ta tvatra dānaṁ śrūyatē tādarthyaśrutistūpakārādapyupapadyata ēvētyupa-
kārō darśitaḥ । śēṣabhāvastu viparīta ēvētyanavada‍yam ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyasyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b853"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tr̥tīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। ājyācca sarvasaṁyōgāta1 ।। 3-5-1 ।।</ab>
<p>yāvaddhaviḥ kiñciccōditaṁ sarvasmācchēṣādavadyatīti sthitam ।
upāṁśuyājē saṁśayaḥ---kiṁ dhruvāsthādaviśēṣādaṅgapradhānasādhāraṇādana-
vadēyaṁ sviṣṭakr̥tē utāṅgapradhānaśēṣamapi pradhānaśēṣamityavadēyaṁ gr̥hītā-
dvā jauhavāt camasavat । aviśēṣādavadēyamiti prāptē । na sādhāraṇē,
śēṣatvābhāvāt । śiṣṭamapi hi tatsādhāraṇamēva । pradhānaśēṣācca
sviṣṭakr̥davadānam । na ca tatkēvalapradhānaśēṣa iti śakyatē vak‍tuṁ
﻿<pb n="b854"/>
sādhāraṇatvādēva । yat‍tu gr̥hītasyaiva pratipattiścamasavaditi
tadayuk‍taṁ, caturavattaṁ juhōtīti śravaṇāt śēṣayitavyē pramāṇābhāvāt ।
sviṣṭakr̥davadānavacanamēva pramāṇamiti cēnna । aprayuk‍tē śēṣē'rtha-
vatvāt । yat‍tu camasavadityuk‍taṁ, tanna । anuvaṣaṭkāraśrutērananya-
viṣayatvāt (na sviṣṭakr̥davadānam । na ca tatpradhānaśēṣa iti
śakyatēṁ vak‍tum) camasasya grahaṇamātraśrutēḥ । darśanaṁ pratyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 2 ।। sākaṁ prasthāyyē sviṣṭakr̥diḍaṁ ca tadvat1 ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kēna viśēṣēṇāyamatidēśaḥ ? prakr̥tivaditi
prāptēḥ kāryārthatayā śēṣaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī ।
﻿<pb n="b855"/>
vacanāt kāryaṁ balavaditi rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 3 ।। sautrāmaṇyāṁ ca grahēṣu1 ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>sautrāmaṇyāṁ <q>‘ucchinaṣṭi na sarvahutaṁ juhōti’</q> iti punarapi
śēṣāśaṅkāyāṁ sviṣṭakr̥di़ḍaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । tasyānyatra
viniyōgāditi rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 4 ।। 2dravyaikatvē karmabhēdāt pratikarma kriyēran ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>sarvapr̥ṣṭhē tu pratipradhānaṁ śēṣasaṁskārādāvr̥ttiṁ manyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b856"/>
agr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatayā kr̥taḥ śāstrārtha iti rāddhāntaḥ । nanu
sādhāraṇē naiva sviṣṭakr̥dastītyuktam । satyaṁ, akr̥tatvātkāryāntarāṇāṁ
guṇaprādhānyāccēti viśēṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 35 ।। aindravāyavē tu vacanāt pratikarma bhakṣaḥ syāt1 ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātra pūrvapakṣa ēva nāsti vacanāt ।
na hi pūrvapakṣē vacanasyānyārthatā śakyatē vak‍tum ।
atōcyatē । ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ sōmasaṁskārārtha-
tvādbhakṣasya dviriti prayōgāntarāpēkṣō'nuvādō bhaviṣyati ।
﻿<pb n="b857"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu vacanātkāryakalpanēti vacanādityuktavān ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 6 ।। 1sōmē'vacanādbhakṣō na vidyatē ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>sōmē śēṣabhakṣō'sti nāstīti saṁśayaḥ । nanu saṁśaya
ēvāyamayuktaḥ sōmasya śēṣabhāvāt । yuktaṁ purōḍāśādīnāṁ
dvirhaviṣō'vadyati iti vacanāt tatra yāgōpasaṁhārāt śēṣavattvam
tasya ca bhakṣaḥ । iha tu tadabhāvāt bhakṣaśaṅkaiva nāsti । kathaṁ
tarhi vacanānyētāni <q>‘ dviraindravāyavasya bhakṣayati’</q> <q>‘sarvataḥ parihāramā-
śvinaṁ’</q> <q>‘anuvaṣaṭa‍karōti’</q> iti ca । atrāpi ca bhavānēva praṣṭavyaḥ atha
vā bhavantvarthakarmāṇi । kathaṁ tarhi <q>‘aindravāyavasya’</q> ‘āśvinaṁ iti ca ।
﻿<pb n="b858"/>
taddharmalakṣaṇārthō bhaviṣyati । tasmādanupapannamēvēdaṁ sōmēbhakṣō-
vidyatē uta nēti । athaitēbhyō'pi vacanēbhyaḥ śēṣayitavyaṁ
iti kalpyatē । na, aprayōjakatvācchēṣāṇām । saṁskāryapradhānaṁ hi
saṁskārakarma bhavati । na cāpradhānaṁ prayuṅk‍tē । tasmāt vaktavyō'tra
nyāyaḥ । ucyatēḥ---nātra sarvahōmē pramāṇamasti । aindravāyavādiṣu
hi tādarthyēna grahaṇam । gr̥hītasyaikadēśēnāpi kr̥tē kr̥taivaindravāyavatā,
kimiti sarvasya hōmaḥ । nanu ca sarvasya yāgārthatā śrūyatē <q>‘sōmēna
yajēta’</q> iti । tatrāpi ēkēdēśainaiva sōmēnētyupapannatvāt । tathā
﻿<pb n="b859"/>
ca asya grahaṇaṁ r̥jīṣādēśca tyāgaḥ । yadyēvaṁ kimiti <q>‘dvirhaviṣō-
'vadyati’</q> ityētasmādēvōpasaṁhāraḥ । yathakathaṁcit tatrāpyupasaṁhāra-
siddhēḥ । niyamārthaṁ taditi cēt । sarvapradānaṁ tarhi pūrvapakṣavādinō na
ghaṭatē kiñca ēkadēśēnāpyupapadyata iti naitāvatā sarvaṁ na hōtavyam ।
sarvahōmēnāpyupapadyata ēva । tasmādvaktavyō viśēṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ayamabhidhīyatē---kr̥tē śāstrārthē punaḥ karaṇaṁ tāvanna vidyatē । ēka-
dēśēna kr̥taḥ śāstrārtha iti pradarśitam । kathaṁ tarhi sarvapradānāśaṅkā ?
﻿<pb n="b860"/>
avakhaṇḍyāvakhaṇḍyadātavyamiti vacanārthavagamāt । na yāgārtha-
tvāt dravyasyētyupasaṁhāraḥ । ataḥ ēkadēśēna niyama ēvāyam ।
ata ēva laukikāḥ pāyasādi dēvatōddēśēna kr̥tvā tata uda‍dhr̥tya
kiñcit dēvatōddēśēna tyak‍tvā śēṣaṁ yathēṣṭaṁ viniyuñjatē । tasmā-
dupapadyatē saṁśayaḥ---kiṁ bhakṣaṇēnaiva śēṣapratipattiḥ uta nēti । vacanā-
bhāvāt na bhakṣaṇēnēti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । bhakṣaṇaviśēṣavidhānāt astīti
dvitīyaḥ । anyathā hi viśēṣavidhānaṁ nōpapadyatē । yadi viśēṣavidhānaṁ
nōpapadyatē kāmaṁ mōpapādi, na punarvacanādr̥tē bhakṣaḥ śakyatē pratipat‍tum
yadā bhakṣayati tadā dviriti ēvamēvōpapattēḥ, ēvaṁ tarhi tānyēva
vacanānīti rāddhāntaḥ yāvadvacanaṁ vacanam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b861"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="22">।।7।। 1camasēṣu samākhyānāt saṁyōgasya tannimittatvāt ।। 22 ।।</ab>
<p>camasēṣu idānīṁ vacanābhāvānnāstīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । taccamasa-
taivānyathā nōpapadyatē । ayamasya camasa iti vacanaṁ yathaiva viśēṣa-
vidhānamanyathā nōpapadyata iti pūrvatra । dravyāntaracamanaṁ takṣaṇādi
ca na kalpanāmarhati iti pradarśitaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 8 ।। udgāṁtr̥camasamēkasya śrutisaṁyōgāt2 ।। 8 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b862"/>
<p>prōdgāṁtr̥̄ṇāmityatra kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ na gānaṁ lakṣayati samā-
khyaiva kimiti lakṣayati ? ucchabdasyāvivakṣā prāpnōti gānakāriṣu
lakṣyamāṇēṣu । tathā ca darśitam---anyadēva gānaṁ anyadēvōdgānamiti ।
samākhyānē tu nāyaṁ dōṣaḥ । nanu cōdgānaṁ nāma gānamēva nāsti
﻿<pb n="b863"/>
bhaktirhi sā । sā cōdgīthavācyā । yaḥ punarudgāyēdityēva-
mādiṣu prayōgaḥ udgīthaṁ gāyēditi tatrārthaḥ । ucchabdō hi
tatra bhaktilakṣaṇārthaḥ । gānaṁ tu gānamēva । tasmādudgātētyr̥-
tvigviśēṣanāmaivaitat । na punaḥ udgānasya kartā udgātā । ata
ēva samākhyaivātra lakṣayituṁ prabhavati na gānakriyēti rāddhāntitam ।
ata ēva apasubrahmaṇyavādinō'pi apanyāyavādina ēva । nātra
﻿<pb n="b864"/>
stutyādiśravaṇamiva saṅkōcakapramāṇamasti । nanu prōdgātr̥̄ṇāmiti
triṣvēva bahuvacanōpapattēḥ kimiti samubrahmaṇyānāṁ bhakṣa iti ?
yadi bahuvacanōpapattyarthaṁ satyamēva । atrōdgātr̥śabdaḥ tadarthakāriṣu
vartata ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 9 ।। grāvastutō bhakṣō na vidyatē'nāmnānāt1 ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>uk‍taṁ vacanāt samākhyānācca bhakṣaṇam । idānīṁ vacanārtha-
vipratipattau sampratipattyarthamētānyadhikaraṇānyārabhyantē । sarvē hāri-
yōjanasyāntē lipsinta iti camasināmēvēti pūrvapakṣa-
﻿<pb n="b865"/>
vādinā śaṅkitam । vākyaśēṣāt । asandigdhatvāt prakr̥ta-
vacanatayā sarvaśabdasya nōpaṁsahārō yuktō vākyaśēṣāditi rāddhāntaḥ
pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 10 ।। vaṣa‍ṭakārācca bhakṣayēt1 ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>atra vaṣaṭa‍kartuḥ prathamabhakṣa iti guṇaśravaṇāt na bhakṣa-
vidhānamiti āśaṅkya viśiṣṭavidhānāditi rāddhāntaḥ । nanu
cātra viśiṣṭavidhānaṁ nāsti । na hi prāthamyaṁ nāma bhakṣaṇasya
kārakaṁ yēna yāgaviśiṣṭā kriyā vidhīyēta ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b866"/>
<p>ata ēva pūrvapakṣavādī na viśiṣṭavidhānamatra saṁbhavatītyāśaṅkatavān ।
kathaṁ tarhi rāddhāntaḥ? prathamabhakṣa iti padadvayasya caikārthyābhidhā-
nāt abhihitavidhānāccaikārthyaṁ manyatē । tadayuktam ।
samāsēpi hi tada‍bhūtādhikaraṇanyāyāt apagatirnāsti । satya-
mēvaṁ, tathāpi pūrvōttarapadasaṁbandhāyattā samāsē ca padārthāntarasaṅgatiḥ
﻿<pb n="b867"/>
iti yuktamuk‍taṁ samāsē ca vidadhatō nānēkaguṇavidhānaṁ duṣkara-
mityataḥ siddhamatna viśiṣṭavidhānam।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 11 ।। hāmābhiṣavābhyāṁ ca1।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>abhiṣutya hutvā bhakṣayati ityapi bhakṣavidhānam। hōmābhiṣavayōḥ
prāptatvāt।</p>
﻿<pb n="b868"/>
<p>aṅgatayā ca vidhānānupapattērbhakṣa ēva vidhātavyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="33">।। 12 ।। pratyakṣōpadēśāccamasānāmavyak‍taśśēṣē1 ।। 33 ।।</ab>
<p>hōtr̥camasa ityēvamādyābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ samākhyābhiḥ sakala-
camasasaṁbandhāvagatēḥ abhiṣutya hutvētyanyatra camasēbhyō bhakṣa iti
manyatē । ēvaṁ prāptē ucyatē । abhiṣavahōmanimittō bhakṣaścamasēṣu
bhavatyēva । nanu ca hōtr̥camasa iti sakalacamasāvagatirityuktam ।
satyamuk‍taṁ na punarabhiṣavanimittatāṁ bādhitumarhati । prāpakāṇyētāni
vacanāni na hōtr̥camasa ityasyāṁ saṁbandhāvagatau saṁbandhāntaranivr̥ttiḥ
śakyatē'vagantum । prāptimātrāvagatēḥ । prāptau hi satyāṁ kasyē-
damiti vivakṣāyāṁ anyanivr̥ttiḥ pratīyatē । yathā āgnēya ityuk‍tē
﻿<pb n="b869"/>
naindrāgnasyāvagatiḥ । iha punaḥ prāptiphalatvādvākyasya nānyanivr̥ttiḥ
śakyatē'vagantum । nanu ca prāptāvapi sakalāvagatērvirōdhō vidyata
ēva । satyaṁ yadi samākhyayā prāptiḥ iha punaḥ praituhōtuścamasaḥ iti
vacanāt । kalpyaṁ caitat abhiṣutya hutvētyanēna ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 13 ।। ēkapātrē kramādadhvaryuḥ pūrvō bhakṣayēt1 ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitaṁ camasinō'bhiṣōtārō hōtāraśca bhakṣayanti iti ।
atrēdānīṁ kaḥ prathamaṁ bhakṣayēditi vicāryatē । adhvaryuḥ
bhakṣayati hastagatatvāt yasya hastē sa jayatīti nyāyāt ।
﻿<pb n="b870"/>
nanu vaṣaṭa‍kartuḥ prathamabhakṣa iti । vacanāt kathamadhvaryōrbhakṣaḥ ? bhakṣa-
mātravidhānādapi vaṣaṭa‍karturēva prathamaṁ bhakṣa iti manvānasya
punaridamadhikaraṇam । pradarśitaṁ ca prāthamyādvaṣaṭa‍kārasyēti । vaca-
nāccētyupasaṁhr̥tam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 14 ।। vacanādanujñātabhakṣaṇam1 ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṁ anujñātētaiva bhakṣayitavyaṁ uta ananujñātēnēti prāptidarśa-
nārthamidamadhikaraṇam । asati vacanē'niyamaḥ । vacanāt‍tu niyama
﻿<pb n="b871"/>
ēva । niyamē sati kiṁ laukikēna śabdēnānujñāpanaṁ uta vaidikēnēti ।
mantrānāmnānāt vaidikēnēti niyamaḥ । idamapi mantraprāpti-
darśanārthamēva ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 15 ।। tatrārthāt prativacanam1 ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṁ prativacanē saṁśayaḥ kiṁ mantrēṇa prativacanaṁ uta lauki-
kēna śabdēnēti । kathaṁ punarupahūta iti mantrāmnānāt sandēhaḥ
upahrayasvētyasyaiva śēṣaṁ manvānasya । na hyanujñāpanāt pūrvapaṭhitaṁ
prativacanasamarthamapi prativacanāyālaṁ bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ । rāddhānta-
vādī tu pūrvataivātra bādhyata iti rāddhāntitavān ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b872"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="43">।। 16 ।। tadēkapātrāṇāṁ samavāyāt1 ।। 43 ।।</ab>
<p>paṭhitē jñāpanē prativacanē ca kimēkapātrāṇāmēvānujñāpanaṁ utā-
viśēṣēṇēti । avidhānādaviśēṣaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । dr̥ṣṭārtha-
tayā tu rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="44">।। 17 ।।yājyāpanayanēnāpanītō bhakṣaḥ pravaravat2 ।। 44 ।।</ab>
<p>yājyāmātrāpanayanaṁ manvānasya pūrvapakṣavādinō hōturēva bhakṣa
ityabhiprāyaḥ । kimanavānaśrutiḥ niṣadya yajatītivat vacanaṁ na
paśyati । na na paśyati, yājyāmātrē । ēvamētada‍dvayamapyupapadyata
﻿<pb n="b873"/>
ityabhiprāyaḥ । yājyābhidhānēna yajēḥ kartr̥tvamupapadyata ityarthaḥ ।
rāddhāntavādī tu manyatē । satyamupapadyatē na punarvaṣaṭa‍kārāpanayē kiñcana
pramāṇamasti iti savaṣaṭa‍kāramēva yājyāprayōgamātrēpyupapadyata iti
vyāpāramaṅgīkr̥tya kartr̥tvaṁ yuktamiti । yat‍tu pravarō nāpanīyata iti
tadatraupadēśikatvāt yathā pravarō nāpanīyatē tathā pradarśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="47">।। 18 ।। phalacamasō naimittikō bhakṣavikāraḥ śrutisaṁyōgāt ।। 47 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṁ phalacamasō bhakṣavikāra utējyāvikāra iti । asmin
saṁśayē brūmaḥ naivātra saṁśayaḥ tamasmaibhakṣaṁ prayacchēt iti bhakṣasaṁba-
﻿<pb n="b874"/>
ndhitvēna vidhānāt । bhakṣē sōmaṁ vikārōti na yāgē । na ca
yāgavikāraḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । utpattiśiṣṭatvāt sōmasya ।
vidhīyamānē tu karmāntarāpattiḥ । tataśca bhakṣavikārō'pi na syāt
dūrē ijyāvikāratā । atrābhidhīyatē---nējyāvikāramantarēṇa bhakṣaṁ
vikartuṁ samarthaḥ phalacamasaḥ । ijyāśēṣasya hi sōmasya bhakṣaḥ । na
cāśēṣabhūtē bhakṣyamāṇē sa vikr̥tō bhavati । tasmādijyāśēṣataiva phala-
camasasyāpi mantavyā । nanu cōtpattiśiṣṭatvāt sōmasya yāgē vidhānaṁ
na saṁbhavatītyuktam । yāgānuvādēna vidhānē hi apratyabhijñāna-
﻿<pb n="b875"/>
muktam । na punaḥ kāryēṇāpi saṁbandhē । kāryata ēvāyaṁ saṁbandhaḥ ।
nanu ca bhāṣyakārēṇa yāgasaṁbandhābhāvaṁ cōdayitvā yāja-
yēditi saṁbandha uktaḥ yajinā । yāgānvayapradarśanārthaṁ taduktam
na punaranūdya vidhānāyētyadōṣaḥ । bhakṣaṁ kuryāditi cōpasaṁhāraḥ
imamēvārthaṁ prakaṭīkarōti । tasmādijyāvikāraḥ phalacamasa iti
siddham । guṇavidhānāni ca pradarśitāni ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="52">।। 20 ।। anuprasarpiṣu sāmānyāt1 ।। 52 ।।</ab>
<p>daśadaśa ēkaikaṁ camasamanuprasarpantīti vidhānāt śataṁ brāhmaṇāḥ
sōmān bhakṣayantītyanuvādaṁ manvānasya nābhakṣō rājēti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b876"/>
satyamēvaṁ yadyanuvādaḥ syāt । na cānuvr̥ttē rājani anuvādaḥ
śakyatē vak‍tum । ayathārthānuvādaprasaṅgāt । nanu cānuvādē
ayathārthatvaṁ adōṣaḥ bhūyastvēna lakṣaṇā bhaviṣyati । satyaṁ yadyē-
kāntatō'nuvādaḥ iha punarvidhēyatayāpyupapadyata ēvēti nāyathārthatvaṁ
śakyatē । tasmāt dvayamapyētadvidhīyatē śataṁ brāhmaṇāḥ daśa ēkaikaṁ
camasaṁ iti ca । nanu ca <q>‘samaṁ syādaśrutatvāt’</q> iti nyāyēna śatē
vibhajyamānē ēkaikatra daśadaśaprāptēḥ daśa daśa ēkaikaṁ camasamanu-
prasarpanti ityanuvādaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b877"/>
<p>na ēkaikatra śataprāptēḥ pratyuddēśaṁ vākyasamāptēḥ । tasmāda-
bhakṣō rājā brāhmaṇavidhānāditi । yatpunaratra śataṁ brāhmaṇāssōmān
ityanēkārthavidhānaṁ manyatē, tadayuktaṁ, yasmāt karmāntaravidhānēnāpi
prākr̥takāryārthatāṁ daśamē vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyasya
pañcamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b878"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>br̥hatyāṁ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>tr̥tīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। sarvārthamaprakaraṇāt1 ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṁ punaratra kāraṇaṁ pakṣadvayōpanyāsasya । kasya pakṣadvayōpanyā-
sasya ? । cōdakādanārabhyavidhiḥ balīyān sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭatvāccēti ।
prathamasya tāvatpakṣasya idaṁ prayōjanaṁ naivātra dviruktatā vidyatē ।
upadēśātidēśābhyāṁ prakr̥tivikr̥tyōḥ sruksaṁbhavān । ēvaṁ tarhi
sāmānyatō darśanēna prakr̥tyarthatēti । aparasya pakṣasyōpanyāsaḥ prāya-
﻿<pb n="b879"/>
darśanavat । ayaṁ tāvadanantaraḥ pakṣō nirākriyatē । na sāmā-
nyatō dr̥ṣṭaṁ śabdārthāvagatau hētuḥ । nāpi prāyadarśanam ।
prakr̥tāviva vikr̥tāvapi saṁkṣēpavistārōpadēśadarśanāt । idānī-
maparasya pakṣasya nirasanaṁ cōdakāpēkṣaścēt anārabhya vidhiḥ ।
prakr̥tau pūrvamupadēśō'pēkṣaṇīyaḥ upadēśāpēkṣatvādatidēśasya ।
upadēśēna cēdupasaṁhr̥tō'nārabhyavidhiḥ nātidēśamapēkṣatē ।
﻿<pb n="b880"/>
kāryata ēva vikr̥tau prāptatvāt । atō dviruktatā'saṁbhavāt advirukta-
tvāditi sthitō hētuḥ । yastu yāgasaṁbandhōpanyāsaḥ1 asāvavaśyaṁ
bhāvī cōdaka iti pradarśayitum । avaśyaṁbhāvitvē cādviruktatvasya
siddhiruktā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 2 ।। prakaraṇaviśēṣāt‍tu vikr̥tau virōdhi syāt2 ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cānārabhyādhītaṁ sāptadaśyaṁ, yacca prakaraṇādhītaṁ
pāñcadaśyaṁ ubhayamapi śrutyaiva sāmidhēnīsaṁbandhitayā
﻿<pb n="b881"/>
cōdyatē । kō'ya prakaraṇōpanyāsaḥ । naivātra(yōtra) prakaraṇaṁ vini-
yōjakaṁ yēna prakaraṇavidhirbalīyān bhavati । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ
prakaraṇasavyapēkṣā ēva śrutyādayō viniyōjakāḥ iti । satyaṁ grāha-
kalakṣaṇaprakaraṇasavyapēkṣāḥ na tu viniyōjakamapēkṣantē । grāhakasa-
vyapēkṣā cānārabhyavidhērapi tulyaiva । atō'trāpi dviruktērasaṁbhavāt
prakr̥tāvēvēti yuktam ।</p>
<p>astyatra viśēṣaḥ । prakr̥tatvē hi pāñcadaśyasya grāhakapratyabhi-
jñānaṁ saṁbhavati । avyavāyāt । anārabhyavidhēḥ punaḥ kāryatō
grāhakāvamarśaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b882"/>
<p>ēvaṁ ca sati na klr̥ptē kalpanā saṁbhavati iti na prakr̥tau
nivēśaḥ । pratipattyavirōdhinī hi kalpanā na pratipannōpamardinī ।
tasmādvikr̥tāvanārabhya vidhānamiti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 3 ।। naimittikaṁ tu prakr̥tau tadvikāraḥ saṁyāgaviśēṣāta1 ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaratra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā । itthamāśaṅkā kratvarthē bādhyamānē upa-
dēśaḥ pīḍitō bhavati । nacōpadēśāśādr̥tē prakr̥tau sāda‍guṇyāvagatirbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b883"/>
vikr̥tau punaḥ kāryata ēva sāda‍guṇyāvagatiḥ ityēkakārya-
tvāt puruṣārthēnāpi kratōḥ sāda‍guṇyaṁ śakyatē vak‍tuṁ kārya-
viśēṣāt । tasmāt puruṣārthānāṁ vikr̥tau nivēśaḥ । satyamēvaṁ
yadi prakr̥tāvapi kāryaviśēṣō na syāt । iha tu dr̥ṣṭārthatvādupadēśasya
tulyaḥ kāryaviśēṣaḥ । (kārya)viśēṣāvagamācca sāmānyatō balīyastvaṁ
viśēṣōpadēśasyēti prakr̥tāvēva nivēśaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">।। 4 ।। iṣṭyarthamagnyādhēyaṁ prakaraṇāt1 ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaratrēṣṭēḥ prakaraṇaṁ ? iṣṭērapi naivādhikāraśrutirasti ।
﻿<pb n="b884"/>
ādhānasyaiva hi sādhikārasya vidhēḥ prakaraṇam । tasmānnēṣṭēḥ prakaraṇaṁ
iti śakyatē vak‍tum । kathaṁ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? bhavatō vā
kō'bhiprāyaḥ । na kiñcitpratibhāti । atrābhidhīyatē---dvayamapya-
trōdāharaṇam । kimādhānaṁ utēṣṭaya iti । dvayōḥ prādhānyamayukta-
miti manvānasya iṣṭēścāṅgabāhulyāt prādhānyārōpēṇa pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu dvayōrapyadhikārābhāvāt । agnyarthatayā ca
viniyōgōpapattēḥ dvayōragnyarthatvam । tathā ca liṅgadarśanam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b885"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 5 ।। tatprakr̥tyarthaṁ yathā'nyē'nārabhyavādāḥ ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>kimidānīṁ prakr̥tyarthamādhānaṁ uta sarvārthamiti । ētaduk‍taṁ
bhavati---kiṁ kratvarthanāmag‍nīnāmādhānaṁ uta āhitānāṁ kratvarthatēti ।
kaścātra viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśēṣaḥ---yadi kratvarthānāmādhānaṁ tataḥ
parṇamayītvavat prakr̥tigāmitvamādhānavidhēḥ । atha tu āhitānāṁ
kratvarthatā tadā hōmādimātraśēṣatayā'g‍nīnāṁ sarvārthamādhāna-
mityucyatē । kiṁ punaratra yuktam ? parṇatādivat kratusaṁbandhānāmēvāgrī-
nāmādhānamiti । āhitāg‍nēradhikārāt āhitānāṁ kratvarthatēti ।
﻿<pb n="b886"/>
yathā vā āhitāgnērādhikārastathā ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । vasantādikāla-
vidhiścaivamupapannō bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 6 ।। tāsāmagniḥ prakr̥titaḥ prayājavat1 ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaḥ pavamānēṣṭiṣu pavamānēṣṭisaṁskr̥tā agnayaḥ āśaṅkya-
ntē । yā api hi tāḥ agnyarthā iṣṭayaḥ tā api
pavamānēṣṭaya ēva । tasmādanāśaṅkanīyamēvēdamāśaṅkitam । atrōcyatē
---idamēvātra cintyatē । kimayamatidēśaḥ prakr̥tau yāva-
dupakārakaṁ tāvadatidiśati uta yathākāryamatidēśa iti ।
﻿<pb n="b887"/>
tatra pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ । yāvadupakārakaṁ tāvadati-
diśatīti । rāddhāntavādī punaḥ yathākāryamati-
dēśaḥ । upadēśētu viparītam । tasmānnaitadupadēśavad
draṣṭavyam । upadēśaviśēṣapradarśanārthaṁ caitadupadēśalakṣaṇē cintitam ।
﻿<pb n="b888"/>
anyathā hi anvārambhaṇīyādhikaraṇēnaiva gatam syāt । agnyartha-
tayā ca pavamānēṣṭīnāṁ upadēśānyatvē yatnaḥ iti viśēṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 7 ।। tulyaḥ sarvēṣāṁ paśuvidhiḥ prakaraṇāviśēṣāt1 ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaridamadhikaraṇaṁ prārabdham । yathaiva bhāṣyakārēṇa । na tathā
śakyatē vak‍tum । tasmādyadi tāvadidaṁ jyōtiṣṭōmākhyaprakaraṇaṁ tadā
﻿<pb n="b889"/>
śrutyādībhirēva paśuyāgasaṁbandhāt viśasanādīnām । kimidaṁ
prakaraṇaviśēṣāditi sarvārthatōcyatē । atha prakaraṇē aviśēṣaḥ
paśūnāmityaviśēṣatōcyatē kathaṁ tarhi sūtraṁ---asti tu prakaraṇē viśēṣa
iti । nacāvāntaraprakaraṇaṁ nāma kiñcidasti jyautiṣṭōmikamahāprakaraṇē ।
prakaraṇāntarē cābhyupagamyamānē('rthē) na tāvatprakaraṇamagrīṣōmīyā-
dērupapadyatē । kimityēva hi tadā jyōtiṣṭōmasaṁbandhō'bhyupagataḥ
syāt । ēvaṁ ca dīkṣaṇīyādēritikartavyatābhāva ēva hīyēta ।
﻿<pb n="b890"/>
﻿<pb n="b891"/>
darśapūrṇamāsayōśca prayājādēritikartavyatāprasaṅgaḥ prakaraṇaviniyō-
jyatayā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b892"/>
<p>tataśca <q>‘avyaktāsu tu sōmasyē’</q>ti sōmikī itikartavyatā
prāpnōti dīkṣaṇīyādēriva dārśapūrṇamāsikī । kimiti vā na bhavati ?
﻿<pb n="b893"/>
uktamavāntaraprakaraṇābhāvāditi । na hyēkasmin prayōgavacanē
nānākimityāṅkṣā saṁbhavati । ēkaścāyaṁ prayōgavacanaḥ sētikarta-
vyatākasya prayōgasyaikaśabda‍yāditi vakṣyati ।</p>
<p>kathaṁ tarhi dīkṣaṇīyādērātidēśikā dharmāḥ ? mā bhūvan,
na punaḥ kimityākāṅkṣādvayamēkasmin prakaraṇē saṁbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b894"/>
ēvaṁ sthitē yadidamucyatē prakaraṇātsavanīyasyēti sthānāccāgnīṣō-
mīyasyēti sarvamidamandhapadam । tasmāt mahatā prayat‍nēnātra bhāṣyaṁ
vyākhyēyam । atrābhidhīyatē---prakaraṇaṁ tāvadidaṁ jyōtiṣ‍ṭōmasya ।
aupavasathyē'hani dharmāścōdyantē । na ca paśavastasminnahani sarvē
sannihitāḥ sannihitavacanaṁ cōddēśakaṁ padam । ataḥ kasyāyamuddēśaka
iti cintyatē viśasanādividhiṣu । tatra prakaraṇāviśēṣāt sarvē
paśavō jyōtiṣṭōmārthatayā prakr̥tā iti sarvārthatāṁ manyatē ।</p>
<p>aparēṇa pūrvapakṣiṇā ahassāmānyasannidhānāt‍tu (sannikr̥ṣṭa iti)
sannidhiviśēṣō vidyata iti asti tu prakaraṇaviśēṣa ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b895"/>
prakr̥talakṣaṇaṁ ca prakaraṇamatrābhiprētam । ataḥ sthānādag‍nīṣōmīyasyēti
yuktam । (siddham) । aprakr̥tasiddha‍yarthaṁ ca sautyē'hani vidhānaṁ
savanīyasyētyēvamāda‍yupapannam । nanu sannidhānaviśēṣēṇāg‍nīṣōmī-
yārthatvē siddhē jyōtiṣṭōmaprakaraṇē cāmnānasyārthavatvē tasminnēva
prakaraṇē paśudvayasyātidēśaḥ । na hyēkaḥ prayōgavacanaḥ upadēśēna
atidēśēna ca tānēva dharmān gr̥hṇāti । asya cōdyasya parihāraṁ
atidēśa ēva vakṣyāmaḥ kr̥ts‍navidhānādapūrvaḥ sōma ityatra । asmin
﻿<pb n="b896"/>
punaradhikaraṇē upadēśaviśēṣō nirūpitaḥ । upadēśaviśēṣatvācchēṣa-
lakṣaṇasya । kaḥ punaḥ aupavasathyē'hani savanīyēṣu vidhīyamānēṣu
āśvinakālē vākyabhēdaḥ? nanvidaṁ pūrvapakṣī cōdayati । kathaṁ ca
sautyēhani savanīyēṣu vidhīyamānēṣu vākyabhēdaṁ rāddhāntavādī
cōdayati । kiñca ubhayatra vākyabhēda ēva cōditaḥ । ucyatē ।
anēkaguṇavidhānamēva vākyabhēdaṁ pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । rāddhānta-
vādyapi vapāpracāramātrōtkarṣaṁ manvānaḥ punarālambhavidhānē ca vākya-
bhēdamēva cōditavān । āg‍nēyyaudāsīnyamuktavān ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b897"/>
<p>kiṁ punaranayōrvākyabhēdayōrdūṣaṇam । rāddhāntavāda‍yuktamēva
dūṣaṇam । aparihāryaṁ hi tatra vākyāntaratvam । pūrvapakṣavāda‍yuktasya
tu viśiṣṭavidhānādapi siddhiḥ <q>“saṁskārō'yaṁ paśuyāgaprayuktaḥ
na jyōtiṣṭōmaprayukta”</q>1 iti । kimidaṁ jyōtiṣṭōmaprayuktaṁ iti ?
nanu ca sarvamēvēdaṁ jyōtiṣṭōmaprayuktam । tatprakaraṇāmnānāt ।
ucyatē । viniyōgābhipnāṁyō'yaṁ granthaḥ । na punaḥ prayōjyābhiprāyaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b898"/>
na prakaraṇaviniyōjyatayā prayuktiḥ(ityarthaḥ) । kiṁ tarhi ? śrutyaiva
viniyōga । <q>‘prakaraṇavantaśca’</q> iti । śaknōti hi svasthānēpi
prayōgavacanaḥ prayōk‍tumiti darśayati । ata ēva ca prakaraṇasthānē
api prakr̥tābhiprāyēṇaivētyuktam । darśanācchidrāpidhānē pratyuk‍tē ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 8 ।। 1dōhayōḥ kālabhēdādasaṁyuk‍taṁ śrr̥taṁ syāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvavadatrāpi sannidhānaviśēṣamaṅgīkr̥tya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ।
﻿<pb n="b899"/>
rāddhāntastu naiva dadhipayasōḥ kālabhēdēna vidhānamasti । yadi paraṁ
kramē kālabhēdaḥ sa ca prakaraṇē pratyarthini na viniyōjaka
ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 9 ।। 1tadvat savanāntarē grahāmnānam ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi pūrvavadēva sannidhānaviśēṣāśaṅkā pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu na dharmāṇāṁ savanaviśēṣē vidhānamiti sarvārthatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b900"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 10 ।। 1raśanā ca liṅgadarśanāt ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>raśanāyāstvagnīṣōmīyaprakaraṇa2 ēva vidhānamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu satyaṁ tatprakramē vidhānaṁ yūpastvēka iti sarvārthatō raśanā-
yāstaddharmāṇāṁ ca । tathā ca liṅgamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 11 ।। 3ārācchiṣṭamasaṁyuktamitaraissannidhānāt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>aṁśvadābhyayōstu prakaraṇē avidhānāt uddēśakasya ca sannihita-
vacanatvāt na taddharma iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu na sanni-
hitamātravacanamuddēśakaṁ prayōjanavatsannihitavacanaṁ hi tat ।
﻿<pb n="b901"/>
abhinnaṁ cātna prayōjanam । prakr̥tānāmaprakr̥tānāṁ ca grahaṇām । tasmāt
prayōjanābhēdāta prayōjanāvacchinnagrahajātīyē grahaśabdō na prakr̥tatvēna
saṅakōcamarhati । maitrāvaruṇē tu nirdēśāt yuktam । iha tu viparītō
nirdēśa ityapi darśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="35">।। 12 ।। agnyarthamaprakaraṇē tadvat ।। 35 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaranayōradhikaraṇayōrviśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśēṣaḥ ।
tatra hi ēkadravyasaṁbandhitvād‍yuktō viśēṣaḥ। iha punaḥ ēkaikēṣṭakā-
vyāpārasaṁbandhitayāpi dharmavidhayō'rthavantō bhavanti । tadayuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b902"/>
tatrāpi hi ēkaikagrahavyāpārabhēdō vidyata ēva । ēvaṁ tarhi citi-
bhēdāt abhyadhikāśaṅkā । rāddhāntastu yadyapi citibhēdaḥ tathāpi
citau dharmāṇāmapratiṣṭhitatvāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 13 ।। naimittikamatulyatvādasamānavidhānaṁ syāt ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē---kiṁ naimittikānāṁ dharmavidhayaḥ samānā
uta kāryavantō bhavantīti । tatra tulyatvāt prakaraṇasya samānā dharma-
vidhaya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । satyaṁ tulyaṁ prakaraṇam dharmavantastu nityāḥ
﻿<pb n="b903"/>
naimittikāśca gōdōhanādayaḥ । tad‍dvāraṁ ca prakaraṇasya grāhakatvamiti
sthitam । naimittikaṁ ca nityakāryāpannaṁ bhavati । ataḥ kāryataḥ
siddhēḥ na punarupadēśamarhati iti । dviruktatādōṣaścōktaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 14 ।। pratinidhiśca tadvat ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>athēdānīṁ pratinidhau kā vārtā । tatra kāryataḥ prāptiriti pūrva-
pakṣavādī manyatē kāryēṇākṣipratvātpratinidhēḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---satyaṁ
kāryēṇākṣiptaḥ pratinidhiḥ upadēśasaṁpadā tulyaḥ, nānyasādhyatayā,
﻿<pb n="b904"/>
tasmādaupadēśika ēva dharmasaṁbandhaḥ na kāryasādhanatayā dravyāntaraṁ
nīvārāḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 15 ।। niyamārthā guṇaśratiḥ ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra punaḥ śrūyatē pratinidhiḥ tatra śrutāśaṅkatayā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
śrutōpapattyarthō'yaṁ niyama iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="41">।। 16 ।। saṁsthāstu samānavidhānāḥ prakaraṇāviśēṣāt ।। 41 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cēdaṁ phalacamasēna gatamēvādhikaraṇam । na naimitti-
kasya dharmā bhavantyupadēśata iti । ucyatē---astyatrādhikā---
﻿<pb n="b905"/>
śaṅkā । kā punarasau ? iyamasau । ukthyādayō hi grahaṇa-
viśēṣāḥ । tē ca saṁskārāḥ svayamitikartavyatābhūtāḥ na cēti-
kartavyatā itikartavyatayā saṁbadhyatē । kiṁ tarhi ? yāgēna ।
﻿<pb n="b906"/>
sarvagrahaṇasaṁskāryadravyakaścāyaṁ sa ēva yāgaḥ sōmēna
yajētēti । nānyōtpattirvidyatē । sa cēdyāgaḥ grahaṇāntarē-
ṣvapi itikartavyatāpi saiva । na ca grahaṇaviśēṣō
yāgasyētikartavyatāprāptau nimittaṁ; kiṁ tarhi prayōga-
cōdanaiva । na ca grahaṇāntarēṣu prayōgāntaracōdanā yāgasya ।
guṇānāmēva hi tatra phalāya cōdanā na yāgasya, yathā
gōdōhanēna paśukāmasya praṇayēditi na darśapūrṇamāsayōḥ
﻿<pb n="b907"/>
prayōgaścōdyatē । tasmādbhavantu grahaṇāni grahaṇadharmōpadēśaśūnyāni phala-
camasavat na punaryāgō'pi yāgadharmaśūnya iti śakyatē vak‍tum । 
sarvasaṁskārēṣvēkaprayōgasya cōditatvāt । prayōgagrāhyatvāccēti-
kartavyatāyā ityuktam । ata ēva cāgniṣṭōmagrahaṇaṁ samuccayaśca
pradarśitaḥ । paśūnāmadr̥ṣṭārthatayā samuccaya ēva nyāyyaḥ । atrōcyatē
-savanīyasamākhyayā sarvapaśūnāṁ tulyakāryāvagamāt । atrābhidhīyatē
---satyamēvaṁ syādyadi saṁsthantārēṣu ukthyādiṣu prayōgacōdanayaiva
labhyatē । yathā gōdōhanēna darśapūrṇamāsayōḥ । iha tu agniṣṭōma-
﻿<pb n="b908"/>
paryantaiva yāgasya prayōgacōdanā । ata ūrdhvaṁ grahā ukthyādaya
ēva cōdanāmākṣipanti yathā grahāḥ āvr̥ttim nimittē । ēvaṁ
cēnna yāgacōdanayā dharmāḥ śakyantē grahītuṁ ukthyādiṣu । ataḥ
phalacamasavat nityānityasaṁyōgavirōdhō yuktaḥ । kāryataśca dharmaprāptiḥ
tasmāt samuccayagrahaṇaṁ vacanāt bhaviṣyati । agniṣṭōmaśabdaścānu-
vādaḥ । tathā hōmādīnāmabhāvadarśanamupapannaṁ bhavati ।</p> 
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
ṣaṣṭaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
<pb n="b909"/>
﻿<pb n="b910"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tr̥tīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। prakaraṇāviśēṣādasaṁyuk‍taṁ pradhānasya ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>barhirdharmāśca kimaṅgapradhānārthā uta pradhānārthā ēvēti sandēhē
prakaraṇāt pradhānārthā ityuk‍tvā upakārakatvēnāṅgapradhānārthatāmāha ।
tadayuktam । śrutyādimirhi tādarthyamavagamyatē nōpakārēṇa ।</p>
<p>ucyatē---śrutyādaya ēvōpanyastā barhiṣi havīṁṣyāsādayatīti ।
upakārakagrahaṇaṁ tarhi kimarthaṁ ? kadācit tadabhāvāt śrutēḥ saṅkōcaḥ
syāt । asti cāsāvēkarūpa upakārō nāmēti tadabhidhānam ।
﻿<pb n="b911"/>
ēvaṁ tarhi vākyēnaiva śēṣāvagatiḥ । kimiti tarhi barhirmātrē(ṇa)
na bhavati ? grāhakatvē sati śēṣatvamityuktam । grāhakaśca dārśapaurṇa-
māsikaprayōgavidhiḥ sannidhānāt । liṅgadarśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। phalasaṁyōgātsvāmiyuktaṁ pradhānasya 2 ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>iha purūṣasaṁskārā udāharaṇam । tē kiṁ karkr̥bhūtasya utādhi-
kr̥tasyēti । kartr̥bhūtasya । ēvaṁ karmāṅgatōpapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b912"/>
kimityaṁśōpanipātinī itikartavyatēti saptamādyē vakṣyāmaḥ ।
ākāṅkṣādvayasya tatprasūtēḥ । tatra yadarthaḥ kartr̥bhāvaḥ saṁskārō'pi
tadartha ēva yuktaḥ । adhikāraniṣpattyarthatvācchāstrasya । tasmādadhi-
kr̥tasyasaṁskāra iti yuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 3 ।।cikīrṣayā ca saṁyōgāt1 ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>barhirdharmādhikaraṇēna kimatrānyatvaṁ yēnēdamādhikaraṇamārabhyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b913"/>
pradhānacikīrṣāṁ dhurvapakṣavādī manyatē । yadarthā cikīrṣā tadarthā-
nyaṅgānītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 4 ।। tathābhidhānēna1 ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>abhimarśanē tu sākṣātpradhānaśabdasaṁyōgāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । satyaṁ,
pradhānaṁ cikīrṣyatē । tat‍tu sāṅgaṁ adhikāranirvr̥ttāviti rāddhāntaḥ ।
ēvamabhimarśanamapi adhikārasādhanasyaivēti ubhayōraṅgapradhānārthatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b914"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">।। 6 ।। dīkṣādakṣiṇaṁ tu vacanātpradhānēsya1 ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>dīkṣādakṣiṇamapi sāṅgādadhikāranirvr̥t‍tēḥ sāṅgasyētyāśaṅkya
vacanātpradhānasyēti rāddhāntaḥ । yuk‍taṁ tāvat vacanāt dīkṣā
prādhānasya । dakṣiṇā punaḥ yadā pradhānasyaiva kathamapi tadā
kathamaparikrītairaṅgāni kriyantē । kēna vōk‍tamaparikrītairaṅgāni kriyanta
iti prākr̥tamānatikāraṇaṁ bhaviṣyatyēva । yadyēvaṁ na tarhi prasaṅgaḥ ।
yathā prasaṅgaḥ tathā prasaṅgalakṣaṇa ēva vakṣyāmaḥ । darśanamuk‍tam ।</p> 
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 6 ।। tathā yūpasya vēdiḥ2 ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>ardhamantarvēdīti kiṁ vēdiḥ yūpāṅgamuta nēti saṁśayē
﻿<pb n="b915"/>
śrutēraṅgamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । bahirvēdipadaikavākyatvāt na śrutyartha-
vidhānaṁ saṁbhavatīti dēśalakṣaṇā । ubhayavidhānē vākyabhēda-
prasaṅgāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">sāmidhēnīstadanvāhuriti havirdhānayōrvacanātsāmidhēnīnām1 ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaḥ pūrvēṇāsyādhikaraṇasya viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśēṣaḥ
padāntarāsaṁbaddhaṁ hyatra havirdhānaṁ śrūyatē nāntarvēdivat bahirvēdipada-
saṁbaddham । tasmādaṅgāṅgibhāva iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē śrutēḥ
﻿<pb n="b916"/>
vijñānaviparītaṁ hi virūddhamabhidhīyatē । rāddhāntavādītu ubhayō---
ranyārthatvāt dēśalakṣaṇasaṁbandha ēva nyāyya iti manyatē । tathā
ca <q>‘havirdhānaṁ’</q> <q>‘sāmidhēnya’</q> iti ca samākhyāpi na pīḍitā syāt ।
anyathāhi havirdhānaṁ sāmidhēnīnāṁ sāmidhēnyō vā havirdhānasyēti
dēvadattasyēdaṁ yajñadattasyēti yathaitadasaṁbaddhaṁ tathēdamapi syāt । tasmāda-
trāpi pūrvavat dēśaviśēṣalakṣaṇaivēti yuktam । āgnēyyadhikaraṇavacca
sāmānyaviśēṣasaṁbandhē vākyabhēdaḥ syāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">śāstraphalaṁ prayōk‍tari tallakṣaṇatvāt tasmātsvayaṁ prayōgē syāt1 ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaratra parikrayādiṣu śrūyamāṇēṣu saṁśayaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b917"/>
ayamabhiprāyaḥ kartr̥gāmikriyāphalamatra śrūyatē । atastadvirōdhāt
gauṇaṁ adr̥ṣṭārthaṁ vaha manyatē । kathaṁ tarhi samākhyāḥ ādhvaryavamityēva-
mādyāḥ ? granthasaṁyōgādupapannā bhaviṣyanti । tasmātsvayaṁ kartr̥-
taiva nyāyyēti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । aniyamavādī tu parīkrītairapi
kriyamāṇaṁ tēnaiva kr̥taṁ bhavati । sa hi tēṣāṁ prayōktā । prayōk‍tuśca
kartr̥tvasmaraṇam । na punarāhatyaiva kartr̥tvam । utsargastu svadravya-
tyāgalakṣaṇatvāt svayamēva kartavyaḥ । ēvaṁ kartr̥tvē upapannē na
parikrayasya gauṇatā, adr̥ṣṭārthatā vā kalpayituṁ śakyatē । samā-
﻿<pb n="b918"/>
khyāśca mukhyārthāḥ na granthadvārikāḥ kalpitā bhaviṣyanti । na hi
adhyētārō'dhvaryuśabdavācyāḥ adhyayanakālē । kathaṁ punaraniyamaṁ
manyatē । ayamabhiprāyaḥ yadā svayamanutsāhī tadā parikrayaḥ yadāsau
parikrayaḥ tadā anyairēvēti manyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu manyatē
nityavadānnānāt parikrayasya yadā svayaṁ na śak‍nuyāt tadā
parikrayēṇēti na śakyatē kalpayitum । nanu ca sāmarthyādbhaviṣyati
lōkavata । na hi śrutau pratyarthinyāṁ sāmarthyaṁ prabhavatītyuktam ।
lōkē tu dr̥ṣṭārthatvāt yathārthamiti yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b919"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="9">।। 9 ।। 1tatrārthāt kartr̥parimāṇaṁ syōdaniyamō'viśēṣāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>ēvaṁ sthitē parikrītakartr̥tvē anyatrōtsargāt aniyamaṁ
saṅkhyāyāḥ pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । ēkasminnapi samākhyāvaraṇayō-
rupapattēḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu utpattau tāvat samākhyātō bhēdaṁ manvānaḥ
na punarēka ēva saṁjñī । cōdanāvagamyatvāt saṁjñānām, cōdanā-
bhēdācca yāvaccōdanaṁ saṁjñibhēdaniyamamuktavān । ēvaṁ darśapūrṇamā-
sādiṣvapītyuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b920"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 10 ।। 1camasādhvaryavaśca tairvyapadēśāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>camasādhvaryavaśca kiṁ r̥tviksaṅkhyāsaṅkhyēyāḥ uta saṅkhyāntara
paricthēdyāḥ । nanu ca hōtr̥kāṇāṁ camasādhvaryava iti vyapadēśāt
anyairbhavitavyam । parasparavyapadēśādapyētadupapadyata iti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ । na hi ṣaṣṭha‍yantānāṁ parasparasaṁbandhō vidyata iti rāddhāntavādī
vyatirik‍taṁ manyatē । utpattau ca saṁjñābhēdāt । tasmādanyē tē
iti ।</p> 
<ab type="sutra" n=" ">।। 11 ।। 2utpattau ca bahuśrutēḥ ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ sandihyatē---kimaniyatā uta bahava iti
﻿<pb n="b921"/>
prātipadikārthasiddhēraniyatā iti । aniyamē'pi bahuvacanōpapattēḥ ।
na, nityavadvahuvacanasya śrūyamāṇatvāt । utpattau ca bahuvacanasya
vivakṣitatvāt । asiddhārthalakṣaṇaṁ hi prātipadikaṁ na vacanama-
pēkṣatē । nōtpādyavacanam । tasmādvahavaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 12 ।। 1daśatvaṁ liṅgadarśanāt ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitē bahutvē kimaniyamaḥ uta niyataiva kācit bahuvacanā-
bhidhēyā saṅkhyā uta tritvasaṅkhyaivēti । kapiñjalādhikaraṇēna tri-
saṅkhyaivēti prāptē darśanāda‍daśapēyē, svāmidaśatvācca daśaivēti niyamaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b922"/>
anyatrāpi śrūyamāṇā niyatā saṅkhyā aniyatōpadēśaṁ niyantumarhati
avirōdhāt । tathā cōktaṁ kāraṇādatikrama iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 13 ।। 1śamitā ca śabdabhēdāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>ēvaṁ sthitē śabhitāpi śabdabhēdāt camasādhvaryuvadbhidyatē ।
saṁjñābhēdaścōpapannō bhavati । ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē-nātra bhēdaḥ utpatti-
nibandhanō hi bhēda uktaḥ । na cāsyōtpattirasti । kathaṁ tarhi saṁjñānyatvaṁ ?
﻿<pb n="b923"/>
naivēyaṁ saṁjñā asya, virōdhāt । kiṁ tarhi ? yaugikābhidhānamēva ।
ēvaṁ cādhvaryavamiti samākhyōpapannā bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 14 ।। 1upagāśca liṅgadarśanāt ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>kēna punarviśēṣēṇāyamadhikaraṇātidēśaḥ ? ayaṁ viśēṣaḥ
upagā iti gānakāriṇāṁ saṁbandhāt camasādhvaryava iva hōtra-
kāṇāmiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । utpattēraśravaṇādityatidiṣṭō
rāddhāntaḥ । liṅgamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b924"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">1vikrayī tvanyaḥ karmaṇō'cōditatvāt ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>sōmavikrayī punaḥ kaḥ ? tēṣāmēvānyatama iti manyatē । nanu
cācōditō vikrayaḥ । cōditasya ca r̥tvijaḥ kartr̥tvēnōpādīyantē ।
krayōpādānaśēṣatvaṁ vikrayē manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu
lōbhādēvākṣēpasiddhēḥ dravyārjanavanna śēṣaṁ manyatē । tasmādanā-
rtvijamētat । atō'nya iti rāddhāntitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 16 ।। karmakāryāt sarvēṣāmr̥tviktvamaviśēṣāt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātra rāddhāntō na ghaṭatē । kathaṁ na ghaṭatē ?
﻿<pb n="b925"/>
utpattāvapi hi parisaṅkhyaiva prāpnōti । camasādhvaryūṇāmapyutpatti-
śravaṇāt । atha parisaṅkhyaivēṣṭā, r̥tuyajananimittanirasanamanarthakaṁ
syāt । atrōcyatē---utpattau naiva parisaṅkhyā prāpnōti । ēkaikatra
udgātrādiśabdatulyatvāt r̥tvika‍śabdasya nātrāpahnavanīyaṁ kiñci-
dasti । r̥tuyajananimittē punarapahnavaḥ prāp‍nōti । na cāsau
śakyatē । ēvaṁ cōparitanamadhikaraṇamupapannaṁ bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b926"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 17 ।। 1niyamastu dakṣiṇābhiḥ śrutisaṁyōgāt ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>kē ta iti । r̥tvigbhyō dakṣiṇāṁ dadātīti prakramya yān
saṁkīrtayati tē ta iti rāddhāntaḥ । tathā yē yajamānāsta r̥tvija
iti darśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 18 ।। 2svāmisaptadaśāḥ karmasāmānyāt ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>saptadaśa r̥tvija iti śrūyatē । tatra kiṁ saha yajamānēn saptadaśa
uta yajamānavyatiriktā anyē saptadaśēti karmakarasaṅkhyaiṣā । na ca
svāmī karmakaraḥ । ēkadharmayuktānāṁ cāvāntarasaṅkhyōpapadyatē ityanya
ēvēti yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b927"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---svāmisaptadaśāḥ saptadaśaḥ svāmī yēṣāṁ tē
tayōktāḥ । nanu ca karmakarasāmānyaprayuk‍taivaiṣā'vāntarasaṅkyā ।
kēna vōk‍taṁ nēti । kathaṁ tarhi svāmisaptadaśāḥ saptadaśa । na
svāmitayā yajamānaḥ saptadaśaḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? kartr̥tayaiva । yajamānā-
pēkṣaiṣā saṅkhyā nādhikāritayā । nanu ca sadasyaṁ vr̥ṇīta iti
varaṇōtpat‍tibhaṅgīkr̥tya ēṣāṁ saṅkhyā, na ca yajamāna utpadyatē ।
ucyatē---ṣōḍaśānāmēva varaṇēnōtpat‍tiḥ । nanu ca sadasyaṁ vr̥ṇīta iti
sadasyaḥ saptadaśō bhaviṣyati yadi brahmaṇyēvāyaṁ sadasyaśabdō vartatē ।
﻿<pb n="b928"/>
tasmāt svāmisaptadaśāḥ parigr̥hyantē । atha kasmādēkaścama-
sādhvaryuḥ na parigr̥hyatē ? na tē yajamānēna varitavyā ityuktam ।
tasmāt karmakaraṇasāmānyāt yajamāna ēvētyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 19 ।। 1tē sarvārthāḥ prayuktatvādagnayaśca svakālatvāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ sandihyatē---kiṁ sarvārthā r̥rtvijaḥ yāvatpuruṣakāryaṁ
yajamānasya tāvattaiḥ kriyatē uta yāvadvacanamiti । <q>“agnayaśca
svakālatvā”</q>diti । kimidaṁ ? nanu cādhānasya sarvārthatāṁ vadatā
agnīnāṁ sarvārthatvamuktam । kimidaṁ punaḥ sarvārthatōcyatē ? saivēyaṁ
﻿<pb n="b929"/>
sarvārthatā'tra sādhyatē svakālatvāditi । nanu ca svakālatvāt
yāvadagnikāryaṁ tatsarvamagnimirityucyatē yathā yāvatpuruṣakāryaṁ tatsarva-
mr̥tvigbhiriti । tataḥ kim ? tadēva nōpapadyatē samadhigatamētat
agnayaśca svakālatvāditi । na hi svakālatvādyāvadagni-
kāryaṁ tadarthatā siddha‍yati । kiṁ tarhi ? svakālatvēna
sarvakarmārthatā siddha‍yati na hi pratikarmōtpattirbhavatītyarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b930"/>
ēvaṁ tarhi bhavataivōk‍tam । yasmādyasyaiva hētuḥ sa ēva pratijñātārthaḥ ।
tasmāt sūtradvayamēvaitat । ādhastyasūtrasya parihārō'yamucyatē ।
idaṁ tu sthitamēva । na hyatra vacanāni nityānuvādatayā kalpyantē ।
tasmādyavadvacanamēvaitat r̥tvijāṁ kāryam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="41">।। 21 ।। 1tasyōpadēśasamākhyānēna nirdēśaḥ ।। 41 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē । yadyēna samākhyāyatē tat
tēnaiva kartavyaṁ uta kiñcidanyēnāpi iti । ēṣa tāvadutsargaḥ
yadyēna samākhyāyatē tattēna kartavyamiti । ucyatē---vacanāt
﻿<pb n="b931"/>
samākhyānācca apavādaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi samākhyāḥ ? brāhmaṇagrāma-
vadityadōṣaḥ । darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="43">।। 22 ।। 1praiṣānuvacanaṁ maitrāvaruṇasyōpadēśāt ।। 43 ।।</ab>
<p>maitrāvaruṇaḥ prēṣyati cānucāhēti kiṁ praiṣamātraṁ anuvacanamātraṁ
maitrāvaruṇēna kartavyaṁ, uta saṁyuktamēvēti । saṁyuktasya vidyamāna-
tvānnāsaṁyuk‍taṁ parigr̥hyatē । caśabdaścaivaṁ samarthitō bhavati ।
darśanamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b932"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="46">।। 23 ।। 1camasāṁścamasādhvaryavassamākhyānāt ।। 46 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṁ camasaiścamasādhvaryavō juhvati utādhvaryurēvēti । samākhyai-
vānyathā nōpapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu---adhvaryuśabda-
syōtpat‍tinimittatvāt । adhvaryuriva camasēṣu bhavantīti cama-
sādhvaryavaḥ tasmādadhvaryurjuhōtīti । kathaṁ tarhi adhvaryuriva bhavati ?
anyatra vyāpr̥tē tasmin tatkāryakaratvāt । darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="50">।। 24 ।। 2vēdōpadēśāt pūrvavadvēdānyatvē yathōpadēśaṁ syuḥ ।। 50 ।।</ab>
<p>śyēnavājapēyāvudāharaṇam । kiṁ śyēnaḥ udgātrā kartavyaḥ
samākhyānāta adhvaryuṇā ca vājapēyaḥ uta ṣōḍaśabhirapīti ।
﻿<pb n="b933"/>
viśēṣasamākhyānāta udgātrā'dhvaryuṇā cēti prāptē upakāradarśanāt
ṣōḍaśabhirapīti vadāmaḥ । klr̥ptō balīyānityuktau hētuḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
saptamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b934"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tr̥tīyādhyāyasya aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1svāmikarma parikrayaḥ karmaṇastadarthatvāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>samākhyayā ādhvaryavamiti prāptē adhikāraśrutivirōdhāt
yājamānamiti rāddhāntaḥ । vacanādanyēṣāmr̥tvijāmapi parikrayaḥ
syāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। saṁskārastu puruṣasāmarthyē yathāvēdaṁ karmavadva‍yavatiṣṭhēran ।।</ab>
<p>vapanādīnāṁ samākhyayā nādhikārō virudhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b935"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu puruṣasaṁskāraṁ manvānō na saṁskartuṁ puruṣāḥ pari-
krīyantē । kiṁ tarhi kārayitum, ataḥ sāmarthyāt samākhyābādhaṁ
manyatē । yatra punaḥ śrutyaiva saṁskāraścōdyatē na tatra sāmarthyā-
nnivr̥ttiḥ yathōpavāsaṁ vakṣyati । athōbhayānugrahāya samānavidhānaṁ
kasmānna bhavatīti cēt ? r̥tvikṣu kriyamāṇō yajamānēna kr̥taḥ
kāritō vā na bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b936"/>
<p>kimiti na kr̥taḥ kāritō vā ? 1sādhāraṇyādēva । nanu cēḍā-
bhakṣaṇavat svayaṁ ca karōti kārayati ca । na । tatra kartr̥tvēnā-
viśēṣāt । iha tu prādhānyāviśēṣādanupapattiḥ । tasmādyājamāna-
iti siddham । vacanādvā yajamānapañcamā iti ।</p>*****
<ab type="sutra" n="9">।। 3 ।। 2tapaśca phalasiddhitvāllōkavat ।। 9 ।।</ab>
<p>kimatrātidiśyatē ? rāddhāntaḥ । kā punaratra pūrvapakṣā-
śaṅkā ? iyamasti klēśarūpatvāt tapasaḥ । parikrayaśca
klēśāpanuttayē dr̥ṣṭārthō bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b937"/>
<p>na saṁskārasāmānyāditi rāddhāntaḥ । darśanamuktam । upa-
vāsaśca vacanādityētadapyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 4 ।। 1guṇatvācca vēdēna na vyavasthā syāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>hiraṇyamālyādiṣu tu guṇatvādēva padārthasya na samākhyayā
kartr̥tvaṁ niyamyata iti sarvartvijāṁ pratipradhānāvr̥ttyā guṇō bhavitu-
marhati । yatra punaḥ kartr̥tayaiva saṁbandhaḥ yathōkthyādiṣu tatrōktaḥ
samākhyayā niyamaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b938"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 5 ।। 1tathākāmō'rthasaṁyōgāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kāmasaṁyōga idānīṁ śrūyamāṇaḥ kimārtvijō bhavatu guṇaphala-
