saṁbandhēṣu uta yājamāna iti । kiṁ yuktam ? ārtvijaḥ ।
kutaḥ ? r̥tvika‍padārthāśritatvāt guṇaphalasaṁbandhasya kāmasaṁyōgō'pi
r̥tvijāmēva । atō guṇakāmēṣu r̥tvijāmadhikāra iti । atrō-
cyatē । yajamāna ēvādhikriyatē sāṅgē karmaṇyadhikr̥tatvāt । nanu
cāsāvārtvijapadārthaḥ । nēti brūmaḥ । tatkartr̥kō hi saḥ na punaḥ
tasya saḥ । yasya ca karma tadāśritamapi tasyaivēti yajamāna
ēvādhikriyatē । ēvaṁ cātmanēpadābhidhānamupapannaṁ bhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b939"/>
yatra ca punaḥ vacanādārtvijō'dhikāraḥ tatrānyadīyapadārthāśritēpi
guṇē vyāpr̥tasya phalaṁ bhavati iti kalpyatē ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 6 ।। 1mantrāścākarmakaraṇāstadvat ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīmāśīrmantrā udāharaṇam । kiṁ yājamāna utārtvijā
iti । ārtvijāssamākhyayēti prāptē brūmaḥ---liṅgādyājamānā iti ।
liṅgaṁ hi samākhyātō balīya ityuktam । prōṣitasamidādhānadarśanaṁ
ca liṅgam । nanu ca mama yajamānasyētyēvamādi liṅgamupapadyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b940"/>
ayamēva dōṣaḥ yadutādhyāhārō nāma । tasmādvak‍turēva mamētyupapannaṁ
bhavati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 7 ।। dva‍yāmnātēṣūbhau dva‍yāmnānasyārthavattvāt ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>kēcinmantrāḥ yājamānē cādhvaryanē cāmnātāḥ । tatra saṁśayaḥ kiṁ
dvābhyāṁ vaktavyāḥ utādhvaryuṇaivēti । kathaṁ punaḥ dva‍yāmnānāta dvābhyāṁ
ca samākhyātāḥ ēkēna vaktavyā iti । ēkakāryatvānmantrāṇā-
miti pūrvapakṣavādī ēkaprayōjyatāṁ manyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu
ēkasyānuṣṭhānasmaraṇādanyasya ca pratyavēkṣaṇāt āmnānadvayasyāpi
arthavattvāt dvābhyāmapi prayōktavyāḥ । samākhyādvayaṁ cānugr̥hītaṁ
bhaviṣyati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b941"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 8 ।। 1jñātē ca vacanaṁ na hyavidvān vihitō'sti ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>k‌lr̥ptīryajamānaṁ vācayatīti śrūyatē । kiṁ vidvānēva vācayi-
tavyaḥ utāvidvānapīti saṁśayēḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ viduṣō'dhikārasiddhēḥ
aviduṣō'dhikārāśaṅkā ? vācayatītyētasmādēva hi na viduṣō
vācayatīti dr̥ṣṭārthatā saṁbhavatīti । ēvaṁ tarhi aviduṣa ēva vācanaṁ
bhavatu । bhavatu kō dōṣaḥ ? viduṣō'dhikārahāniḥ prāpnōti ।
nādhikāraṁ nivārayāmaḥ aviduṣō'pyastīti । idaṁphalamidamadhi-
karaṇam । atrōcyatē---nādhikāramākṣēp‍tumidaṁ vacaḥ । bruvantamēva
hi vācayatīti bravīti । nābruvataḥ pravr̥ttimāha । viduṣaśca
﻿<pb n="b942"/>
prakr̥tyarthē pravr̥ttiḥ nāviduṣaḥ śrutaḥ । atō yathādhikāraṁ vācanamiti
siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 9 ।। 1yājamānē samākhyānāt karmāṇi yājamānāni syuḥ ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>iha dvandvānyudāharaṇam । kiṁ yajamānēna kartavyāni utādhva-
ryuṇēti saṁśayaḥ । ēkatra padārthāmnānāt । anyatra samabhyā-
śīkaraṇāt । tatra viśēṣasamākhyayā yājamānāni । padārtha-
pūrvakatvāt samabhyāśasya । atrōcyatē । padārthāstāvadādhvaryavā ēva
﻿<pb n="b943"/>
akriyamāṇē padārthē na yajamānēna samabhyāśaḥ śakyatē kartumiti
ādhvaryava ēva । viśēṣasamākhyāpravr̥ttistu darśitā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 10 ।। 1vipratiṣēdhē karaṇaḥ samavāyaviśēṣāt itaramanyaratēṣāṁ
yatō viśēṣaḥ syāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>r̥tvigantarakāryōpadēśē kimātmīyaṁ karma karōtu uta ati-
diṣṭamiti saṁśayē atidiṣṭaṁ pratyakṣavidhānāditi siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 11 ।। 2praiṣēṣu parādhikārāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>praiṣapraiṣārthau kimēkēna kartavyau uta dvābhyāmiti ।
﻿<pb n="b944"/>
prāptakālabhrāntyā ēkēnēti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । yuṣmadarthaparityāga-
kāraṇābhāvāditi rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 12 ।। 1adhvaryuśca darśanāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṁ kimadhvaryuḥ praiṣārthaṁ karōtu utānya iti saṁśayaḥ । artha-
vādadarśanādanya iti prāptam । mantraliṅgadarśanāt samākhyānārtha-
saṁbhavāccādhvaryuḥ । arthavādastu guṇavādēna parihr̥taḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b945"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 13 ।। 1r̥tvikphalaṁ karaṇērṣvathavattvāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarāśīrmantrairasya viśēṣaḥ ? samākhyātaḥ sthitē'dhvaryu-
kartr̥tvē agnyanvādhānasya śratyā mantravidhānam । na ca guṇānu-
rōdhēna pradhāna (kartr̥tva)bādhaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । tasmādādhvaryavō mantra
iti sthitē kasyāśīriti cintyatē । liṅgādadhvaryōḥ । vaktā hi
uttamapuruṣēṇa saṁbadhyatē । nanu karmasaṁbaddhaphalasaṅkīrtanāt karmārthatā
mantrāṇām । na । karmaprayuktayaśaḥ prakāśayataḥ upapannaiva karmārtha-
tēti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu yaścārthādarthō na sa
cōdanārtha iti manvānaḥ karmasaṁbaddhamēva phalaṁ prakāśayan mantraḥ
﻿<pb n="b946"/>
karmōrthō bhavati । yajamānasaṁbaddhamēva phalam । yajamānasya mamēti
mantrārthaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 14 ।। 1karmārthaṁ tu phalaṁ tēṣāṁ svāminaṁ pratyarthavattvāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra punaḥ dr̥ṣṭārthamēva tat kimr̥tvijāmēva uta atrāpi karma-
phalamēvēti । uk‍tēna nyāyēna karmaphalamēvēti vadāmaḥ । atrōcyatē ।
yaścārthādarthō na sa cōdanārtha iti anupakāramaṅgīkr̥tyaitaduktam । yat
punaḥ karmaṇa upakarōti tadupādānaśēṣatayā bhavatyēva karmārthamiti
nākarmārthatā mantrāṇām ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b947"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 15 ।। vyapadēśācca ।। 29 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra ca vyapadiśyata ēva tatra bhavatyēva phaladarśanam---tannau
sahēti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 16 ।। dravyasaṁskāraḥ prakaraṇaviśēṣāt ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>vēdirvēdidharmāścētyuktamuttaravivakṣayēti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 17 ।। nirdēśāt‍tu vikr̥tāpūrvasyānadhikāraḥ ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitamaṅgapradhānārthaṁ prakr̥tau barhiriti । vikr̥tāvidānīṁ
cintyatē---kimatrāpi aṅgapradhānārthē barhiṣi dharmā bhavanti
cōdakēna uta prākr̥takāryaprayukta ēvēti । tatra prakr̥tivadvikr̥tā-
vapōṁti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b948"/>
<p>rāddhāntavādī tu kāryamukhēnāṅgapradhānārthasaṁbandhitayā sāmānyēna
prakr̥tivadvikr̥tāviti dharmāṇāṁ vikr̥tau nirūpaṇam । na yathā
prakr̥tisaṁvandhitayā । saṁbandhasāmānyēna hi sarvatrōpadēśaḥ
syāt । tataścōhadarśanaṁ nōpapadyatē । tasmātsiddhaṁ na yūpabarhiṣi
dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ । añjanājyē na ājyadharmāḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 18 ।। 1virōdhē ca śrutiviśēṣādavyaktaḥ śēṣē ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>anēkatra śēṣabhāvō na nyāyyaḥ iti paribhōjanīyādanyat
kartavyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b949"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="33">।। 19 ।। 1ayanayastvēkadēśasya ।। 33 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvādhikaraṇanyāyēnānēkatra śēṣabhāvō na nyāyya iti manvānasya
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । dvayavadānōpasaṁhārāt pratipattēśca rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 20 ।। 2vikr̥tau sarvārthaḥ śēṣaḥ ।। 34 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṁ vikr̥tābupāṁśutvādayō dharmāścintyantē । kiṁ
tatrāpi prakr̥tivat aṅgapradhānārthatā dharmāṇāṁ uta nēti
saṁśayaḥ । prakr̥tivadaṅgapradhānārthatā dharmāṇāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b950"/>
naupadēśikātidēśikaiḥupadēśaḥ saṁbadhyata iti । upadēśāpēkṣa-
tvādatidēśasya sāpēkṣatvaṁ rāddhāntaḥ । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ na
saṁbadhyata iti ? upadēśāpēkṣatvādatidēśasya sāpēkṣanirapēkṣayōḥ
nirapēkṣaṁ balīya iti nyāyavidaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 21 ।। 1sannidhānaviśēṣādasaṁbhavē tadaṅgānām ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>śyēnē tvaupadēśikasaṁbandhābhāvāt ātidēśikairēva saṁbandha iti
viśēṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b951"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 22 ।। 1tatkālē vō liṅgadarśanāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṁ liṅgadarśanabhrāntyā sutyākālānāmēvātra vidhānamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । aviśēṣāt sarvēṣāmiti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 23 ।। māṁsa tu savanīyānām ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>tarasāḥ savanīyāḥ purōḍāśā bhavantīti । atra savanīya-
purōḍāśayōḥ vivakṣāyāṁ vākyabhēdaprasaṅgāt kasyāyathārthatvamiti ।
dr̥ṣṭavyabhicārāt purōḍāśasya ayathārthatvamiti rāddhāntitam ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ tr̥tīyādhyāyasya
aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b952"/>
﻿<pb n="b953"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1athātaḥ kratvarthapuruṣārthayōrjiṁjñāsā ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>kratvarthapuruṣārthayōrjijñāsā kimiti pr̥thak pratijñāyatē ?
aidamarthyalakṣaṇamēva hi śēṣatvam; śēṣaḥ parārthatvādityuktam । kratvartha-
tāpi tadantaḥpātinī pratijñātaivāthātaḥ śēṣalakṣaṇamityanēna ।
tasmāt punaḥ pratijñāyāḥ prayōjanaṁ na vidmaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b954"/>
<p>atha mataṁ na śrutyādibhiḥ puruṣārthatā'vagamyatē tasya lipsārtha-
lakṣaṇēti vakṣyati । kratvarthagrahaṇaṁ tarhi pratyuktam । na cēyamapi
puruṣārthatālakṣaṇā śakyatē vak‍tum । na ca śabdādr̥tē yāgaḥ svargārtha
iti jñānamutpadyatē । na ca tatsādhyaḥ svargaḥ puruṣārtha iti svatō'ya-
mapyasamādhiḥ । yadapi śrutyādīnāṁ saṅkīrtanaṁ tadapi kasmai prayōjanā-
yēti na vidmaḥ । śrutyādibhiśśēṣalakṣaṇaṁ nānyēna pramāṇēna । ataḥ
śēṣalakṣaṇamityētāvataiva tathā । tataḥ śrutyādisaṅkīrtanaṁ mandaprayō-
janamiva pratibhāti । yadapi kratvarthapuruṣārthayōḥ prayōjakāprayō-
jakādīnantarbhāvayan pratijñātān kathayati tadapyasamañjasa iva ।
kutaḥ ? antarbhāvō hi svarūpatō lakṣaṇataḥ kāryatō bhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b955"/>
trayamapyatra nāsti । svarūpaṁ tāvat pr̥thagabhidhānādēva bhinnam ।
lakṣaṇamapi svarūpabhēdādēva bhinnam । lakṣaṇabhēdādr̥tē na svarūpabhēdaḥ
kāryamapi yaddarśitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa tadayuktam । pradēśāntaraviruddha-
ścārthavādastāvat stutyarthaḥ prādhānyamapi upakāryōpakāranibandhanam ।
prayōjakamapi prayōjyaṁ prati prādhānyamātmanaḥ pratipādayati । na
punarātmanaḥ parārthatām । tadidaṁ rātriprayāṇamivādēśakaṁ bhāṣyaṁ
vyāmōhamupajanayati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b956"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---dvayamapyētad‏yuk‍taṁ bhēdōpanyāsō'ntarbhāvaśca yathā
tatra । yatpunaḥ tādarthyaṁ śēṣatvē hēturiti satsu śrutyādiṣu
tadityuktam । nanu caivaṁ sati kratvarthatā pratyuk‍tētyapyuktam ।
bhavēdētadēvaṁ yadi vainiyōgikamucyatē । iha tu upādānanibandhana-
mēva pratijānāti । kimupādānaṁ nāma ? niyōgākṣēpa upādānam ।
tatkr̥taṁ ca prōkṣaṇādēḥ kratvarthatvam । viniyōgāt punaḥ vrīhyarthataiva ।
﻿<pb n="b957"/>
bhēdārthapratijñānaṁ tarhi kimiti ? kimitivā'ntarbhāvaḥ । avagati
hētubhēdādbhēdaḥ upakārasāmānyādantarbhāvaḥ । prayōjakaḥ kaścit
puruṣārtha iti kaścid‌grahaṇaṁ kiñcitprayōjakasyāpyapuruṣārthatājñāpanārthaṁ
yathā---kasya ? ācāryakaraṇavidhēḥ svādhyāyasya ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1yasmin prītiḥ puruṣasya tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇāvibhak‍tatvāt ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p><q>“tasya lipsārthēnaiva bhavati na śās‍trēṇa”</q> iti viruddhamuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b958"/>
na śāstrādr̥tē svargaḥ sādhyatayā pratīyatē । kartr̥gāmitayā ca ।
saṁbandhaśāstramaṅgīkr̥tyaitaduktam । arthaśca niyōgasiddhiḥ taccōpādāna-
mityuktam । nanu ca kratvarthatāpyupādānēnaivōktā । viniyōgē-
satītyuktam । arthādēva hi puruṣārtha iti viśēṣaḥ ।
kimidamavibhāgāditi ? puruṣasya kratusaṁbandhāvibhāgādityarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b959"/>
ētacca ṣaṣṭhē nipuṇataramupapādayiṣyāmaḥ । pariśēṣādviniyōgē satīti
kratvarthatōktā bhavati ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ vā । nanu guṇaphalacōdanā ētā ityuktam । kō'yaṁ
punarvicāraḥ ? ucyatē---pradarśitamasmābhiḥ viniyōgatastaduktamiti ।
iha punarupādānatō dr̥ṣṭaprayōjanasaṁbhavāt nādr̥ṣṭaṁ prayōjanaṁ saṁbhavati
iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>na, yathāviniyōgaṁ kāryāvagatēḥ । viniyuktasyaiva hi kārya-
kalpanā nāviniyuktasyēti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b960"/>
<p>atō viniyōgataḥ upādānataśca puruṣārthataiva guṇaphalacōdanā-
sviti sthitam । bādarigrahaṇaṁ punarupakārapradarśanārtham । na punaḥ
parārthatvāditi śēṣahētunivr̥ttyartham । kathaṁ ? viniyōgē hi sa
uktaḥ । nanu bādariṇāpi viniyōga ēvāsāvupanyastaḥ । ata
ēvāsau nirākr̥taḥ । iha punaḥ kāryata ēvōpādānamityupanyastam ।
﻿<pb n="b961"/>
ayathāviniyōgatayā nirasyata ityavirōdhaḥ । ēvaṁ vā । iha
dravyārjananiyamā udāharaṇam । tatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । niyamaniyō
mānāmadhikāraśūnyatvāt kāmaśrutiniyōgēnaikavākyatvāt adhi-
kārasiddhēḥ । ēvaṁ ca kṣāmavatyādīnāmapi spaṣṭaiva karmārthatōpapannā bhavati
iti । tasmādanadhikāriṇē vidhērānarthakyaṁ mābhūditi kratvarthatā ।
nanu kratvarthatvē svatvamēva na bhavatīti yāga ēva na saṁvartētēti
pralapitamidaṁ kēnāpi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b962"/>
<p>ārjanaṁ svatvaṁ nāpādayatīti vipratiṣiddham । kathaṁ tarhi
kratvarthatā ? vanīvananavat tadarthaṁ svatvamityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---nēmē adhikāraśūnyā niyamavidhayaśśakyantē
vak‍tum । jīvanāya pravr̥ttā adhikr̥tā bhaviṣyanti ।
﻿<pb n="b963"/>
na ca śabdādēvādhikāraḥ adhikārādēva [hyadhikāraḥ] sa tu kvaci-
cchabdāvagamyaḥ kvacit pramāṇāntarāvagamyaḥ । ataḥ svatvasyā-
viśēṣāt sarvapuruṣārthanirvr̥ttau na viśēṣaśśakyatē'vadhārayitum ।</p>
<p>1api ca yadi śāstrāt karmārthaṁ dravyaṁ tannānyatra viniyujyēta,
tathā''rjitaṁ, tatra sarvatantraparilōpaḥ syāt2 । kō'rthaḥ ? kimidaṁ
tantram ? jīvanamiti cēt aniyamāttarhi jīviṣyati । niyamasya
kratvarthatvāt । atha kratvantarāṇi tantraśabdābhidhēyānyabhiprētāni
tathāpi pratikratu niyamānna lōpaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---kratvantarāṇyēva tantraśabdābhidhēyānyabhiprētāni ।
﻿<pb n="b964"/>
nacārjanasya viśēṣōpādānatvē pramāṇamasti । na ca sarvatantraṁ sarvēṇa
dravyēṇa śakyatē kartuṁ iti tantraparilōpaḥ sarvakarmaṇām, ayaṁ
cāparō dōṣaḥ nānyasya tantrē pratatē anyattantraṁ pratāyatē iti darśanaṁ
nōpapadyatē । atha naivēdaṁ kasyacidēkasyāṅgamiti । ēvaṁ tarhi naivēdaṁ
prayōgavacanēna gr̥hyatē, anupāttaprayōgavacanasyāṅgataiva nāsti ।
asatyaṅgatvē yasya kila aṅgatā nāsti tasyāprayōgēṇānupa-
kārakatvamiti sō'yamaṅgatā'bhāva ēvānupakārakatvēna darśitaḥ1 ।
﻿<pb n="b965"/>
na cādhānavadbhavitumarhati । na ca dravyārthamēvēdamārjanaṁ ādhāna-
vadagnyarthamēva bhavitumarhati, jīvanāya pravr̥ttasyādhikārāvagamāt ।
ataḥ puruṣārthamēvēdamārjanam । tasmāt kratvarthatvē tantraparilōpaḥ
sthitō dōṣaḥ । kṣāmavatyādīnāmāhitāgnēradhikārāvagamāt bhavatu
kratvarthatā phalaṁ kalpayitum । puruṣārtha ēva vā naimittikō'stu ।
tasmāt puruṣārthā dravyārjananiyamā iti sthitam । atō niya-
mātikramaḥ puruṣasyānarthaḥ na kratōḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">।। 3 ।। tadutsargē karmaṇi puruṣārthāya śāstrasyānatiśaṅkyatvāt
na ca dravyaṁ cikīrṣyatē tēnārthēnībhisambandhāt kriyāyāṁ puruṣaśrutiḥ ।। 3 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b966"/>
<p>yasmin prītiḥ puruṣasya tasya lipsā arthalakṣaṇētyuktam ।
iha tu prītēraśravaṇāt arthataśca śravaṇādanavagamāt adhikāri-
śūnyatā vidhēḥ । na cānadhikāraṁ puruṣārthaṁ bhavati iti tasya kratvartha-
syaivēkṣaṇasyāyaṁ pratiṣēdhaḥ niyamō vā । atrābhidhīyatē---prītyu-
tsargēpyētaduktam । adhikārāśravaṇēpi adhikārō yuktaḥ kalpayitum
na punaḥ kratusaṁbandhakalpanā । kaḥ punaratra viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti
viśēṣaḥ । yathaivādhikārē śrūyamāṇē gamyamānatatkartr̥taiva nyāyyā ।
﻿<pb n="b967"/>
ēvaṁ gamyamānakartravagamāt adhikārakalpanaiva nyāyyā । kathaṁ tarhi
kartradhikaraṇam ? tatra hi viniyōgō'dhikārakalpanāyāḥ
pratipakṣaḥ । iha tu apratipakṣā'dhikārakalpanēti । kiṁ bhūtaḥ
punaratrādhikriyatē ? <q>“ētāvatā hainasā viyuktō bhavati”</q> iti
śravaṇāt jīvata ēva vā'dhikāraḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b968"/>
<p>atō nityō'yaṁ jauvanānupālanīyō niyamaḥ svadharmatayā । nanu
ca prasajyapratiṣēdhō nyāyyaḥ । satyam, tasya vratamityanvayāvagatē-
rlakṣaṇaiva nyāyyā । ādhānavadapyatra naiva dravyārthatā saṁbhavati ।
aviniyuktadravyasaṁyōgāt । dr̥ṣṭasya ca saṁskārasyāvidyamānatvāt ।
kiṁ dr̥ṣṭārthatā śakyatē vak‍tum ? bāḍhaṁ śakyatē darpaṇapramārjanavat
lōka ēvōpayōgadarśanāt । tasmāt puruṣārthō niyam iti yuktam ।
dr̥ṣṭārthāsaṁbhavēna ca karkarīkarṇādayō'pi puruṣārthā ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b969"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 4 ।। dravyōṇi tvaviśēṣēṇānarthakyāt pradīyēran ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>uktaṁ <q>‘spha‍yaśca kapālāni ca’</q> <q>‘spha‍yēnōddhanti’</q> ityētayōḥ
kiṁ viniyōjakamiti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī <q>“spha‍yēnōddhanti”</q>
ityēvamādibhirvākyaiḥ sākṣāt yajñasaṁbandhānavagamāt yajñā-
yudhānīti vidhyantaraṁ manyatē । nanu vājapēyasya yūpa itivat
praṇāḍyāpi saṁbandha upapadyatē । yuktaṁ yūpābhāvātkratōstatra ।
﻿<pb n="b970"/>
iha punaḥ kiṁ nōpapadyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē---yajñā-
yudhānīti tāvat lakṣaṇā । lakṣaṇā cēt sākṣādva‍yavadhānē ca na
kaścidviśēṣa pramāṇāntarānusāriṇī hi lakṣaṇā । na ca vidyamānē
pramāṇē pramāṇāntarakalpanā śakyā । spha‍yēnōddhantītyubhaya
siddhatvāt । ēvaṁ ca vikalpadōṣaḥ parihr̥tō bhavati । liṅgaṁ cāpyupapannaṁ
bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b971"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">।। 5 ।। tatra caikatvamayajñāṅgamarthasya guṇabhūtatvāt ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>ēkatvaṁ viniyōgābhāvānna yajñāṅgamiti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhi-
prāyaḥ । kathaṁ punarēkatvaṁ na viniyujyatē ? vibhaktayō hi prāti-
padikārthasya svārthasaṁbandhamabhidadhati । tasmādēkatvaṁ karaṇatvaṁ ca
prātipadikārthasyaiva । naikatvasya karaṇabhāvaḥ । karaṇasaṁbandhē sati
prātipadikārthasaṁbandhō na syāt । yathā <q>‘arūṇayā’</q> iti na
dravyēṇa ataḥ pratīyamānamapyētanna kriyayā saṁbadhyatē yathā pūrvō
dhāvatītyaparapratyayaḥ । liṅgadarśanāni caivamupapannāni bhavanti ।
ēvaṁ prāptē ucyatē---na viniyōgādēva kriyāṅgatā, kiṁ tarhi ?
﻿<pb n="b972"/>
upādānādapi hi śēṣatābhavati । yathaiva hi karaṇībhūtasyai-
vōpādānaṁ ēvamēkatvayuktasyāpi । na hyakārakasyōpādānamasaṅkhyā-
yuktasyāpi saṁbhavati । tathā ca laukikāḥ gāmānayētyēvamādiṣu
tathaiva pratipadyantē । tadidamuktaṁ <q>“na śrutirbrūtē (pramitē)
vākyārthō nāsti”</q> iti1 । na viniyōgō brūtē upādānaṁ
nāstītyarthaḥ । nanu <q>‘na śrutirbrūtē vākyārthō nāsti’</q> iti
anya ēvārthaḥ pratīyatē । kō'rthaḥ ? ayamarthaḥ pratīyatē ।
na śrutyā vākyārthasya virōdhō'stīti । śrutyarthāparityāgēna
vākyāt kratvarthatāvagamyatē । virōdhē na daurbalyamuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b973"/>
uktamasmābhiḥ viniyōgō na saṁbhavatīti karaṇasyēvaikatvasyēti ।
kathaṁ tarhi vākyaśabdaḥ ? samabhivyāhāraparyāyō'yaṁ na viniyō-
jakaparyāyaḥ । tasmātsiddhamupādānataḥ śēṣatvaṁ saṅkhyāyā liṅgasya
ca । ēvaṁ darśanānyupapannāni pūrvapakṣadarśanaṁ cānuvādaḥ ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ vā । liṅgādhikaraṇam punaḥ ēvaṁ vēti
vadataḥ kō'bhiprāyaḥ aparicchēdakatvaṁ liṅgasya pūrvapakṣavādī
manyatē । paricchēdikā hi saṅkhyā dravyasya parimāṇamācaṣṭē
﻿<pb n="b974"/>
śravaṇāviśēṣālliṅgamapyupādīyata iti rāddhāntaḥ । nanu cāpari-
māṇāpādakatvālliṅgaṁ nōpādātavyamityuktam । nātra parimāṇa-
mupādānē upayujyatē । viśēṣaniṣṭhatvādupādānasya । yathā'nuṣṭhāna-
viśēṣākāṅkṣā tathā kārakaviśēṣākāṅkṣāpi । atassaṅkhyāvadupādāna-
miti siddham । śēṣaṁ pūrvavat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 7 ।। 1āśrayiṣvaviśēṣēṇa bhāvō'rthaḥ pratīyēta ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>ihāśrayiṇaḥ padārthā udāharaṇam । nanu bhāṣyamayuktaṁ
kiṁ yajimātraṁ saṁskārō dēvatāyā uta yajinā'dr̥ṣṭaṁ
dēvatāyāṁ kriyata iti yasmātsaṁskāramātramadr̥ṣṭa[ma]kurvadanarthakam ।
﻿<pb n="b975"/>
dvividhamākhyātamuk‍taṁ paraprāptaniyōgānuvādakam । avahantītyāg‍nē-
yādicōdanāvagataniyōgānuvādakaṁ svaniyōgasaṁbandhitayā'dhikāra-
sādhanaṁ ca । ihēdānīṁ sandihyatē---kiṁ paraprāptaniyōgānuvādātmakaṁ
uta svaniyōgasaṁbandhitayādhikārasādhanamiti । kutaḥ saṁśayaḥ ?
aṁśēna dr̥ṣṭasya saṁbhavaḥ aṁśēnādr̥ṣṭasyēti pūrvapakṣavādī dr̥ṣṭē
saṁbhavatyadr̥ṣṭakalpanā na nyāyyēti paraprāptānuvādaṁ manyatē । nanu
yajyarthō'tra na niṣpadyatē । anuṣṭhānād‌dr̥ṣṭōpapattyarthō
('dr̥ṣṭō)bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---dr̥ṣṭōpapattyarthataiva
na ghaṭatē । kasmāt ? niyōgasiddhēravivakṣitatvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b976"/>
niyōgāddhi niyōgārthē pravr̥ttiḥ । atha tadarthamutpattiniyōgō
vivakṣyatē siddhamapūrvārthatvam । paścādadhikāraniyōgārthatvē yāgasya
---nirūpaḍhē'ṅgasaṁbandhē sati tad‌dvārēṇa dravyadēvatāgatadr̥ṣṭasaṁskāraniṣpa-
ttyarthamityanumanyata ēva । na ca tr̥tīyaprakārō'yaṁ niyōganiṣpattē-
stulyatvāt samidādivat । prayōjanaṁ tu dr̥ṣṭamadr̥ṣṭaṁ vā bhavatu ।
prayōjanavaśācca anuṣṭhānamananuṣṭhānaṁ vā bhavatu । sarvathā sidhyati
svaniyōgārthatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b977"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 8 ।। 1arthē samavaiṣamyamatō dravyakarmaṇām ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘atikrāntastr̥tīyaviṣayaḥ’</q> iti । kō'yaṁ tr̥tīyaviṣayaḥ ?
pārārthyapratipattiḥ । sā'tikrāntā । idānīṁ punaḥ sthitē pārārthyē
kēvalamupādānamēva cintyatē kēna prayōjanēnōpādānaṁ kēna nēti ।
nanu ca prāgapyasmāt prayōjanakr̥taivōpādānacintā । kēna viśēṣēṇa-
damucyatē idamidānīmiti । satyaṁ---kintu pārārthyamapi tannimitta-
kamēva, na (vi)niyōganimittakam । ata idamuk‍taṁ tr̥tīyaviṣaya
iti । tr̥tīyasyāyaṁ viṣayaḥ na punaḥ tārtīyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ śakyatē-
'vagantum । atō vidhinimittakamēvāsya pārārthyamiti caturthē
cintitam । ētacca vyākhyātam---na śrutyādibhiḥ sarvasya
﻿<pb n="b978"/>
pārārthyaṁ śakyatē pratipādayitumiti । ētadēvātra kathyatē । tathā ca
yāgaphalayōradhikārāt pārārthyaṁ vakṣyati । ata ēva vādarērēṣā
bhrāntiḥ dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣvēva śēṣatvamiti । śrutyādīnāṁ tatra
dravyādau saṁbhavāt upādānādhikārayōḥ sāmarthyamapaśyatō'va-
dhāraṇāt । ata ēvēdaṁ lakṣaṇāntaramucyatē śēṣāvagamatulyatvēpi ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 9 ।। ēkaniṣpattēḥ sarvaṁ samaṁ syāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>ataḥ prabhr̥tīdānīṁ kēvalōpādānavyāpāra ēva cintyatē ।
śēṣatā tu viniyōgata ēva । nōpādānataḥ । pūrva-
pakṣavādī tu kēvalōpakāradarśanādēvōpādānamāha, na śēṣatā-
'pēkṣaṇīyēti manyatē । yathaivōpādānaśēṣēṣu paś‍vēkatvādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="b979"/>
tasmādubhayaṁ prayōjakamiti । atrābhidhīyatē---nātra prayōjakatvaṁ
vājinasya । kutaḥ ? śēṣabhūtasya hi prayōjanākāṅkṣā । sā ca
yasya śēṣabhūtā tēnaiva prayōjanēna nivr̥ttērna prayōjanāntaraṁ prayōja-
katvēnāpēkṣatē । kathaṁ tarhi aśēṣabhūtasyōpādānaśēṣatvaṁ, ēkatvādēḥ
aśēṣabhūtasya prayōjanākāṅkṣaiva nāstīti । aśēṣatvē upādāna-
syaivānupapattēḥ । atrōcyatē---śēṣasyāvagamāt anyathānavagamāt
avagamapūrvakatvāccōpādānasya । kiṁ ca śēṣabhūtasya prayōjyatvānya-
thānupapattēḥ । na hyanavacchinnamupādātuṁ śakyata ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b980"/>
yatpunarna śēṣabhūtaṁ na ca śēṣasthamavagamyatē na śēṣōpādānēnā-
pēkṣyatē na tat prayōjyaṁ bhavitumarhati । yathā na dadhyānayanaṁ
na vājinaśēṣabhūtaṁ tathā pradarśitaṁ bhāṣyē । tathā ca liṅgaṁ
pradarśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 10 ।। padakarmāprayōjakaṁ nayanasya parārthatvāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarādhastyēnādhikaraṇēnāsya viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti
viśēṣaḥ tatra hi dadhyānayanaṁ āmikṣānirvr̥ttisamakālamēva
vājinamanuniṣpādayati । atō yuk‍taṁ vājinaniṣpattēḥ na
kāraṇāntarāpēkṣā । iha punaḥ saptamaṁ padaṁ ityuk‍tē bhavatyā-
kāṅkṣā kasyēti । prakr̥tatvādēkahāyanyā iti gamyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b981"/>
tasmādubhayārthāmēkahāyanīṁ manyatē । ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē---satyaṁ
yadi kasyētyākāṅkṣōpapadyatē anirjñātasaṁbandhāntarē saṁbandhinyu-
padiśyamānē bhavatyākāṅkṣāpūrvikā prajñā । yatra punassaṁbandhyantarapūrvaka
ēvōpadēśaḥ । tatra yathānirjñātasaṁbandhipurassara ēvōpadēśaḥ iti
darśitamaśvapratigrahē । ataḥ krayārthaivaikahāyanī saptamapadasaṁbandhinīti na
prayujyatē । atra bhāṣyam---<q>‘prasaṅgamupajīvatā’</q> iti । nanu cēdaṁ prayōjana-
lakṣaṇam । kaḥ prasaṅgasyāvasaraḥ ? vidyamānē hi prayōjakatvē prasaṅga
uktaḥ । iha tu prayōk‍tr̥taiva nāstīti । ucyatē---śās‍traprasaṅga-
maṅgīkr̥tyaitaduktam । na prayōgaprasaṅgamityadōṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b982"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 11 ।। 1arthābhidhānakarma ca bhaviṣyatā saṁyōgasya tannimittatvāt
tadarthō hi vidhīyatē ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘purōḍāśakapālēna tuṣānupavapati’</q> iti nātra śāstra-
prasaṅgaḥ saṁbhavatīti prayōk‍tr̥tvaṁ pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē
tuṣōpavāpasyāpi na ca nāntarīyakaḥ śakya upavāpō vak‍tum
vājinavat । tasmādubhayaṁ prayōjakamiti । atrābhidhīyatē
---satyaṁ viniyōgē nāsti śāstraprasaṅgaḥ । nāpi nāntarīyaka-
﻿<pb n="b983"/>
bhāvaḥ । kintūpāttasyāyaṁ viniyōga iti nōpādānakalpa-
nā kramatē । tadidamuktam---<q>“bhaviṣyatā saṁbandhō'yaṁ na bhūtavartamānā-
bhyāṁ”</q> iti । yadi punaḥ bhūtavartamānābhyāṁ saṁbandhaḥ kimupādānaṁ
syāt ? ucyatē---na bhūtasya, tasya bhaviṣyadarthatayā anupātta-
syaiva pālanaṁ bhaviṣyati । pālanabhūtamēvōpādānaṁ yataḥ । vartamāna-
syāpi yaḥ saṁbandhī tasyānyatra viniyōgō na saṁbhavatītyarthādanya-
dupādēyam । bhaviṣyadarthatvē punaḥ anyārthamēvōpāttasya viniyōgaḥ
saṁbhavatīti siddhamaprayōjakatvam । tuṣōpavāpastu kartavyō na
kartavya iti nāsyādhikaraṇasyāyaṁ viṣayaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b984"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 12 ।। paśāvanālambhāllōhitaśakr̥tōrakarmatvam ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>āsminnadhikaraṇē hr̥dayādyavadānavacanaṁ lōhitaśakr̥tsaṁpravyādha---
vacanaṁ ca tulyam । prakr̥tapaśuviṣayatayā <q>‘agnīṣōmīyaṁ paśumālabhēta’</q>
iti dvayōrapi prayōjakatāṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---<q>‘hr̥dayasyāgrē'vadyapi’</q> iti yāgō-
pasaṁhr̥tiriyam । aṅgaistr̥tīyasavana iti śravaṇāt ।
﻿<pb n="b985"/>
śakr̥tsaṁpravyādhastu tāvanmātraparyavasāyitvāt prakr̥tāśrayatvācca ।
pratipattiśca na prayōjikā । na pratipādyaṁ pratipattyarthamupādīyata
iti nyāyāt । atō na prayōjakaṁ paśōḥ śakr̥tādīti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 13 ।। ēkadēśadravyaṁ cōtpattau vidyamānasaṁyōgāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātraṁ pūrvapakṣa ēva nōpapadyatē । upāttadravyaviṣayatvāt
iśukhaṇḍavacchēṣāvagatēḥ । satyamēvaṁ, kintvatra purōḍāśasyānyārtha-
tvāt nānyatra kāryāntarē viniyōga upapadyata iti ।
﻿<pb n="b986"/>
atō dravyāntaramupādēyamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu
na dva‍yavadānamātrōpasaṁhāraḥ dvayavadānamātrēṇaivāg‍nēyayāganirvr̥ttimupa-
saṁhāramanyatra viniyōgōpapattyarthamuktavān । yadyanyasmai dīyatē
dīyamānaṁ hi tadā saṁpradānārthamiti tannōpapadyatē । tasmānna yāga-
kāryādanyatra viniyōgassaṁbhavati । yāgakāryatayā punaḥ nānyārthatā
śakyatē vak‍tum । atō nāg‍nēyādicōdanāyā virōṁdhaḥ । tasmāda-
pratipakṣēkṣukhaṇḍanyāyēnānupādānaṁ siddham śēṣadarśanāt tathā samava-
dānaśrutirityuktaṁ bhāṣyē ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n=" ">।। 14 ।। 1abhidhāraṇē viprakarṣādanuyājavatpātrabhēdaḥ syāt ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b987"/>
<p>kiṁ punaḥ purōḍāśakapālēnātra viśiṣyatē ? dravyōpādānaṁ
tāvat tadvannāstīti sthitamēva । dhāraṇasya tūpādānaṁ haviṣaḥ
prādhānyānnānyārthatayā virudhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । kathaṁ
punaḥ haviṣaḥ prādhānyaṁ dvitīyāśravaṇādabhidhāraṇasya tadarthatvāt
prayājaśēṣasya ca purōḍāśakapālavat tadarthatvāt ।
siddhāntastu na prādhānyaṁ haviṣāṁ dr̥ṣṭārthatayā''jyasyaivēti yuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b988"/>
tasmāt pratipattirēvēyaṁ prayājaśēṣasyēti । kathaṁ tarhi havīṁṣya-
bhidhārayatīti bahuvacanaṁ ēkēna haviṣā'bhidhāraṇanirvr̥ttēḥ । agr̥-
hyamāṇaviśēṣatvāt bahuvacanamaviruddham । atō dravyōpādānavat
dhāraṇōpādānamapi na yuk‍taṁ sannihita ēva haviṣi pratipattisiddhēḥ
iti ।</p>
<p>nanu dvitīyātr̥tīyayōranyārthatā grahītuṁ na śakyā yathārthatayāpi
vacanāvirōdhāt । satyaṁ, yadyavirōdhī vacanasya syāt । iha tu
﻿<pb n="b989"/>
prayājaśēṣaśabdēna virudhyatē pratipat‍tau punaḥ nāyaṁ virōdha iti
prātipadikārthānurōdhinī guṇabhūtārthavādinī vibhaktiriti yuktam ।
atrāpyanyārthataiva nyāyyā dvayōḥ karmaṇōrēkasmin vākyē saṁbandhānu-
guṇaḥ saptamyarthō draṣṭavyaḥ । darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 15 ।। 1samānayanaṁ tu mukhyaṁ syālliṅgadarśanāt ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘atihāyēḍō barhiḥ prati samānayatē’</q>
ityatra sandēhaḥ---kimuparitanaprayājadvayārthamēvēdaṁ samānayanaṁ
﻿<pb n="b990"/>
tattaścaupabhr̥tasyājyasya prayājānūyājārthasya taddharbhāṇāṁ ca prayōjakam ।
uta miśrīkaraṇārthamēvēdaṁ jauhavasaṁskārārtham । tataśca paraprayukta-
dravyasādhyatvāt aprayōjakamājyasya dharmāṇāṁ cēti । tatra pūrva-
pakṣavādī samānayanamātraśravaṇāt miśrīkaraṇamātraṁ manyatē । aṣṭā-
vupabhr̥ti gr̥hṇātīti ca sarvaprayājārthatāṁ manyatē । kutaḥ ?
viśēṣāśravaṇāt । tasmādadr̥ṣṭārthamēvēdaṁ samānayanamiti ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē---prayājadvayasādhanārthamēvēdaṁ samānayanam ।
kutaḥ ? ēvaṁ dr̥ṣṭārthatā samānayanasya bhavatiupabhr̥ti ca
prayājārthasya grahaṇasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b991"/>
<p>nunu cāviśēṣēṇa tadaupabhr̥taṁ sarvārthaṁ śrūyatē । śrutānu-
sārēṇa cādr̥ṣṭārthatā nyāyyā । nāviśēṣaśrutiḥ sāmarthyēna viśēṣē-
'vasthāpyamānā śabdārthatāṁ jahāti । tasmāt śabdasyāpratirōdhi---
tvāt dr̥ṣṭē saṁbhavati adr̥ṣṭakalpanā na nyāyyēti rāddhāntadarśana-
muktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 16 ।। tatrōtpattiravibhaktā syāt ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ubhayamubhayārthamiti
vadataḥ iti । ayamabhiprāyaḥ aviśēṣēṇa śravaṇāt---caturjuhvāṁ
gr̥hṇātīti, viśēṣataśca kāryasiddhēḥ prayājagrahaṇamanūyāja-
vannityānuvādaṁ manyatē jauhavē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b992"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---yadyupādānata ēva prāptiḥ syāt syādētadēvaṁ
upādānamātrādubhayārthatāpratītēḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi anūyājamātrārtha-
mēvaupabhr̥taṁ bhavatu । kēvalānūyājārthaśravaṇāt । ucyatē---prāptārtha-
tvādasya viniyōjakasya kēvalānūyājasaṁbandhinō'nuvādaṁ manyatē ।
kutaḥ prāptiḥ ? prayājānūyājabhyastadgr̥hṇātītyubhayārthatvāt ।</p>
<p>nanu samānayanādhikaraṇē sthitē kathamidānīmāśaṅkyatē । tatra
hi uparitanaprayājārthamaupabhr̥taṁ samānīyata iti vadatā ubhayārthatva-
muktam । kathaṁ kēvalānūyājārthatā āśaṅkyatē । ucyatē---sthitē
ētasmin tadbhavati anyathā'dr̥ṣṭārthamēva samānayanaṁ saṁskāramātraṁ
syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b993"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="46">।। 17 ।। 1tadaṣṭasaṅkhyaṁ syāt ।। 46 ।।</ab>
<p>aṣṭāvupabhr̥ti gr̥hṇāti iti śrūyatē । atra saṁśayaḥ kiṁ dvē
ētē caturgr̥hītē utāṣṭagr̥hītamēkamēvēdamiti । nanu samānayanādhi-
karaṇa idamuktam dvauṁ prayājau yaṣ‍ṭumēkamidaṁ caturgr̥hītaṁ samānīyata
iti । kayā yuktyā ? ēvaṁ ca dr̥ṣṭārthatā bhaviṣyatītyanayā yuktyētyarthaḥ ।
tadēvēdamākṣipyatē । aṣṭasaṁṅkhyāśravaṇāt । dr̥ṣṭārthatā ca samānayana-
syōpapadyata ēva āghārē prācīnē prayājatrayē ca vyāpr̥tasya jauhavasyā-
jyasya svakāryaṁ pratyaśak‍tasyānugrahāya samānīyata iti । atō'tra
﻿<pb n="b994"/>
pūrvapakṣavādī śrutatvādaṣṭasaṅkhyākamēva grahaṇamiti manyatē ।
rāddhāntastu bhinnaviṣayatvāt catussaṅkhyāṣṭasaṅkhyayōḥ nānya-
tarasyāprāptiḥ śakyatē varṇayitum avirōdhāt । kathaṁ punaraṣṭasaṁkhyā
catussaṅkhyāṁ niṣyādayati hōmē ? yasmād‍dvē ētē caturgr̥hītē saṁyō-
ginī, prayājānūyājēbhya ityubhayārthatvēna viniyōgāt । ubhayōśca
dvābhyāṁ caturgr̥hītābhyāṁ prayōjanamaṣṭagrahaṇēna saṁpādyatē aṣṭāvupabhr̥ti
gr̥hṇātīti । dvē ētē caturgr̥hītē iti darśanaṁ ca pūrvavat samarthitaṁ
bhavati । catugr̥hītānyājyāni bhavantīti hētuvannigadaśca
samarthitō bhavati ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ caturthādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b995"/>
﻿<pb n="b996"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। svarustvanēkaniṣpattiḥ svakarmaśabdatvāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>ēkamatrādhikaraṇaṁ vākyāntarābhiprāyēṇa varṇitam । dvitīya-
ntvēkavākyamaṅgīkr̥tya । yuktayaścaikavākyavicārē vākyāntarā-
pēkṣiṇyāṁ ca mīmāṁsāyāṁ tulyā iti pradarśitam । yuktiśca
śrutyā vidhānam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b997"/>
﻿<pb n="b998"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 2 ।। śākhāyāṁ tatpradhānatvāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamasmin prayōjakāprayōjakalakṣaṇē ?
nātra vidhitaḥ pūrvapakṣō rāddhāntō vā'vagamyatē ।
atrōcyatē---vidhita ēvēyaṁ cintā । kiṁ vr̥kṣaprāgdē-
śāt śākhōpādānamuta vihāraprāgdēśādānayanōpādānamiti ।
﻿<pb n="b999"/>
viniyōgavadabhidhānamanuvartatē upādānamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu---aparihāryalakṣaṇamidamābhidhānamiti śākhaivōpādēyā
prācīnānayanamēva dēśaviśiṣṭam । ayaṁ cāparō viśēṣaḥ ।
avaśyōpalakṣayitabyā śākhā pakṣadvayēpītyayamēva pakṣō nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 2 ।। śākhāyāṁ tatpradhānatvāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>atra parivāsanōpādānaṁ śākhōpādānaṁ vā cintyatē, avi-
﻿<pb n="b1000"/>
śēṣāt । kiṁ punaratra yuktam ? ubhayaṁ parivāsanasya
prayōjakaṁ mūlamagraṁ ca dvayōrapi śākhābhidhānatvāt । nanu
ca kriyādvayamatra śrūyatē parivāsayati karōti iti ca ।
tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tataḥ bhavati । śākhāparivāsanasya karma
karōtērupavēṣaḥ । tasmānnōpavēṣaḥ karmakārakasya prayōktā । ucyatē
---śākhāśabdaḥ samūlamagramācaṣṭa ityuktamasmābhiḥ । tatra mūlamupavēṣaṁ
karōti । agramapi kāryāntarē viniyuktamiti dvayōḥ prayōjakatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b1001"/>
atrōcyatē---syādētadēvaṁ yadi mūlamupavēṣaṁ karōtīti saṁbandhaḥ । kathaṁ
tarhi saṁbandhaḥ ? upavēṣaṁ karōtīti mūlata iti । kimatō yadyēvaṁ ?
ētadatō bhavati । anyatō niṣpannānmūlādupavēṣa iti । tasmāt
yadyapi samūlamagraṁ śākhāśabdēnōcyatē tathāpi na parivāsanamupa-
vēṣārthaṁ iti siddham ।</p>
<p>kiṁ ca śākhāśabdābhidhānaṁ ca kāryāntarēṣu agra
ēva prayuk‍taṁ śākhayā vatsānapākarōti iti । atō viniyō-
gāta mūlaparivāsanārthō'yamagrē śākhāśabdaḥ prayukta iti ।
﻿<pb n="b1002"/>
tasmānnōpavēṣaḥ prayōjakaḥ । prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 3 ।। 1haraṇē tu juhōtiryōgasāmānyāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cēdaṁ haraṇaṁ prastarapratipattyarthamēva; yadyapi haratiḥ yajatyarthō
māntravarṇikō dēvatāvidhiḥ tathāpi pratipattikarmaivaitat yathōttamaḥ
prayājaḥ । pratipattau ca na dravyasya guṇabhāvaḥ । nanu ca yathōttamaprayājē
ājyaṁ pratipattāvapi guṇabhūtaṁ tathātra śākhāpi bhaviṣyatīti cēt ।
﻿<pb n="b1003"/>
naivam । dravyasyātra pratipattiḥ । tatra punardēvatāsmaraṇārthō
yāga iti yuktō dravyasya guṇabhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu cōttamaprayājō naiva pratipattiḥ dravyaṁ hi yatra pratipādyatē
tatpratipattikarma । kēnēdamuk‍taṁ kārakārthō yō yāgaḥ pratipattikarmē-
tyucyatē kvaciddēśavirēcanāt saṁskāraḥ, kvacit smaraṇamiti ।
prayōjanaviśēṣā hyētē । atō na śākhā guṇabhūtēti śakyatē pūrva-
pakṣayitum । ucyatē---pratipattāvēva tr̥tīyāśravaṇāt guṇabhāvaṁ pūrva-
pakṣavādī manyatē, nāvaśyaṁ pratipattau sarvamēva pradhānaṁ bhavati । yadyathā
śrūyatē tattathaiva bhavitumarhati yathā juhvā juhōtīti guṇabhūtaiva juhūḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1004"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । bhavēdētadēvaṁ yadyatra sahaśabdō na śrūyatē ।
sahaśabdaśravaṇē tu tulyayōgitvaṁ prastarēṇa saha śākhāyā avagamyatē ।
tasmācchākhāpi pratipādyata ēva । anyathā hi tulyayōgō na syāt ।
ataśśākhāyāmapi dvitīyārtha ēva prastaravad‌draṣṭavyaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi
tr̥tīyā ? na cēyaṁ kārakalakṣaṇā kiṁ tarhi sahayōgalakṣaṇārthā ।
prasiddhēna ca sahayōgō lakṣyata iti vibhaktivyatyaya uktaḥ ।
prasiddhatvāt prastarasya praharaṇē । śēṣamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1005"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 5 ।। 1utpattyasaṁyōgātpraṇītānāmājyavadvibhāgaḥ syāt ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>apaḥ praṇayatīti kāryadvayāsaṁbandhamapāṁ praṇayanamutpannam ।
paścātkāryadvayaṁ śrutamityaviśēṣēṇa dvayōḥ prayōk‍tr̥tāṁ manyatē । nanu
ca <q>‘apō ninayati’</q> iti dvitīyā śrūyatē । anīpsitatvāt
kārakamātrē bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ । atōcyatē---nānīpsitatvē
hēturasti । kr̥taprayōjanamapi hi tat pratipādyatayā iṣyata ēva ।
﻿<pb n="b1006"/>
na cēpsitē saṁbhavati anīpsitāśrayaṇamupapadyatē tatpurassarā-
vagatēḥ । tasmāt saṁyavanē kr̥tārthānāmapāṁ pratipattirēva ninayanam ।
iti siddhamaprayōk‍tr̥tvam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 6 ।। 1prāsanavanmaitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍapradānaṁ kr̥tārthatvāt ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṁ prayacchatīti pratipattirapāmivēti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
nanu ca karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa sampradānamiti siddhō guṇabhāvaḥ
﻿<pb n="b1007"/>
sasaṁpradānakē karmaṇi । sampradānagaprītyutpādakatayaiva karmaṇō
guṇabhāvaḥ na punaḥ karmāntarasādhyatayā karmabhāvānupapattēḥ । kathaṁ
tarhi <q>‘daṇḍī praiṣānanvāha’</q> ityādidarśanam saṁpradānē yadr̥cchayā
prāptasyāyamanuvādaḥ ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṁ iti vyapadēśāt daṇḍī
praiṣānanvāha ityēvamādi ca darśanāt । arthakarmaivēdaṁ na pratipattiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1008"/>
nanu ca yadr̥cchayā prāptasyāyamanuvāda ityuktam । ayamēva dōṣaḥ
pākṣikatvaprasaṅgāt । kathaṁ tarhi dvitīyā ? tathā yuk‍taṁ cānīpsita-
mityuktam । tadayuktamiva pratibhāti । anupādēyaṁ hi tatrōdā-
haraṇam ahiṁ laṅghayati iti । tathā ca sak‍tuṣu vibhaktivyatyaya
uktaḥ upādēyatvādanīpsitatvaṁ na bhavatīti । ucyatē---suṣṭhūk‍taṁ
sak‍tuṣu hōmārthaṁ tatrōpādānam । iha tu na prayacchatyarthamupādānaṁ
upāttamēva hi prayacchatīti । atastathāyuktamēvēdaṁ karmēti śakyatē
vak‍tum nēpsitatamam । nāpi vibhaktyantarayōgyam tasmādartha-
karmēti sūktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1009"/>
<p>kiṁ punaratra dhāraṇamēva prayujyatē utōtpat‍tipīti cintāntara-
mētat । asti tāvat prayōk‍tr̥tvamiti rāddhāntaḥ । adhikaraṇā-
ntaramuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">।। 8 ।। 1saumikē ca kr̥tārthatvāt ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra prayājaśēṣēṇa viśēṣaḥ ? nanu ca prayājaśēṣēṇēti
﻿<pb n="b1010"/>
prayājārthatā'vagamyatē । sōmaliptēnēti karmārthatā(vagatiḥ) kimiti
na viśēṣaḥ । ucyatē---sōmaliptēnētyapi sōmayāgārthatayaiva sōma-
saṁbandhaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi avabhr̥thaśrutēḥ karmāntarayōgaṁ sōmaliptasya
manvānaḥ śēṣabhāvaṁ manyatē ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---karmāntarayōgēpi nānyaśēṣō'nyaśēṣatayā
pratipat‍tuṁ śakyatē anyatra vyāpr̥ta ivānyatra । tasmātkarma-
śabdō lakṣaṇayaiva pratipattavyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1011"/>
<p>yantīti ca prakr̥tyarthō'ntarṇītaṇijarthō vihitō bhavati ।
anyathā'nuvādamātraṁ dhātvarthaḥ syāt । tadidamuktam---<q>“śrutiśca
vākyādbalīyasī”</q> iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 9 ।। kartr̥dēśakālānāmacōdanaṁ prayōgē nityasamavāyāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cānuvādakatvapakṣē apratipādakatvāt vākyānarthakyamēva
prāpnōti । na brūmō viniyōgē ānarthakyamiti । viniyōgē itthamēva
anvitō vākyārthaḥ pratīyatē । prayōk‍tr̥tvaṁ tu na saṁbhavati । kathaṁ
na saṁbhavati ? nityaprāptatvāt kārakagrāmasya । dravyasya hyatra niyamaḥ
﻿<pb n="b1012"/>
kriyatē na kārakāṇām । na cākārakasya prayōk‍tr̥tvaṁ
saṁbhavati । tasmādviniyōga ēvāyaṁ(niyama) viṣayaviśēṣō'vagamyatē
na prayōk‍tr̥vyāpāra iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---yadi dravyādanyat kārakatayā'vagamyatē
tatō yathā bhavānāha । iha tu dravyamēva kāraka-
tayā'vagamyatē । tasyābhidhānādvibhaktyutpat‍tēḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1013"/>
<p>nanu ca kārakaṁ hi kriyāprayuktyaiva prayujyatē । na ca kārakaśūnyaṁ
karmāsti । satyaṁ na kārakaśūnyaṁ karma na punaḥ sāmānyaṁ kiñcidasti
kārakaṁ nāma । yadēva hi vibhaktyā dravyaṁ guṇō vā samarpyatē
tadēva kārakam । tasmādviniyōgāt prayōk‍tr̥tvēpi niyamaḥ
saṁbhavati । uktaṁ ca viniyōgānusārī niyōgaḥ sati saṁbhavē
iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 10 ।। 1tathā dravyēṣu guṇaśrutirutpattisaṁyōgāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>yuktaṁ tāvat dravyasyōpādānaṁ vibhaktibhistasya kārakatayā-
﻿<pb n="b1014"/>
'vagatēḥ guṇastu tadviśēṣaṇamātramēva ś‍vētādiṣu । yatra punararuṇayēti
vibhaktyaiva kārakatvēnāvagatiḥ tatra pūrvādhikaraṇēnaivāvagatam । atō
dravyōpādānārthatvāt guṇajātyōravivakṣēti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē ।
atrōcyatē---satyaṁ dravyōpādānārthamidam । tadēva tu dravyaṁ tadrahitaṁ
na śakyatē tadviśiṣṭamupādātumiti guṇajātyōrapi dravyavadupādāna
siddhiḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 11 ।। 1saṁskārē ca tatpradhānatvāt ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p>saṁskārē punaḥ kō viśēṣaḥ ? ayaṁ viśēṣaḥ । adhikāraśūnyō
hi saṁskāravidhirbhavati saṁskāryārthatvāt saṁskārasya, nātrādhikārārthaṁ
﻿<pb n="b1015"/>
karmāvagamyatē । tasmādavivakṣaivēti pūrvābhyāṁ viśēṣaḥ । atrōcyatē
---satyamadhikārō nāvagamyatē । adhikr̥tadravyārthatayā tu pratīyatē ।
tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tatō bhavati ? saṁskāraviśiṣṭadravyaṁ adhikāra-
vidhiviśēṣaṇatayā'vagamyatē । tataśca guṇavat tadapi adhikāra-
vidhinaivōpādīyata iti tadvadityucyatē । tatpradarśitamēvaṁ satyaṅga-
vidhiranuvāda iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 12 ।। 1yajati cōdanādravyadēvatākriyaṁ samudāyē kr̥tārthatvāt ।। 27 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1016"/>
<p>kē punastē'dhikāraviṣayāḥ ? yāgadānahōmāḥ । <q>“svargakāmō
yajēta,”</q> <q>“āyuṣkāmō hiraṇyaṁ dadyāt”</q> saubhāgyakāmō juhuyāt”
ityēvamādayaḥ । ētaccōpalakṣaṇamātram । anyēpi yē kāmaśruti-
saṁyuktāḥ । kaḥ punastyāgātmakatvē sati yāgadānahōmānāṁ parasparaṁ
viśēṣa ityāśaṅkānivr̥ttyarthaṁ svarūpavarṇanamityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1017"/>
﻿<pb n="b1018"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 14 ।। vidhēḥ karmāpavargitvādarthāntarē vidhipradēśaḥ syāt ।। 29 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarasyōpādānalakṣaṇēna saṁbandhaḥ ? ēṣa saṁbandhaḥ । kimu-
pāttasyātithyārthaṁ dhāraṇamātraṁ dvābhyāṁ prayujyatē, uta niriṣṭakasya
punarupādānam, uta pr̥thagēvōpādānaṁ, dharmamātrātidēśakamidaṁ
vacanaṁ, uta sādhāraṇamētadēvōpādānamiti । anyaśēṣasyānyatra-
﻿<pb n="b1019"/>
viniyōgō nāsti[yathā] anyatra vyāpr̥tasyaivānyatra vyāpāraḥ
ityuktam । viniyōgānusārī cō(nō)pādānamityētadapyuktam ।
tasmānnātithyōpāttasya upasadagnīṣōmābhyāṁ dhāraṇaṁ prayujyata iti
ghaṭatē । niriṣṭakōpadēśaśca śiṣṭācāravirōdhānna bhavati । lakṣaṇā-
śrayaṇaṁ ca nōpapadyatē । ēvaṁ dharmātidēśō'pi lakṣaṇābhayādēva
tyajyatē । tasmātsādhāraṇāvagatirēva śrutyōpapannā bhavatīti
sādhāraṇamupādānamiti siddham ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ caturthādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1020"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1dravyāsaṁskārakarmasu parārthatvāt phalaśrutirarthavādaḥ
syāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>uktamadhyāyādau sarvatra niyōgavyāpāra ēva cintyata iti । ihē-
dānīṁ kiṁ phalasaṁbandhitayā puruṣasya vidhivyāpārassaṁbhavati nēti ci-
ntyatē । puruṣaphalasaṁbandhāsaṁbhavē kathaṁ prāmāṇyaṁ saṁbhavati iti pramāṇa-
lakṣaṇē cintitam । yō'pi tatra pūrvapakṣaḥ asāvapi kriyākāraka-
saṁbandhō'vagamyamānaḥ kathaṁ kriyāntaraviṣayaṁ niyōgaṁ pratipādayatī
﻿<pb n="b1021"/>
tyasyārthasya nirākaraṇāya । iha tu svaviṣayō niyōgō na saṁbhavatīti
cintā । kathaṁ ? yasyētyēvamādīnāmadhikāriviśēṣaṇatayā'saṁbhavāt ।
kathamasaṁbhavaḥ ? tatsaṁbandhasya niyōgasyānupapattēḥ kimiti ? siddha-
vadupadēśāt । yathā dēvadattaḥ ōdanaṁ pacati iti puruṣōpalakṣaṇatā
pratīyatē । na puruṣēṇōdanaḥ paktavya iti । nāyaṁ śabdārthaḥ yasya
parṇamayī juhūrbhavati na sa pāpaṁ ślōkaṁ śr̥ṇōti iti । pratyayāntarā-
﻿<pb n="b1022"/>
vagamyatvādasyārthasya । na ca tatpratyayāntaramasti prathamalakṣaṇōkta
ēvāyamartha iti sthitaṁ ēvaṁbhūtānāmarthavādatvamiti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">।। 2 ।। 1naimittikē vikāratvāt kratupradhānamanyat syāt ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṁ punaratra dva‍yarthaṁ vākyamupanyasyatē । yatrāpi tāvadarthadvayē
viśēṣō nāvagamyatē tatrāpyēkārthēnaiva vākyēna bhavitavyam । prakaraṇā-
dibhistu viśēṣō'vagantavyaḥ । kiṁ punaratra viśēṣa ēvāvagamyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b1023"/>
dva‍yarthatā cābhidhānasya pramāṇalakṣaṇa ēva nirākr̥tā । tasmāta-
saṁbhavātpūrvapakṣamēvēdamadhikaraṇaṁ pratibhāti ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---ēvamēvaitadēkārthatvamēva anvitābhidhānē । prayōjana-
dvayaṁ tu atra saṁbhavatīti kratvarthatāmapi pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । saṁbandhā-
nusāri cōpādānamityuktam । nanu ca viniyōgānusārītyuktaṁ na saṁba-
ndhānusārī । naivaṁ, viniyōgō hi saṁbandhahētutayōktaḥ, na punarviniyōga-
﻿<pb n="b1024"/>
taivāśrīyatē । tasmāt dvayamupādāpakaṁ, saṁbandhadvayāvagamāt
na kriyāsaṁbandhatyāgēna dravyādēḥ puruṣārthatā'vasīyatē ।
atrābhidhīyatē । naitad‍yuk‍taṁ yaduk‍taṁ saṁbandhamātrānusāryu-
pādānamiti śabdōpapāditasaṁbandhānusāryupādānaṁ na saṁbandhānu-
sārī śabdācca puruṣārthatayaivānvayō'vagamyatē । nanu kriyayāpya-
nvayō'vagamyatē । satyam gamyatē puruṣārthaupayikatayā ।
﻿<pb n="b1025"/>
tasmāt tadēvōpādāpakaṁ yadarthamēvānvayāvagamaḥ । yatpunaridaṁ bhāṣya-
kārēṇōk‍taṁ viśēṣānavagamāt dviṣṭhaṁ vākyamalambusānāṁ 1yātēti
tat prakaraṇādyasaṁbhavē anirṇayāyaiva na punaḥ śabdāt dvaya
avagantuṁ śakyatē । iha tu viśēṣāvaṇamānnānirṇaya ityarthaḥ ।
nanu na kiñcidvihitamastīti paricōdya sāmānyavidhānōpanyāsaḥ
sāmasādhyastutyapēkṣayā nābhivartaparatayētyadōṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1026"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">।। 3 ।। 1ēkasya tūbhayatvē saṁyōgapr̥thaktvam ।। 5 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaḥ pūrvaparkṣiṇa āśaṅkāhētuḥ ? ayamāśaṅkāhētuḥ yathā
<q>‘agnihōtraṁ juhōti’</q> <q>‘agnihōtraṁ juhuyāt svargakāma’</q> iti ca na pr̥thak
prayōk‍tr̥tvamasti svargakāmapadānvayēpi hōmānvayāvagatēḥ । ēvamatrāpi
<q>‘dadhnā juhōti’</q> <q>‘dadhnēndriyakāmasya juhuyāt’</q> iti kāmasaṁyōgēpi
dadhihōmāvagatēḥ puruṣārthasyaiva prayōk‍tr̥tvaṁ manyatē[pūrvavādī]ēvaṁ prāptē-
'bhidhīyatē । naitad‍yuktam kratōrapyatra prayōk‍tr̥tvamavasīyatē kraturapi
hi sādhikāraḥ । na guṇaphalasaṁbandhaḥ āśrayē aidamarthyamapēkṣata
﻿<pb n="b1027"/>
ityuktam । tasmāt <q>‘dadhnā juhōti’</q> iti hōmārtha ēvāyaṁ
viniyōgaḥ <q>‘dadhnēndriyakāmasya’</q> ityēva puruṣārthaḥ । yaduk‍taṁ <q>‘agnihōtraṁ
juhōti’</q> <q>‘agnihōtraṁ juhuyāt svargakāmaḥ’</q> ityēkaḥ prayōk‍tēti yuk‍taṁ
adhikārāntarāśravaṇāt upādāturēvādhikārakalpanā । iha tu
adhikāradvayaṁ nityaṁ naimittikaṁ cāstīti yuktō viśēṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 4 ।। 1dravyāṇāṁ tu kiyārthānāṁ saṁskāraḥ kratudharmaḥ syāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>iha tu prāṇadhāraṇārthatvādvratasya puruṣārthatāṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣa-
vādī niyamasyaiva prāṅmukhō'nnānibhuñ‍jīta iti vat pratigraha-
niyamavacca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1028"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---nāyaṁ niyamaniyōgō'dhikārakalpanāṁ sahatē ।
sannihitaśca kratvadhikāraḥ । sākṣāt śrutādhikārasannidhau yadaśrūya-
māṇādhikāraṁ tata tadarthamēvābhidhānēna pratibhāti । tādarthyēnaiva ca
niyamasya niyōjyasaṁbandhalābhāt nādhikārāntarāpēkṣā'sti । yaduktaṁ
pratigrahādiniyamavat bhavitumarhatīti । yuk‍taṁ tatrādhikārāśravaṇāt
iha punaḥ tadviparītaṁ iti darśitam । ataḥ kratuprayōjya ēva dravya-
niyama iti sthitam । kratvadhikāraprayōjyamityuk‍taṁ bhavati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 5 ।। 1cōdanāyāṁ phalāśrutēḥ karmamātraṁ vidhīyēta na hyaśabdaṁ
pratīyēta ।। 10 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1029"/>
<p>ihādhikāraśūnyā vidhaya udāharaṇam । kiṁ tēṣāmadhikāra-
kalpanā uta tāvatyēva paryavasānamiti saṁśayaḥ । nanu ca <q>‘saphalaṁ’</q>
<q>‘aphalaṁ’</q> ityatra sandēhō bhāṣyē śrūyatē । ucyatē---adhikārādr̥tē
phalaṁ nāstīti svargakāmādhikaraṇē <q>‘tasmātsiddhō'dhikāra’</q> iti vadatā
pradarśitam । anyathā hi siddhaṁ svargasya prādhānyamityupasaṁhāraḥ
syāt । tasmāta sādhikāraniradhikāracintaivēyam ।</p>
<p>kiṁ tāvatprāptam ? yāvadvacanaṁ vacanamiti kartavya-
tāparyavasāyyēva niyōgō nādhikāraparyantō bhavitumarhati ।
nanu ca niyōga ēvādhikārādr̥tē na nirvartyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1030"/>
<p>kēna vā uktamadhikārādr̥tē na niyōgō niṣpadyata
iti adhikr̥tasya niyōgaḥ na punaḥ niyōgata ēvādhi-
kāraḥ । nanu cādhikārādr̥tē'nanuṣṭhēyatvāt niyōgāvagati-
rbādhyēta । nāvagatēḥ kaścidbādhaḥ । anadhikr̥tāstu na kurvatē
kimāyātamavagatēḥ । taduk‍taṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa <q>‘kṣēmyō'yaṁ panthāḥ gacchatu
bhavān anēna’</q> iti । tasmānnātra kasyacidadhikāraṁ paśyāmaḥ ।
adhyāhriyamāṇēpyadhikārē kasyādhikārō'dhyāhriyēta yasmānna niyōgā-
﻿<pb n="b1031"/>
dviśēṣākṣēpaḥ saṁbhavati । na cāparipūrṇa vākyamityatra pramāṇamasti ।
<q>‘paṭōbhavati’</q> ityētāvadēva vākyam । <q>‘raktaḥ paṭōbhavati’</q>
ityapi bhavati । tasmāt padāntaraśravaṇanibandhana ēva
vākyēṣu arthāntarāvagamaḥ । na punaḥ aśrūyamāṇa ēvārthāntara-
kalpanāpramāṇamasti । kathaṁ tarhi <q>‘vasantāya kapiñjalānālabhatē’</q>
grīṣmāya kalaviṅkān iti agr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatvāditi tatrō-
ktam । lōkē tarhi kathaṁ <q>‘dvāraṁ’</q> <q>‘dvāra’</q> mityēvamādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="b1032"/>
yuktaṁ kārakāṇāṁ kriyāpēkṣatvāt na punarniyōgō'dhikārama-
pēkṣata ityuktam । tasmādyāvadvacanaṁ vacanaṁ iti । atrā-
bhidhīyatē---kārakamiva kriyāpēkṣaṁ niyōgamapyadhikārāpēkṣaṁ
vadāmaḥ । kutaḥ ? lōkē tathā darśanāt dēvadattagāmabhyāja śuklāṁ iti ।
na hi anapēkṣitaviśēṣaṁ lōkē vaktārō bhavanti iti dēvadattaṁ
yajñadattaṁ vā'dhikr̥tya liṅādayaḥ prayōjyāḥ । nanu ca dēvadattādayaḥ
kartr̥viśēṣaṇam । yathā na kartr̥viśēṣaṇaṁ tathā ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1033"/>
adhikārāddhi kartr̥tvaṁ sthāsyati na kartr̥tvādadhikāra-
tasmāt śrutyēkadēśaḥ sa ucyatē---yatpunaratra bhāṣyakārēṇōk‍taṁ
<q>“ēvaṁ laukikō'dhyāhāraḥ prāpnōti”</q> iti parihr̥taṁ ca <q>“vaidikamēvādhyāha-
riṣyāma”</q> iti, vyavadhānaṁ cāśaṅkya <q>‘api paśyasi’</q> iti dr̥ṣṭāntā-
bhidhānaṁ sarvamidaṁ asamañjasamiva pratibhāti yanniyōgādavagamyatē
kathaṁ tadavaidikaṁ ? vyavadhānē ca kathamanuṣaṅga ? yadapyuk‍taṁ <q>‘api
paśyasi dhāvantaṁ’</q> iti । asaṁbandhipadavyavāyāt naivāyaṁ vyavāyaḥ
yōgyapadasaṁbaddhaṁ vyavahitamityucyatē । atrōcyatē---vaidikamēvādhyā-
hariṣyāmaḥ iti । ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati । na kārakatayā'dhyāhriyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b1034"/>
kathaṁ tarhi ? adhikārimukhēnaivēti । kārakatayā hi phalasaṁbandhō
laukikō bhavati pramāṇāntarāpēkṣatvāt dr̥ṣṭāntō'pi yathā na
padavyavadhānamātrādva‍yavahitaṁ bhavati kintu yōgyapadasaṁbaddhaṁ vākyā-
ntaravyavahitaṁ vyavahitaṁ bhavati । tasmānnādhikārādhyāhārē vya-
vadhānam । api paśyasīti ca sūktam । atō'śrūyamāṇādhi-
kārāṇyapi sādhikārāṇīti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13,15">।। 6 ।। 1tatsarvārthamaviśēṣāt sa svargaḥ sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭa-
tvāt ।। 13, 15 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitaṁ niyōgō nādhikāraśūnya iti । kēnādhi-
﻿<pb n="b1035"/>
kārēṇēti na jñāyatē । atō'gr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatvāt sarvārthibhiḥ
saṁbadhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । atrōcyatē---bahubhiḥ saṁbandhē niyatamēkēna
saṁbandhaḥ bhavati । ēkēna cēdupapannō niyōgaḥ nādhikārāntarasaṁbandhē
pramāṇamasti । nanu cāgr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatvānnāsau nirūpayituṁ śakyata
ityuktam । satyaṁ yadi na gr̥hyatē viśēṣaḥ । iha tu sarvān pratyaviśi-
ṣṭatvāt svargakāmasyaivādhikārō'trāvagamyatē । sāmānyakalpanāyāṁ hi
viśēṣāvagamahētvabhāvāt । tadidamuktaṁ---<q>“sa svargaḥ syāt sarvān
﻿<pb n="b1036"/>
pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt”</q> iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 8 ।। kratau phalārthavādamaṅgavat kārṣṇājiniḥ ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitamaśrūyamāṇādhikārēṣu sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt svargō-
'dhikāravidhihēturiti । yatra punaḥ viśēṣābhidhāyinō'rthavādāḥ
śrūyantē yatra saṁśayaḥ---kiṁ atrāpi svarga ēvādhikārahētuḥ । atha
vā'rthavādābhihitaṁ vastviti । pūrvapakṣavādī niyōgādyadavagamyatē
tadēva yuktamiti manyatē । arthavādastvarthavāda ēva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1037"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---arthavādābhihitamēva phalaṁ yuktam । kutaḥ ?
ēvamarthastutyaiva stutyartha upapannō bhavati । nanu ca niyōgāt
svargārthataivāvagamyata ityuktam । sandigdhē ca vākyaśēṣānnirṇayaḥ
uktaḥ । atrōcyatē---satyaṁ saṁśayō nāsti । niścayō'pi naiva
vidyatē । ataśca vākyaśēṣādyō'rthō'vagamyatē sa ēva
vākyārthaḥ । na cāpratipannē vākyārthē kēvalānniyōgāt
kiñcitpratipadyatē । tasmātsūktamarthavādābhihitamēvādhikārahēturiti ।
﻿<pb n="b1038"/>
yatpunarbhāṣyakārēṇōktaṁ---vibhaktimātraṁ kalpyatē sa sahadhātvarthēna
prayōgavacanō vidhāsyatīti । pakṣē kāryē kāraṇaviśēṣakalpanā[nāya]
na khēdanīyaṁ mana ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 9 ।। 1kāmyē karmaṇi nityaḥ svargō yathā yajñāṅgē kratvarthaḥ ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē---yadi punarniyōgāt svargādhikāraḥ ।
padāntarayōgāccōpādhayaḥ kalpyantē śākamapyāharētivat kō dōṣa
﻿<pb n="b1039"/>
syāt । na khalu kaściddōṣaḥ । kintu aniścitāt sāmānyādhikārāt
viśēṣa upādhiriti tu duśśakaṁ vak‍tum । kāṣṭhasaṁyuktamiva śākā-
haraṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 10 ।। 1sārvakāmyamaṅgakāmaiḥ prakaraṇāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>sarvēbhyaḥ kāmēbhyō darśapūrṇamāsāviti kimayamanuvādaḥ । atha-
vā'yamapi vidhiriti prāptārthatvādanuvāda iti manyatē । kathaṁ
prāptiḥ ? kiñcidaṅgadvārēṇa kiñcitsvata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1040"/>
nanu pradhānasaṁbandhitayaivaitacchrūyatē kathamaṅgāpēkṣō'nuvādaḥ । aṅga-
dvāramapi hi pradhānēna vyapadiśyatē yūpavat ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---pramāṇāntarāvagamyamidaṁ yadutānyasaṁbandhī
anyēna vyapadiśyata iti । siddhē cānuvādē pramāṇāntaragamyatā,
pramāṇāntaragamyatāyāṁ cānuvāda itītarētarāśrayatvam । tasmānnira-
pēkṣācchabdānniyōga ēvēti manyāmahē । yūpē punararthāntaravidhēyatvāt
pramāṇāntarapramēyatā yuktā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 11 ।। 1tatra sarvē'viśēṣāt ।। 17 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1041"/>
<p>idamidānīṁ cintyatē---sakr̥tsarvakābhāvāptiḥ uta yāvatkāmaṁ
prayōga iti । sarvakāmanimittatayā śravaṇāt na prayōgē viśēṣā-
vadhāraṇā śakyā । ēkatvāditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nanu ca sarvakāmō nāma
naiva kaścidastyadhikārī anadhikārācca phalōtpattērasaṁbhavaḥ । ucyatē
---yadi kāmanā aṅgaṁ syāt anutpannā satī nāṅgabhāva upapadyata iti
bhavati kāmanānāmanutpādaḥ sakr̥tprayōgē sarvaphalānutpattau hētuḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1042"/>
iha tu sarvakāmairyuktasya kāminō'dhikāra iti na prayōga-
kālē kāmanōtpāda upayujyatē । tasmānnanimittē sati naimitti-
kasya vyāghātō bhavitu marhati । atrōcyatē---yāvatkāmaṁ
prayōga iti । ēvamadhikārasiddhirupapannā bhavati । na hi
akāminaḥ phalādhikārō'stīti ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । nanu
ca prayōgakālē kāmanōtpādō'naṅgatvānnōpayujyata ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b1043"/>
kēna vōktaṁ prayōgakālē utpādō hēturiti । adhikārāvagatāvēva
sarvakāmitā yugapanna saṁbhavatītyuktamasmābhiḥ । asaṁbhavē ca yugapat
sarvaniyōgānupapattiḥ । tasmāt pratikāmamadhikāraḥ । yadvā
yathōddiṣṭakāmābhiprāyamiti bhāṣyakārēṇōktam anirdiṣṭānāmava-
gamābhāva ityabhiprāyaḥ । atō nirdiṣṭāpēkṣī sarvaśabdaḥ sarvaṁ
kr̥tamitivat । ataḥ siddhaṁ pratikāmaṁ prayōga iti । ata ēva
ca viruddhānāmapi phalānāmadhikāraḥ siddhōbhavati । sakr̥tprayōgē
hi maraṇāyuṣōranutpattiḥ syāt । tasmādyōgasiddhirvēti
sūktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1044"/>
<p> ēvaṁ vā ।।</p>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇē niyōgasya phalaṁ prati kiṁ śarīragrahaṇapūrvakaḥ
prayōjakabhāvaḥ uta yāvacchrutaṁ prayōk‍tr̥tvamiti । tata pūrvapakṣavādī
śarīragrahaṇasya kāraṇāntarādarśanāt paśvādīnāṁ ca kāraṇāntarēṇō-
papattēḥ śarīragrahaṇapūrvakaḥ phalākṣēpa iti manyatē । paśvādīnāṁ kāraṇaṁ
pratigrahādi pratyakṣaṁ bhaviṣyatīti । rāddhāntavādī tu yāvacchrutaṁ prayō-
k‍tr̥tvaṁ manyatē । kasmāt ? kēvalaśravaṇāvagamyatvāt prayōk‍tr̥bhāvasya ।
﻿<pb n="b1045"/>
sarvāviśēṣāt । na hi gamyatē viśēṣaḥ ihaiva amutraiva vēti
kāmaśrutisāmānyāt ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakārō'nantarādarśanamupanyasya pratyakṣānumānābhyāṁ
nōpalabhāmahē śabdādavagamyata ityuktavān । tadayuk‍taṁ, śabdādapi
hi nānantaryamupalabhyata ityuktam । ayamabhiprāyaḥ bhāṣyakārasya
---sāmānyāvagamāt ihāmuṣminniti ca viśēṣānavagamāt śabdatō
na pramāṇāntarābhāvaḥ ānantaryaṁ vihantīti । liṅgamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 12 ।। 1samavāyē cōdanāsaṁyōgasyārthavattvāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>vājapēyēnēṣ‍ṭvā br̥haspatisavēna yajēta’ iti lakṣaṇē ktyāpratya-
﻿<pb n="1046"/>
yōtpattau kālaśravaṇāt kālārthaḥ saṁyōga iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
samānakartr̥kyōrdhātvarthayōḥ anvayāvagatēḥ dhātusaṁbandha ēvāyam ।
sa ca aṅgāṅgibhāvādr̥tē na saṁbhavatīti aṅgāṅgitaivēti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 13 ।। 1ubhayārthamiti cēt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>paurṇamāsīṁ saṁsthāpyēti parisamāptivacanatvāt saṁsthāśabdasya
nāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ paurṇamāsyāṁ saṁbhavatīti prakaraṇāt darśapūrṇamāsāṅgataiva
vaimr̥dhasyēti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1047"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---yadi samāptivacanatvāt saṁsthāśabdasya
nāṅgitvaṁ paurṇamāsyāḥ prakaraṇādapi naivāṅgitvaṁ saṁbhavati । atha
saṁsthāpyēti pūrvavihitāṅgakalāpaparisamāp‍tyabhiprāyō'yaṁ saṁsthā-
śabdaḥ ēvaṁ tarhi vākyāt paurṇamāsyaṅgataiva vaimr̥dhasya । na ca
niyōgaikyē kaścidviśēṣaḥ asyāpyadhikārasaṁbandhāt । atassiddhaṁ
paurṇamāsyaṅgaṁ vaimr̥dha iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 14 ।। anutpattau tu kālaḥ syāt prayōjanēna sambandhāt ।। 36 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1048"/>
<p>nirjñātaparāṅgabhāvayōḥ saṁbandhē niyōgaḥ kālavidhānaparyavasāyyēva
karmaṇaḥ pratyabhijñānāt tasmāt kālārthō niyōgaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 15 ।। utpattikālaviśayē kālaḥ syādvākyasya tatpradhāna-
tvāt ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā sōmēna yajēna’ ityatrākarmavidhānāt
kālārthō niyōga ityuktam । tatpunaridamayuktam । vājapēyēnēṣṭvā
br̥haspatisavēna yajētētyanēnāviśēṣāt tēnātrāpi kālārthēna niyōgēna
bhavitavyam । ubhayatra vā karmārthatvaṁ niyōgasya । vaktavyō vā
﻿<pb n="1049"/>
viśēṣaḥ । atra kaiścidanārabhya vidhānaṁ viśēṣa uktaḥ । kaḥ punaranāra-
bhyavidhānēna viśēṣa upalabhyatē ? ayaṁ viśēṣaḥ---karmadvayavidhānaṁ
tāvanna saṁbhavati anēnēṣṭvā anēna yajētētyēvamādiṣu । anārabhya-
vidhānē ca naikamapi karma prakr̥tamasti । tasmānnāmataḥ prasiddha-
karmōpādānaṁ kālaniyōgārtham । uktaṁ ca nāmadhēyamapi guṇaphalōpabandhē-
nārthavat iti । vājapēyē punaḥ prakr̥tatvādvājapēyasya karmāntara-
vidhānaṁ śrutyōpapadyatē । nāma ca taddharmātidēśārthaṁ bhaviṣyati
prakaraṇāntarē prayōjanānyatvamiti nyāyāt । anārabhyavidhānē
punaḥ prakaraṇāntarābhāvāt dvayōrapi (akarmārthatvaṁ yuktam)
﻿<pb n="1050"/>
karmāntaratvamayuktam । yēṣāṁ punaḥ darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇa ēvaitatpaṭhyatē
tatra kā kathā bhavatu । tatrāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ kā nō bādhā ? atha vā pari-
hr̥tamēvaitat śākhāntarādhikaraṇē sarvaśākhāpratyayamēkaṁ karmēti vadatā ।
kathaṁ parihr̥taṁ ? tadēvēdaṁ śāstramiti yuktam । bhavatvēvaṁ tathāpi na
vidmaḥ kiṁ anārabhyavādasya yō'rthaḥ tēna śās‍traṁ pratyabhijñāyatāṁ uta
prakaraṇē'pi yō'rthaḥ iti । avirōdhādanārabhyavādēna pratyabhijñānaṁ bhēda-
vidō manyantē । tasmātsūktamiha kalārthaḥ saṁyōga iti । darśana-
muktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1051"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="38">।। 16 ।। phalasaṁyōgastvacōditē na syādaśēṣabhūtatvāt ।। 38 ।।</ab>
<p>atra saṁśayaḥ kiṁ yasya niyōgaḥ tasya phalaṁ uta anyasya
niyōgō'nyasya phalamiti । adhikārī ca niyujyatē । yadarthaṁ
karma sō'dhikārī sa ēva niyujyatē । yadarthaṁ karma sō'dhikārī sa
ēva niyujyatē । anadhikārē ca pituḥ nāsya niyōjyatā syāt ।
tasmādbhavati saṁśayaḥ । kiṁ yuktam ? niyōjyasya pituḥ phalamiti ।
kutaḥ ? adhikārasidhyarthō niyōgaḥ na saṁbandhamātrāvagamyaḥ
tasmāt pituridaṁ phalaṁ putraphalānvayasya stutyā'nvayō bhavatu ।
lakṣaṇayā'dhikr̥taviśēṣaṇam । tathā ca kratusaṁbandhinimittē
﻿<pb n="1052"/>
niyōjyasyaiva phalaṁ na kratunā saṁbadhyatē । atrōcyatē
---yasya phalānvayaḥ tasyaiva phalaṁ nimittatayāpyadhikāra-
siddhēḥ । itarasya putrajanmanā nimittēnāpi puruṣārthatā'stī-
tyadhikārasiddhiḥ । kathaṁ tarhi phalapadaṁ ? na karma viśēṣaṇaṁ, nāpyadhi-
kārōpanipāti । ucyatē---bhaviṣyatyadhikārōpanipāti । katha-
mēvaṁvidhasya putrajanmanō'dhikāriviśēṣaṇatvēna śravaṇāt । tasmādyasya
niyōgastasyaiva phalamiti aviruddhamētat prītyāpyadhikārasiddhēḥ ।
yaduk‍taṁ kratusaṁbandhē niyōjyasyaiva phalamiti, yuktamadhikārānu-
﻿<pb n="1053"/>
pravēśānnimittasyēti ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ vā ।।</p>
<p><q>‘putrē jātē’</q> iti śrūyatē । tatra saṁśayaḥ---kiṁ jananānantaramēva
naimittikaṁ bhavatu utāṅgōpasaṁhāramapēkṣatē prakr̥tivadabhiprāptamiti ।
yadyēvaṁ kimiti kumārasya prāṇadhāraṇamutkarṣahētutvēnōpanyasyatē ।
ēkamēvēdamadhikaraṇamastu । sāṅgasya naimit‍tikatvāt na nimittāna-
ntaraṁ prayōgaḥ saṁbhavati iti svakāla ēva kartavyaḥ । na cānantaryē-
'sati nimittatvavyāghātaḥ bhūtapratyayayōgānnimittasya । na ca
pratīkṣaṇē bhūtatvamapaiti । tasmāt pr̥thagadhikaraṇaṁ niṣprayōjanamiva
pratibhāti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1054"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---nimittānantaraṁ naimit‍tikamityautsargikō
nyāyaḥ na kāraṇādr̥tē kālōtkarṣō'vagamyatē । nanu ca kāraṇamuk‍taṁ
sāṅgasya naimit‍tikatvam । ētadēva na vijānīmaḥ kiṁ nimittakālē
niyōgāvagamāt viniyōgāvagamyamaṅgaṁ tyajyatāṁ uta niyōgakāla-
syōtkarṣa iti । niyōgārthatvādviniyōgasyāṅgatyāgaṁ viniyōga-
vidō manyantē । yathā rajasvalādisparśanēna pūrvāhṇādikālaḥ vihita
upēkṣyatē । ata ētadbādhanārthaṁ pūrvamadhikaraṇam । yadi hi
niyōgakāla ēvānuṣṭhānaṁ kriyatē yadarthō niyōgastadēva hīyatē ।
﻿<pb n="1055"/>
tasmānniyōgakālāvagatirēvōtkraṣṭavyā । utkr̥ṣṭā cēt svakāla
ēva syānnāṅgatyāgē pramāṇamastīti dvitīyamadhikaraṇaṁ
likhitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 17 ।। pradhānēnābhisaṁyōgādaṅgānāṁ mukhyakālatvam ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘vājapēyēnēṣṭvā br̥haspatisavēna yajēta’</q> ityatra
saṁśayaḥ---kimēkō niyōgaḥ uta niyōgadvayamiti । nanu
niyōgadvitvē'ṅgāṅgibhāvō nōpapadyatē । asti cāṅgāṅgitvaṁ,
tasmānna prayōgabhēdaḥ । bāḍhamupapadyatē । viniyōgādaṅgāṅgitā
﻿<pb n="1056"/>
prayōgānyatvēna viniyōgānyatvam । nanu ca niyōgānyatvē śāstra-
bhēdaḥ prāpnōti । bhavatu prayōgāpēkṣayā na kaściddōṣaḥ । viniyōgā-
pēkṣayā tvēkamēvēdaṁ śāstram । kathaṁ punarēkatvē śāstrasya prayōgabhēdaḥ ?
kēna vāryatē vidhānabhēdavat anubandhanimittakam । yadyathaivānu-
badhyatē tat tathaiva tantraṁ bhinatti । iha tu prayōgānubandhabhēdāta
prayōgabhēdaḥ prāpnōti । bhavatu prayōgabhēdāpēkṣayā na dōṣaḥ ।
tasmānna śāstrāntarāpattiḥ kēvalaṁ prayōgabhēdaḥ । yathā ca
prayōgabhēdastathā darśitam ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ caturthādhyāyasya tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="1057"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1prakaraṇaśabdasāmānyāccōdanānāmanaṅgatvam ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu ca nāmadhēyavicārē yajisāmānādhikaraṇyānnāma bhavatī-
tyuktam । kathaṁ punarayajyarthasyāpyētadabhidhānaṁ śaṅkyatē ?
ataḥ pūrvapakṣa ēvāyaṁ nōpapadyatē । ucyatē---iha tu
niyōgaikyād‍yugapadabhidhānaṁ dhātvarthasya । niyōgaikyaṁ ca
prakaraṇāyattamiti sarvaprakr̥tābhidhāyī dhāturiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē ।
﻿<pb n="1058"/>
ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē---satyaṁ prakaraṇānniyōgaikyaṁ na punaḥ śrutānu-
bandhaparityāgē kāraṇamasti । kathaṁ ? itikartavyatāpi hi
niyōgaikyaṁ naiva viruṇaddhi । tathābhūtōpadēśāditi vakṣyāmaḥ ।
atō yāgavyatiriktamaṅgamiti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। 1madhyasthaṁ yasya tanmadhyē ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātrāpi kramāt prakaraṇa balīya ityētadēvōdāhr̥tam ।
﻿<pb n="1059"/>
sthitaṁ ca sarvārthatvaṁ tr̥tīyē । ucyatē---satyaṁ viniyōgāt sthitam ।
idānīṁ tu pr̥thak prayōjyatvādabhiṣēcanīyaniyōgasya tasya ca
sannidhānāt tēnaivaikya yuktamiti manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । na viniyōga-
virōdhaḥ ; pratyēkasaṁbandhahētutvāta prakaraṇasya । ataḥ sannidhi-
viśēṣasyātikramō nōpapadyatē । atrōcyatē---sthitamaikaśabdyamadhi-
kāravidhēḥ । tataḥ kiṁ ? idaṁ tatō bhavati । yasyaiva prayōgānubandha-
bhēdaḥ tasyaiva pr̥thak prayōgō'vasīyatē svēnētikartavyatā-
kālāpēna । yasya punaraṅgasyādhikāravidhirēva prayōgaṁ jñāpayati
na tasyāvāntaraprayōgaḥ śakyatē jñāpayitum । tasmāt
kramāt taddēśasyaiva anuṣṭhānamadhikāravidhisamadhigamyamēva ।
﻿<pb n="1060"/>
prakaraṇāvirōdhastvayaivōktaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 3 ।। 1prakaraṇāvibhāgē ca vipratiṣiddhaṁ hyubhayam ।। 5 ।।</ab>
<p>purastādupasadāṁ saumyēna pracarantīti । kaḥ khalvāgnimārutā-
dūrdhvamanūyājaiścarantītyanēnāsya viśēṣaḥ । na khalu kaścidviśēṣaḥ ।
kimityadhikaraṇāntaraṁ saumyādīnāṁ anyadadhikaraṇāntaram । kā nō
bādhā ? । na khalu kaścidbhavatō bādhā । adhikaraṇānarthakyaṁ tu
bhavati । ayaṁ tarhi viśēṣaḥ । prakaraṇāt sarvasya prādhānyaṁ iti-
kartavyatātvaṁ vā rājasūyē । asaṁyuk‍taṁ ca prakaraṇādityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="1061"/>
tasmādvākyādupasadaṅgamēvēti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ । api ca
sannidhānaviśēṣēṇōpasadaṅgataiva yuktā, adhikāraniyōgāt ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē---na tāvadupasadāṁ prakaraṇamasti adhikāra-
nibandhanatvāt prakaraṇasya । nanu ca vākyādupasadaṅgatvamityuktam
nōbhayapadasaṁbandhābhāvāt vākyaṁ saṁbhavati । tasmāt
purastādupasadāmityēva saṁbandhaḥ । atha kasmādupasadāṁ saumyēnētyēṣa
saṁbandhaḥ na bhavati । purastādityananvayaḥ prāpnōti
﻿<pb n="1062"/>
purastāditi saṁbandhē kālavidhānāt saumyēna carantītyaviruddham ।
tasmādidamapi āgnimārutādityanēnāviśiṣṭam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 4 ।। 1phalavadvōk‍tahētutvāditarasya pradhāna syāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>sāṅgrahaṇyāṁ tu phalavatsannidhau aphalaṁ tadaṅgamiti siddhēpyanu-
ṣaṅganivr̥ttyarthamidamadhikaraṇam । darśitaṁ ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1063"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 5 ।। 1dadhigrahō naimittikaḥ śrutisaṁyōgāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>anityadōṣanirharaṇārthasaṅkīrtanāt naimittikaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣa-
vādī । khadiravadubhayārthatāmācāryadēśīyaḥ । nityatvē sati jyēṣṭha-
śabdōpapattiriti manyatē । rāddhāntastu nimittasaṁyōgābhāvāt
na dōṣanirharaṇārthatayā naimittikatvamasya śakyatē kalpayitum ।
kimiti na śakyatē naimittikadōṣanirharaṇānyathānupapattyā
tasyāpi naimittikatvaṁ bhavitumarhati । satyaṁ yadyanyathā
nōpapadyatē । arthavādatayā tūpapadyata ēvēti na kalpanāmarhati ।
﻿<pb n="1064"/>
sārūpyādyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 6 ।। vaiśvānaraśca nityaḥ syānnityaiḥ samānasaṅkhyatvāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>anityadōṣanirharaṇārthavādatayāpyupapadyata iti yadyu-
cyēta vaiśvānarē'pi nityatā bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhimānaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu na brūmō dōṣanirharaṇānnaimittikatvam nimitta-
saṁyōga ēvātra śrūyatē । na ca nimittaśrutirarthavādatayā śakyatē
vyākhyātum । śrutyarthē saṁbhavati nārthāntarakalpanōpapadyatē ।
darśanamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1065"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 7 ।। 1ṣaṭ‌citiḥ pūrvavattvāt ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>ṣaṣṭhīṁ citimiti pūraṇapratyayāvagamāt nimittaśrutiḥ artha-
vādatayā varṇayituṁ nyāyyēti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ kutaḥ ?
vidhēyānurōdhāt adhikārakalpanā nyāyyēti manyatē ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu satyamēvaṁ yadi virōdhaḥ syāt na tvatra virōdhaḥ,
upadēśavivakṣayāpi pratyayārthōpapattēḥ nāvaśyama(rthā)nuṣṭhānāpēkṣayaiva
bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ pūraṇasūtraṁ śakyatē varṇayitum । tasmāda-
﻿<pb n="1066"/>
virōdhaḥ । avirōdhē ca na nimittaśratiḥ tyak‍tuṁ pāryatē ।
tasmānnaimittikatvaṁ siddham । darśanōpanyāsaparihārāvuktau ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 8 ।। 1pitr̥yajñaḥ svakālatvādanaṅgaṁ syāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>phalakalpanātō varaṁ lakṣaṇēti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ ।
darśādhikārānupravēśē sati nādhikārāntaraṁ śakyatē kalpayitu-
mityuk‍taṁ bhavati । tasmādaṅgataivāmāvāsyāyāḥ pitr̥yajñasya ।
atrōcyatē-naikaniyōgatā saṁbhavati amāvāsyāyāmiva kālasaṁyōgā-
﻿<pb n="1067"/>
viśēṣāt piṇḍapitr̥yajñasya । nāmāvāsyāyāṁ śrautaḥ piṇḍapitr̥yajñē
ca lakṣaṇēti viśēṣō'vagamyatē । ubhayatra kālasaṁyōgasya saṁbhavāt ।
tasmātpūrvāparaśrutistatkālalakṣaṇētyavirōdhaḥ । prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 9 ।। paśvaṅgaṁ raśanā syāt tadāgamē vidhānāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1068"/>
<p>atrāpi ktvāpratyayasya kriyāntarāpēkṣitvāt ēkaniyōga-
tāṁ pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । tatra ca paśvarthataiva prāpnōti yūpasyāpi
tadarthatvāt । rāddhāntavādī tu samānakartr̥katāmātraṁ ktvāpratyayāda-
vagamyatē na niyōgaikyamiti yūpasyaḥ punaḥ dvitīyātaḥ prādhānyamēva
yuktamiti rāddhāntitavān ।</p>
<p>nanu caikaniyōgādr̥tē samānakartr̥kataiva na saṁbhavati । satyaṁ
na saṁbhavati kintu adhikāraikyāt siddhaṁ samānakartr̥katvam ।
﻿<pb n="1069"/>
nanu ca kālalakṣaṇā naivātra saṁbhavati । uccāraṇakālavibhāgō hi
ktvāpratyayōtpattau hēturityuktam । satyamuktaṁ, sa ēvōccāraṇakālō-
'nuṣṭhānēpi lakṣaṇayōcyatē । sarvatra ca kālavidhāviyamēva prati-
pattirlōkē vēdē ca । samānakartr̥katāpi naiva tatrādriyatē kāla-
niṣṭhatvānniyōgasya । ata ēva ca darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā sōmēna
yajētēti samānakartr̥katācōdyaṁ parihr̥taṁ bhavati । prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 10 ।। 1svaruścāpyēkadēśatvāt ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>yūpasya svarupamiti svarumān yūpa iti gōmānitivat
tādarthyaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । dr̥ṣṭō hi tādarthyē sati
﻿<pb n="1070"/>
matvarthaḥ । ēvamatrāpītyabhiprāyaḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu yavamatītyē-
vamādiṣu anaikāntyāt paśumanak‍tītī dvitīyānirdēśāt dr̥ṣṭārthaḥ-
tvācca paśvarthataivēti । ṣaṣṭhī tūtpat‍tisaṁyōgēpyupapannā cētyadōṣaḥ ।
prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 11 ।। darśapūrṇamāsayōrijyāḥ prādhānyaviśēṣāt ।। 29 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1071"/>
<p>sthitaṁ rājasūyādhikaraṇē anijyā vyudasyantē । yajiśabda-
saṁyōgēnādhikāraśravaṇāt । yatraiva ca dhāturvartatē tatraivaupapadaṁ
nāmatayā vartata iti nāmadhēyavicārē sthitam । ataḥ pūrvapakṣavādī
yāgamātra'vacanō'yaṁ yajiḥ yatra yajiḥ tatraivōpapadaṁ vartata iti
manvānō dvivacanāntasarūpamēvēdamabhidhānaṁ manyatē । yatpunaḥ
<q>‘prayājē prayājē kr̥ṣṇalaṁ juhōti’</q> iti vikr̥tiṣu darśanaṁ tat katha-
﻿<pb n="1072"/>
masmin pakṣē bhaviṣyati ? pramāṇāntaraṁ mr̥gyaṁ yatrēti vā,
vyāmōhō vā, karmāntaraṁ vā nāmataśca dharmagrahaṇaṁ bhaviṣyati । yatpunaḥ
ya ēvaṁ vidvānamāvāsyāṁ yajata iti tat prakr̥tasamudāyadvayaṁ kimiti
na parigr̥hyatē dvivacanayōgāt । uktaṁ ca dhātvarthānusāryupapadamiti ।
darśaśabdāccānyatvāvagatēḥ । tasmādrājasūyavadanijyaivātrāṅgamiti
sthitam । atrōcyatē---satyamidaṁ dhātvarthānusāryupapadamiti
﻿<pb n="1073"/>
tathāpi samudāyadvayasya prakr̥tatvāt dvivacanasya cārthāntarānupapat‍tēḥ ।
saṁbhavati ca svārthē sarūpakalpanāyā asaṁvāt । dhātvarthānusāri-
tāyāṁ cāvirōdha upapadasya । kathaṁ ? naivēdamupapadaṁ adhātvarthē pravr̥ttaṁ,
dhātvarthapravr̥ttau satyāṁ na nāmārthaparityāga upapadyatē । kaścāsyārthaḥ
prakr̥tasamudāyadvayavacanatā । ēvaṁ ca tadanusāritvē upapannē
nārthāntarakalpanāyāṁ pramāṇamasti । nanu ca prakr̥tayāgaparityāgē
nāsti pramāṇaṁ ghātōḥ; kēna vā uk‍taṁ aparityāgē pramāṇamastīti
kintūpapadārthavirōdhābhidhānē nāsti pramāṇamityuktamasmābhiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="1074"/>
yacca darśaśabdaśravaṇāt na prakr̥tapratyabhijñānamastīti parihr̥taṁ
tadvākyaśēṣēṣvēkārthatvadarśanāditi । śakyatvācca darśaśabdē-
nāpi tadarthābhidhānasya । tasmātsūk‍taṁ phalavatsannidhāva-
phalaṁ tadaṅgamiti । yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ kasmānnānuṣaṅgō bhavatīti cōdyaṁ
parihr̥taṁ tadanuṣaṅgatō vara[mitikartavyatā]kāṅkṣāparipūraṇamiti ।
anyathā tvanavasthaivākāṅkṣāyā iti । yadyavaṁ kimiti vyavā-
yānnānuṣajyētē iti sāṅgrahaṇyāṁ darśitaṁ tatrāpyayamēva nyāyō yuktaḥ
vaktavyō vā viśēṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ayamabhidhīyatē---yuk‍taṁ tatra prakr̥tivaditikartavya-
tāyāṁ sthitāyāṁ nirākāṅkṣatvāt vyavāyādēvānuṣaṅga-
niṣēdhaḥ । iha punaraparyavasitatvāditikartavyatārthitāyāṁ sthitāyāṁ
﻿<pb n="1075"/>
pūraṇēnaivaikaniyōgatvaṁ yuktam । na punaradhikārāntarakalpanēti
sūktam । darśanāni cōktāni । aṅgavatstutayaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 12 ।। jyōtiṣṭōmē tulyānyaviśiṣṭaṁ hi kāraṇam ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>iha tu dvivacanādyabhāvāt na yāgamātrapratipattiḥ
śakyatē vārayitum । [jyōtiṣṭōmaśabdasya ca nāmadhēyatvāt
pravr̥ttau nimittaṁ abhidhēyaṁ nānvayītyuk‍taṁ nāmadhēyavicārē] ।
﻿<pb n="1076"/>
nanu ca nāmataivātra hīyatē viśēṣaṇamēvaitattadā bhavati kiṁ na
śchinnam । tathāpi rāddhāntaḥ siddha ēva । kintu viśēṣaṇa-
padamapi ētannāmaiva arthāntarānupapattēḥ yajyarthasya viśēṣaṇa-
mātrāvagamahētutvāt । (tadētad‍‌dvitvamapi) । atō'nvitamapi
viśēṣaṇaniṣṭhamiti nāmaiva, arthāntarānupādānāt । stutidarśanaṁ
cōktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ caturthādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1077"/>
﻿<pb n="b1078"/>
﻿<pb n="1079"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>atha br̥hatyāṁ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1śrutilakṣaṇamānupūrvyaṁ tatpradhānatvāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu kratvarthapuruṣārthacintāpi tatra vr̥ttā kimidaṁ prayōjakā-
prayōjakalakṣaṇaṁ vr̥ttamiti । ucyatē---kramacintāyāmasyaivōpayōgāt
vakṣyamāṇaupayikatayā vr̥ttaṁ saṅkīrtyatē na vr̥ttatayā । ēkaprayōgaprayuktanāṁ
hi kramō bhavati nāprayuktānāmiti prayōjakāprayōjakasaṅkīrtanam ।
﻿<pb n="1080"/>
yadi(prayōjakāprayōjaka)prayuktānāṁ kramaścintyatē । avidhēyastarhi
kramaḥ vihitaṁ hi prayujyatē nāprayuktasya vidhānam ।
kēna vōktaṁ kramōvidhīyata iti । vihitavitānamēvātra
cintyatē kiṁ yathāpratipannavihitavitānamanuṣṭhēyaṁ utā-
niyamēnēti । kathaṁ punarayathāpratipannānuṣṭhānamāśaṅkyatē ।
﻿<pb n="1081"/>
viniyōgaśūnyatvādvihitavitānāvagamasya । nāntarīyakō hi vidhēyā-
vagatau vitānapratyayaḥ । atō yaścārthādarthō na sa cōdanārtha iti
manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī aniyamaṁ manyatē । nanu ca <q>‘adhvaryurgr̥hapatiṁ
dīkṣayitvā’</q> ityatra kramavidhānamēvōpanyastaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa
vidhēyāntarābhāvāditi vadatā । yadyēvamayuktabhidam । astyēvātra
vidhēyāntaraṁ anēnāmī dīkṣitavyā iti kartr̥viśēṣavidhānam ।
﻿<pb n="1082"/>
adhvaryuvidhāvapi niyamaḥ ēva । kiṁ hēyamēvēdaṁ bhāṣyam ?
nēti vadāmaḥ । yadi ktvēti paurvāparyamabhidhānē
gamyatē kartr̥vidhau, tadanuṣṭhānaupayikatayaiva kartr̥vidhāvupa-
yujyatē na saṁbandhividhāviti tanniṣṭhā śrutirityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="1083"/>
aprayuktasyāvidhēyatvamēva hēturuktaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi hr̥dayasyāgrē'vadyati
atha jihvāyā atha vakṣasa ityētadapyudāharaṇaṁ atra syāt ।
﻿<pb n="1084"/>
nēti brūmaḥ । pāṭhāvagatasyāyamathaśabdō'nuvādaḥ । kartr̥viśēṣavidhau
punarnānyataḥ kramō'vagantuṁ śakyatē ktvāpratyayāt iti
sūktam । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ nāntarīyakō'yaṁ niyamaḥ ādriyatē ।
na hyacōdanālakṣaṇasya cōdanālakṣaṇanirvr̥ttāvaṅgatōpapadyatē । satyaṁ
nōpapadyatē; ata ēva ca nānuṣṭhīyatē kintvarthaprāptamēva
kramāntaraṁ niruṇaddhi tasyānavagamādityucyatē । atō'napēkṣatva-
mivā'vidhīyamānamapyupakārāyaiva bhavatīti na dōṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="1085"/>
punaruktyādyāśaṅkā tūktā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। 1arthācca ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>ēvaṁ tāvat ananyaparākṣaratayā niyamitaḥ kramaḥ । idānīṁ
kāryānurōdhēna kramō'pi niyamyatē । tatparatvādanuṣṭhānasya । tatra prada-
rśitānyudāharaṇāni । kiṁ pāṭhakramasya bādhō'yaṁ nēti cintyatē । nēti
brūmaḥ । idamapi kramaniyamahētukāraṇaṁ na kasyacidvirōdhitayā pradarśyatē
﻿<pb n="1086"/>
balābalacintāyāṁ tu virōdhē balīyastvaṁ ca । iha punaḥ
svarūpapratipattyarthamēvēdamupanyastam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">।। 3 ।। 1aniyamō'nyatra ।। 3 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra kramaniyamapramāṇaṁ nāsti uktaṁ vakṣmāṇaṁ vā tatrāniyama
ēva । yathā śākhāntarīyāṅgavidhānaṁ śākhāntarē upasaṁhriya-
māṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">।। 4 ।। 2kramēṇa vā niyamyēta kratvēkatvē tadguṇatvāt ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra punastātparyamakṣarāṇāṁ nāsti yathā adhvaryurityādau
na ca kāryatō virōdhaḥ । tatra kā kathā ? tatrāpi
﻿<pb n="1087"/>
pāṭhaniyamaḥ । nanu ca pāṭhakramāvagatirnirmūlā । na tasyāḥ
kiñcidavagatinimittamasti padānāṁ vākyārthāvagatihētutvāt ।
nirmūlā cāvagatirna pramāṇam । pūrvō dhāvatītyatra parānvaya iva ।
tasmādyathēṣṭamatra kramaparigrahaṇaṁ manyāmahē । ucyatē---maivaṁ vōcaḥ ।
vākyakrama iva vākyārthē kramō'pi śabdanibandhana ēvēti ।
yathā na śabdādr̥tē śabdakramō'vagamyatē nārthādr̥tē'rthakramaḥ । yasmiṁśca
satyēva yadavagamyatē'vyabhicārāt tat tasya nimittamiti
vadāmaḥ । tasmānnaidaṁ nimittam । ata ēva ca niyamakramamadhyayanaṁ
﻿<pb n="1088"/>
dr̥ṣṭārthamēva bhavati । anyatra kāryaviśēṣāt । ata ēva ca
laukikāḥ pāṭhakramēṇa dhūpādiṣu vyutkramābhidhānē pratiṣēdhaṁ kurvatē ।
adr̥ṣṭārthēṣvapi darśitam । tasmādatrāpi na kramāntarakalpanā
yuk‍tēti yuktam । ata ēva ca <q>‘adhvaryurgr̥hapatiṁ dīkṣayitvā’</q>
ityēvamādiṣu tātparyamātrāt kramasiddhiḥ । nimittatvamātraṁ
hi atra parigr̥hyatē । tasmāt sanimittā pratipattiḥ pramāṇamityuktaṁ
pramāṇaparīkṣāyām । atō yāvatī sanimittā pratipattiḥ sā sarvaiva
kramāvadhāraṇē anyatra vā vēdārthānuṣṭhānōpakāriṇī pramāṇamiti
mantavyam । darśanamuk‍tam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1089"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 5 ।। 1pravr̥ttyā tulyakālānāṁ guṇānāṁ tadupakramāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>kimaparaṁ kāraṇaṁ kramaniyamē ? pravr̥ttiriti brūmaḥ ।
pravr̥ttyāpi hi kramabuddhirupajāyatē । kathaṁ punavaidikatvam ?
tadarthāśrayāt । tasmāt pravr̥ttirapi niyamahētuḥ । yatpunaridaṁ
bhāṣyakārēṇōk‍taṁ <q>“ēvaṁ pradhānapratyāsat‍tirbhavati”</q> iti tathā
sauryādibhiśca sāmyamāśaṅkya punarvaiṣamyamupanyastaṁ kastasyō-
payōgaḥ ? nātīva kramāvadhāraṇē upayujyatē । astyatrōpayōgaḥ
pravr̥t‍tirnāma kramanirapēkṣaṁ kvacidanuṣṭhānaṁ nirapēkṣaṁ cēdanuṣṭhānaṁ pravr̥t‍taṁ na
﻿<pb n="1090"/>
punarapēkṣāyāṁ (pramāṇaṁ)prayōjanaṁ astīti manvānasyēdamuttaraṁ
---pradhānapratyāsat‍tiḥ sahacōdanātō'vagatā vaiṣamyāt pīḍitā
bhavati । sāmyē punaḥ yathābhyanujñātaiva bhavati । tatsiddha‍yarthaṁ
niyamō'bhyupagantavyaḥ । sa ca prathamapravr̥t‍tipūrvaka
iti tayaiva vyākhyāyatē । sauryādidarśanamidānīṁ kimartham ?
﻿<pb n="1091"/>
yadi kramāvagatimātratayaiva krama ādriyatē sauryādiṣu kaḥ
pradvēṣaḥ । na khalu kaścit । anuṣṭhānānaupayikatayā tu pratītamapi
tyajyatē varṇasvarūpamiva padēṣu (vākyēṣu) ēkatvamiva grahēṣu
ubhayatvamiva haviṣvu naitāvatā aupayikasyāpi tyāga upapadyatē ।
﻿<pb n="1092"/>
atō'pēkṣitaṁ pratipannamādriyatē । pratipannamapyanapēkṣitamu-
pēkṣaṇīyamēva । nanu caivaṁ sati pratipattiranarthikā prāpnōti । kēna
vōk‍taṁ pratipattēra(na) rthavattvaṁ arthavatpratipattirēvārthavattvē hētuḥ na
pratipattimātraṁ, nāpratipattiḥ pratipattiparyantaivēti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 6 ।। 1sthānāccōtpattisaṁyōgāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>atra bhāṣyakārēṇa triṇavādiṣvadarśanāt samāmnāya[krama]sya
vidyamānasyāpyaviṣayatāṁ manvānaiḥ idamudāhr̥tamityaviṣayatāṁ matvēda-
mudāhr̥taṁ saha paśūnālabhata iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1093"/>
<p>atra ca adhikaraṇāntarasiddhamarthamupādāya sahapaśūnā-
labhata iti savanīyasthānē sahatvamiti sthitē kaḥ kramaniyama
iti cintyatē kimatrāpi pravr̥t‍tirēva nimittaṁ uta
nimittāntaramastīti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī avaśyaṁbhāvini
kramē yadi pravr̥t‍tirnēṣyatē pūrvāvagatapāṭhādēva niyama iti
manyatē । rāddhāntavādī tu sahavacanēna sthānasyābādhi-
tatvāt savanīyasyaiva pūrvamanuṣṭhānaṁ nyāyyamityuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="1094"/>
yadyēvamagnīṣōmīyānubandhyayōḥ kā vārtā ? kathaṁ paurvāparyaṁ atra ।
kimanayā'nupanyastayā cintayā ? yadvā sthānavat kālabādhō'pya-
yukta iti agnīṣōmīya ēva pūrvam । yadyēvaṁ savanīyādapi tarhi
pūrvatvaṁ bhavitumarhati । na । vihitatvāt savanīyakālasya pracayā-
vagamyatvādagnīṣōmīyakālasya । vidhānārthatvācca pracayasya vihitaṁ
balīyaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi balābalacintēyam (na pramāṇasyārthānniyamō
yuktaḥ) । naivaṁ, sthitē pramāṇāntaratvē balavadabalatvamiti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 7 ।। 1mukhyakramēṇa cāṅgānāṁ tadarthatvāt ।। 14 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1095"/>
<p>yatra yaugapadyēna cōdanā sārasvatau bhavati iti tatra kiṁ
pramāṇāntaramasti kramaniyamasya aṅgānāṁ uta yathēṣṭā pravr̥t‍tiriti ।
tantrēṇōccāraṇācchās‍trasya na kramaḥ pratīyatē ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē---mukhyē kramadarśanāt aṅgēṣvapi kramō
yuktaḥ । ēvaṁ ca sati yāvadanujñātaṁ vyavadhānaṁ bhaviṣyati ।
aniyamē hi anujñātātikramaḥ । kramabādhō na yukta iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 8 ।। 1 prakr̥tau tu svaśabdatvādyathākramaṁ pratīyēta ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṁ pāṭhamukhyayōrvirōdhē cintyatē । tatra mukhyā-
﻿<pb n="b1096"/>
rthatvādaṅgānāṁ mukhyakramō balīyāniti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । ēvaṁ ca
prayōgacōdanānugrahaḥ pratyāsat‍tēḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---na pratītasya
bādhō yuktaḥ pāṭhācca nirapēkṣāt kramō'vagatō'ṅgānāṁ nānyāpēkṣayā
bādhituṁ yuktaḥ । nanu ca pratyāsat‍tēḥ prādhānyācca balavat‍tōktā ।
satyamuktā---ayuktā tu sā । yathāpratītaṁ hi prayōgavacanō gr̥hṇāti ।
na prayōgavacanādaṅagāvagatiḥ । aṅgaṁ sat prayōgavacanēna gr̥hyata
ityuk‍tam । tasmāt yathāvagamaṁ pratyāsattiḥ । na pratyāsāt‍tērava-
gamō'ṅgānāṁ, ataḥ pāṭhō balīyāniti yuktam । uktaṁ ca
svaśabdatvāditi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1097"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 9 ।। 1mantratastu virādhē syāt prayōgarūpasāmarthyāt tasmā-
dutpattidēśaḥ saḥ ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>mantrabrāhmaṇapāṭhavirōdhē kiṁ balīya iti । aniyama iti prāptē
ucyatē---mantrakramō balīyāniti । kutaḥ ? pāṭhasyānanyaparatvāt ।
prayōjyatvānmantrāṇām । nanu brāhmaṇēpyananyapara ēva pāṭhakramaḥ ।
yatpunaḥ (kramōtpattiḥ)karmōtpattiḥ prayōjanamityuk‍taṁ, vākyasya
tatprayōjanaṁ na pāṭhakramasya । ucyatē---utpattyarthaḥ sa pāṭhakramaḥ,
na prayōgārtha ityuktaṁ bhavati । mantrē punaḥ prayōgārthaḥ kramō bhavatīti
balavattvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1098"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 10 ।। 1tadvacanādvikr̥tau yathā pradhānaṁ syāt ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṁ mukhyakramādvikr̥tau kramaḥ uta pāṭhakramāt prakr̥tau yathā
nirjñātō'ṅgakramaḥ vikr̥tāvapi tathaiva prayōk‍tavya iti । kiṁ yuk‍taṁ ?
prayōgārthatvāt kramasya vikr̥tau prayōgāvagamāt yathāvikr̥ti
prayōga iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu na nirjñātakramaṁ prayōgavacanō bādhitumarhati ।
nirjñātasya hi prayōgō aṅgānāmiva kramasya(āha) । anirjñātē hi
hētvantarakalpanā na niścitē । tasmādyathā prakr̥tau tathā vikr̥tā-
vapyaṅgānāṁ prayōga iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1099"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 11 ।। vikr̥tiḥ prakr̥tidharmatvāt tatkālā syāt yathā-
śiṣṭam ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>sadyaskāladvayahakālacintā । kēyaṁ kramacintāyāṁ ? krama-
sidhyarthēti brūmaḥ । sadyaskālatāyāmanyathā kramō bhavati । dvayaha-
kālatāyāṁ cānyathā । tasmād‌yuktō vicāraḥ । tatra prakr̥tivaditi
dvayahakālatāṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । aharantarēpi savanaśrutēra-
viśēṣāt । rāddhāntī tu kālāntaraśravaṇāt na prākr̥taṁ kālamapēkṣata
iti sadyaskālatāṁ manyatē । savanāni caikāhaḥ saṁbandhānyēva śrutyā'va-
gamyamānāni na kāraṇādr̥tē'harantarāpēkṣāṇi yuktāni kalpayitum ।
﻿<pb n="b1100"/>
darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 12 ।। aṅgānāṁ mukhyakālatvādyathōktamutkarṣē syāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>aśrūyamāṇānāmutkarṣavākyē'pakarṣavākyē ca kimityutkarṣāpa-
karṣau । satyaṁ śrutasya padārthasya utkarṣō'pakarṣō vā śrūyatē na
punaruparitanamādhastyaṁ vā'kr̥tvēti । na cēdidamavagamyatē kramāda-
vagatamanuṣṭhānaṁ kēna vāryatē । ataḥ kimatrōtkarṣavākyē'śrutatvaṁ
kariṣyati । anyataḥ siddhēḥ । tasmāt yuktamuk‍taṁ---tadādi
vā'bhisaṁbandhāt tadantamapakarṣē syāditi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1101"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 13 ।। 1pravr̥ttyā kr̥takālānām ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>kimalaṅkaraṇādayō dharmāḥ praiṣōttarakālaṁ kartavyā uta pāṭhādēvā-
vagatāḥ saumikā iti । tatra vacanabalāt nirvāpamātramēva madhyē
kartavyaṁ, atō'niyama iti prāptē abhidhīyatē---prōkṣaṇādayaḥ kartavyāḥ
anirjñātakartavyatā hi pāṭhānniyamyatē । na punaḥ nirjñātakartavyatāṁ
niruṇaddhi pāṭhaḥ । praiṣāt praiṣārthakartavyatā vijñāyatē । ataḥ paraṁ tu
pāṭhānniyamaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1102"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 14 ।। 1asaṁyōgāt‍tu tadēva pratikr̥ṣyēta ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>dīkṣāsu yūpaṁ chinattītyapakarṣaḥ śrūyatē tatra tadantāśaṅkā-
nivr̥ttyarthamidamadhikaraṇam । abhisambandhābhāvāt । yāvadvacana-
mapakarṣa iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 15 ।। 2prāsaṅgikaṁ ca nōtkarṣēdasaṁyōgāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>prāsaṅgikēpyayaṁ tulyō hēturiti prāsaṅgikaṁ ca nōtkarṣēdityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 16 ।। 3tathā'pūrvam ।। 29 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1103"/>
<p>paurṇamāsyāṁ pāṭhakramāt kramasaṁbandhō nirjñāta iti
tadapakarṣa iti tadantāpakarṣaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī
tu na paurṇamāsīprakr̥tikamāmāvāsyaṁ karmēti manvānaḥ apakarṣōttara-
kālamēva kramō niyamyatē śēṣāṇāmiti yāvadvacanamapakarṣamuktavāt ।
kāryavirōdhaścābhyuccayaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 17 ।। 1sāntapanīyāṁ tūtkarṣēdagnihōtraṁ savanadvaiguṇyāt ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>parārthamuddhr̥tē'gnau prasaṅgādr̥tē nāgnihōtraṁ hōtavyaṁ
iti manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī utkarṣamuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="b1104"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu nimittatvātkālasyānutkarṣaṁ manyatē । kathaṁ punaḥ
kālō nimittaṁ ? tasmin sati prayōgāt na punaḥ adhikāri-
viśēṣaṇatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1105"/>
<p>atō nimittē sati naimittikēna bhavitavyamityarthāt
prasaṅgasiddhiḥ । atō'nutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="35">।। 18 ।। ṣōḍaśī cōkthyasaṁyōgāt ।। 35 ।।</ab>
<p>ṣōḍaśinyapyaṅgakālavirōdhāta kādācitkatvāccōtkarṣasya anu-
tkarṣaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu avaśyaṁbhāvitvā-
cchāstrātikramasya varaṁ aṅgaśāstrātikrama ityuktavān ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ pañcamādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1106"/>
</section>
<section>
