<head>br̥hatī</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1sannipātē pradhānānāmēkaikasya guṇānāṁ sarvakarma
syāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu ca pravr̥ttyā kramō niyataḥ । kimidamēkaikasya kr̥ts‍namiti ।
ucyatē---sthita ētasminnadhikaraṇē tat । iha punaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī
manyatē sakalapadārthānuṣṭhānēnāpi sahatvamupapadyata ēva । kimiti
kālavyavadhānaṁ kalpyatē । ēvamēvānujñātamupapannaṁ bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1107"/>
<p>rāddhāntavādī tu sahatvacōdanādēkaikasya padārthasya sahānuṣṭhāna-
mavagamyamānaṁ na śakyatē tyak‍tum । atastadanurōdhēna vyavadhānānu-
jñānaṁ na tatparityāgēnēti padārthānusamayamuktavān । adhikaraṇāntaraṁ
vēti kāryavirōdhāt sahatvāvagamatyāgaḥ pāṭhavat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">।। 3 ।। 1muṣṭikapālāvadānāñjanābhyañjanavapanapāvanēṣu caikēna ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇē anāvr̥ttēnāpi muṣṭyādinā kr̥taṁ
śāstrārthaṁ manyamānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī padārthānusamayamuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="b1108"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu cōdanātaḥ padārthādhyavasānaṁ vaidikēṣu ca na lōkavat
pramāṇāntarāvasēyam । ēkaṁ cēdaṁ śās‍traṁ caturō muṣṭhīnnirvapatīti
dvirhaviṣō'vadyatīti ca । tasmācchāstrārthānusamayō nyāyya iti
manyatē ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">।। 4 ।। 1saṁyuktē tu prakramādaṅgaṁ syāditarasya tadarthatvāt ।। 6 ।।</ab>
<p>yadi śāstrādanusamayō dvirhaviṣō'vadyatīti ēkatvā-
cchāstrasya ētāvataivānusamaya ēva nyāyyaḥ iti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1109"/>
tasmāt pradānāntamēvānusamētavyamiti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 5 ।। 1vacanāt‍tu parivyāṇāntamañjanādi syāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>arthādyūpadhāraṇamiti pūrvapakṣavādī padārthānusamayaṁ manyatē ।
śāstrabhēdāt śāstrārthānāṁ saha cōdanāt । rāddhānta-
vādī tu vihitōpapattyarthatvātkramasya kāṇḍānusamayaṁ manyatē ।
nanu ca dr̥ṣṭārthatvādanyēnāpi tat kriyata ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b1110"/>
satyaṁ yadyarthād dr̥ṣṭārthatā syāt । vidhau tu sati dr̥ṣṭēpyarthē na
śāstrārthō vyatikramituṁ śakyatē । darśitamētat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 6 ।। 1paśugaṇē tasya tasyāpavarjayēta paś‍vēkatvāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi śāstrabādhaṁ manvānaḥ kāṇḍānusamayaṁ manyatē
pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu padārthānusamayēpyabādhaṁ manvānaḥ
sahacōdanānugrahāya padārthānusamaya ēva nyāyya ityuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="b1111"/>
man‍trōccāraṇatan‍tratā ca sahatvē liṅgam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 7 ।। 1nānābījēṣvēkamulūkhalaṁ vibhavāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra viśēṣō'vadānādihōmaparyantānusamaya ityanēnādhi-
karaṇēna । na khalu kaścidviśēṣaḥ । kimarthaṁ tarhīdamadhikaraṇaṁ ?
vidhānāt padārthāvacchēdō bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhimānaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntavādī tu vidhēyānyatvēna vidhānōpapattau na padārthā-
vacchēdāya prabhavō'stīti pūrvōk‍ta ēva nyāyyaḥ । anēna ca
﻿<pb n="b1112"/>
viśēṣēṇa tadapyatrōdāharaṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 8 ।। 1vikārē tvanūyājānāṁ pātrabhēdā'rthabhēdāt syāt ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarayaṁ kramacintāyāṁ pātrabhēdōpanyāsaḥ । kramasiddha‍yarthaṁ
iti brūmaḥ । bhēdābhēdē kramānyatvadarśanāt । tatra pūrvaḥ pakṣō-
dravyavikāraśaṅkyā pātravikāraśaṅkyā ca । kālānyatvēna
cōpapattēḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1113"/>
<p>rāddhāntastu dravyavikārāpattēḥ kālānyatvē ca grahaṇayōḥ
sahāvagamabādhāt tadanuguṇaḥ pātrabhēdō nyāyya iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 9 ।। 1prakr̥tēḥ pūrvōktatvādapūrvamantē syāt na hyacōditasya
śēṣāmnānam ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>vaikr̥tānāṁ pāṭhakramaḥ prākr̥tairvyavadhīyatē nēti cintā । vyavadhī-
yata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । padārthānuṣṭhānēna vyavadhānāvagamāt ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu vaikr̥taprayōgavacanāt prākr̥tapadārthāvagamāt (a)
vyavadhānam । atassūk‍taṁ antē tu bādarāyaṇa iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1114"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 10 ।। 1kr̥tadēśāt‍tu pūrvēṣām sadēśaḥ syāt tēna pratyakṣa-
saṁyōgāt nyāyamātramitarat ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>rājasūyēpi vidēvanādayō vaikr̥tēna pāṭhēna viruddha‍yamānā
nāntē'nuṣṭhānamarhanti । nyāyamātramitaraditi ।</p>
<p>ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati---nāntē'nuṣṭhānaṁ kēnacitkramēṇāvagamyatē ।
kiṁ tarhi ? pūrvāvagamavirōdhāt antē'nuṣṭhānamiti nyāyamātra-
mityucyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1115"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="22">।। 11 ।। 1prākr̥tācca purastāt ।। 22 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi prākr̥takramāvagamāt prayōgacōdanāta ēva antē'nu-
ṣṭhānaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । punaḥ śrutistu ananyārthā kramamēvā-
vagamayatīti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 12 ।। 2sannipātaścēdyathōktamantē syāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1116"/>
<p>atrāpi dīkṣaṇīyāsaṅkīrtanaṁ pūrvavat kramārthaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣa-
vādī । tat‍tu pūrvapadārthakramaparatayaivōktamiti(vōpayuktamiti) ।
rāddhāntavādī tu parastādyathōk‍taṁ nyāyyaṁ manyatē । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ
pūrvasminnēvōpayujyatē na punaḥ parasminnapīti । atrōcyatē---paratō'na-
nyatvāvagamāt pūrvasmiṁścānyatvāvagatēḥ yuktamuktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ pañcamasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1117"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>br̥hatyāṁ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1vivr̥ddhiḥ karmabhēdāt pr̥ṣadājyavattasya tasyōpadiśyēta ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>kramārtha ēva pratyēkasamudāyasambandhaścintyatē । pratyēkasambandhē
hi vyavadhānamahatvaṁ samudāyasambandhē tvalpatvam । tasmād‍yuktā
cintā । kiṁ punaryuk‍taṁ ? pratyēkamabhisaṁbandha iti । pratipradhānaṁ guṇā
āvartanta iti nyāyāt । nanu ca pr̥thaktvanivēśinī saṅkhyētyuktam ।
satyamuktaṁ vidhānavaśāt‍tu yathōpapadyatē tathōpakalpanīyam ।
﻿<pb n="b1118"/>
ata ēva <q>‘pañcadaśānyājyāni’</q> iti ca pratyēkamabhisaṁbandhaḥ ।
atrōcyatē---na vidhānaṁ padārthamanyathā kartumutsahatē ।
padārthānurōdhī hi vidhiḥ na vidhyanurōdhinaḥ padārthāḥ । <q>‘agninā
siñcēt’</q> ityēvamādiṣu darśitam । tasmāt yāvatpr̥thaktvaṁ
tāvadabhyāsakalpanā na sambhavatīti samudāyābhisambandhaḥ ।
pr̥ṣadājyē tvētadviparītaṁ iti pratyēkamabhisaṁbandhaḥ । yadapyuk‍taṁ
pañcadaśānyājyānīti āvr̥ttau ḍapratyayaṁ vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">।। 2 ।। 1svasthānāt‍tu vivr̥ddha‍yēran kr̥tānupūrvyatvāt ।। 3 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1119"/>
<p>saṅkhyāsampattyarthamabhyasē prāptē idaṁ cintyatē---kiṁ daṇḍakalita-
vadabhyāsaḥ uta svasthāna iti । samudāyābhisambandhāt daṇḍakalita-
vadabhyāsammanyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । pūrvapratītakramānurōdhāt svasthānē
yukta iti rāddhāntaḥ । samudāyasaṁbandhasya tūbhayathāpyavirōdhaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 3 ।। 1samidhyamānavatīṁ samiddhavatīṁ ka cāntarēṇa dhāyyāḥ syuḥ
dyāvāpr̥thivyōrantarālē samarhaṇāt ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu vacanē sati pūrvapakṣa ēva na sambhavati । arthavādapūrvakaṁ
tadvacanamiti pūrvapakṣavādī nyāyānusārēṇāpi gacchatyēvēti manyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b1120"/>
rāddhāntastu nāyathārthagrahaṇē pramāṇamastyarthavādasya iti na śabdārthaṁ
nyāyō niruṇaddhi iti nyāyamātraṁ tadityuktam । atō yathārtha-
vādamēvēdaṁ vidhānaṁ nyāyyaṁ, dhāyyāśabdanirūpaṇaṁ tu prāsaṅgikam ।
pradarśitaṁ ca tat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 4 ।। 1stōmavivr̥ddhau bahiṣpavamānē purastāt paryāsādāgantavaḥ
syuḥ tathāhi dr̥ṣṭaṁ dvādaśāhē ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>nyāyamātraṁ vacanaṁ bādhituṁ na kṣamata ityuktam । vacanaṁ
cēdaṁ vr̥ṣaṇvantastr̥cā bhavanti tr̥ca uttamaḥ paryāsa iti ।
nanu dvādaśāhē ētadvacanaṁ, atadvikārēṣu kēyamāśaṅkā ।
﻿<pb n="b1121"/>
uttamaśabdaśravaṇāt1 । kimidamuttamaśabdaśravaṇāditi ? uttamaḥ
paryāsō bhavatīti padārthāṅgatāṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । nanu ca
padārthāṅgatvē ānarthakyamuktam । na tat paryāsē bhavitumarhati ।
sarvasya paryāsasyārthavattvāt kratusaṁbandhinī hi paryāsasaṁjñā
udgīthavata । tasmād‍yuktamuktam । dvādaśāhavikr̥tiṣvapi nirā-
karaṇīya ēvāyamartha ityupanyāsaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1122"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē-nāyaṁ padārthadharmaḥ । kastarhi ? kratudharmaḥ । kathaṁ ?
prakaraṇāt dvādaśāhaniyōgaikyamavagamyatē । na kratvantaraniyōgai-
kyam । nanu ca padārthānusārī niyōgaḥ । padārthānusārēpyatrā-
virōdhāt । tasmānna kratvantarasaṁbandhakalpanāyāṁ pramāṇamasti ।
dvādaśāhavikārēṣvēvaitat syāt । na vā tatrāpi । atha vā
vr̥ṣaṇvatāṁ dharmaḥ । nanu ca padārthadharmō na bhavatītyuktam, satyamuktaṁ,
﻿<pb n="b1123"/>
na punaḥ kratvarthāparityāgēnēti । tasmātsūk‍taṁ tadvikārēṣvapi na
bhavatīti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 5 ।। 1antē tūttarayōrdadhyāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kathamatra pūrvapakṣō yuktaḥ, vacanamadr̥ṣ‌ṭvētyayuktamidam । adhīta-
vēdasya hi dharmajijñāsā । ayaṁ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । idamapi dvādaśāha
ēva vacanam atra viśēṣāgrahaṇāt tadvikārēṣu bhavatu ata-
dvikārēṣu mābhūditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1124"/>
<p>atrōcyatē---āvāpanibandhanamētadvacanaṁ yāvadāvāpaṁ bhavitu-
marhati । kathaṁ tarhi prakr̥taniyōgaikyaṁ ? na, kāryāśritatvādasya
vidhēḥ vr̥ṣaṇvatsūpadēśāśraya ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 6 ।। 1grahēṣṭakamaupānuvākyaṁ savanacitiśēṣaḥ syāt ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpyaṅgāṅgicintā kramārthaiva । kathamatra pūrvapakṣaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b1125"/>
atrōcyatē---kāryānupravēśitvānniyōgārthasya niyōgasya । citi-
savananiṣpattyā cānupravēśasya । tasmāccitisavanaśēṣō'yamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---upadēśasiddha‍yarthaṁ hi kāryaṁ na kārya-
siddha‍yartha upadēśaḥ yāgāgrisaṁbandhaścāyaṁ upadēśaḥ । nanu
ca nyāyapaunaruktyamidaṁ aruṇayā krīṇātīti darśitam ।
﻿<pb n="b1126"/>
tatrāsambhavādapi bhavantīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । tannirā-
karaṇārthamidam । prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 7 ।। 1antē syuravyavāyāta ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu vacanē sati atra pūrvapakṣō nōpapadyatē । na
nōpapadyatē । sarvā brāhmaṇavatya ityanuvādaṁ manyatē । ēvaṁ
sati anyā anyā iti darśanamupapannaṁ bhavati
﻿<pb n="b1127"/>
iti । ēvaṁ prāptē abhidhīyatē । brāhmaṇavatyaḥ śrutiviniyuk‍tāḥ pari-
gr̥hyantē । kimiti---mantraviniyōjyatvācchēṣāṇām । samākhyā
punarlaukikyēvētyuktam । tasmānmadhyamāyāṁ citāvupadhātavya
iti । nanu ca mantrēṇāpi viniyujyamānāḥ brāhmaṇēnaiva viniyuktā
na svatantraliṅgapramāṇamityuk‍tam । viśēṣābhiprāyēṇēdamuktam
vacanasyārthavattvāyētyadōṣaḥ । darśanē tu mantrābhiprāyēṇānyatvaṁ
varṇanīyam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">।। 8 ।। 1prāglōkaṁ pr̥ṇāyāstasyāssampūraṇārthatvāt ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cāntē vādarāyaṇa iti nōpapadyatē, lōkaṁpr̥ṇāpi
brāhmaṇavatyēva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1128"/>
<p>nanu ca mantravidhānārthaṁ tadvacanam । nanu ca sarvā ēva
mantradvāṁrēṇa cōdyantē । satyaṁ; tathāpīṣṭakābhidhānapradhānō'yaṁ nirdēśaḥ
<q>‘citriṇīrupadadhāti’</q> ityēvamādiṣu । iha punaḥ <q>‘lōkaṁ pr̥ṇa chidraṁ
pr̥ṇa’</q> iti mantrapradhānō'yaṁ nirdēśa iti laiṅgikyēvēyam । antē tu
bādarāyaṇa iti yuk‍tam । rāddhāntastu mantrārthavādānyathānupapattēḥ
laiṅgikā api prāgēva brāhmaṇavatya iti yuk‍tam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1129"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 9 ।। saṁskr̥tē karma saṁskārāṇāṁ tadarthatvāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>āhitāgnēradhikāraśravaṇāta ādhānēna cāgnīnāmutpattēḥ
bhavatyanantaramadhikāra iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । ādhānānantarakramasiddhiścā-
nēna prakārēṇōk‍tā । yathā <q>‘āhitāgnirnaklinnaṁ dārvabhyādadhyāta’</q>
ityēvamādīnām । ēvaṁ prāptē'bhidhīyatē---ubhayamapyagnyarthamityuk‍tam
āhavanīyādimukhēnāhitāg‍nēradhikāraḥ । na cēṣṭibhirvinā''havanī-
yō bhavati iti na karmasvadhikāraḥ । darśanaṁ punaḥ agnyarthasyaiva
hōmasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1130"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 10 ।। 1sañcitē tvagnicid‍yuktaṁ prāpaṇānnimittasya ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p>ihāpi cayanānantaraṁ vrataprāptiṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī ।
atrōcyatē---nēdamāhitāgninā tulyam । tatra hi agnyarthamādhānam
iha punaḥ agnikāryārthaṁ cayanaṁ, prōkṣaṇamiva vrīhikāryārtham । kāryaṁ
ca kr̥ts‍nakratuprayōgasādhyamiti kratusamāptāvēvāg‍niciditi । na
cāg‍nicayananimittā hyētē niyamāḥ kratōravagamyantē bhēdanahōmavat
﻿<pb n="b1131"/>
kr̥taprayōgasyāg‍nicidabhidhānāt । tasmātkratvantē niyamā iti
siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 11 ।। 1parēṇāvēdanāddīkṣitaḥ syāt sarvairdīṁkṣābhisambandhāt ।। 29 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi dīkṣitapadārthakramasiddha‍yarthamidaṁ cintyatē । kiyadbhi-
rdīkṣitō bhavati iti । yāvatā dīkṣābhisambandhaḥ tāvadbhirdīkṣitō
bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । sarvēṣāmutpattyarthatvāt yathā''dhānēna
pavamānēṣṭibhiścāgnayaḥ । anyathā hi vikalpaḥ syāt
pratyēkaṁ dīkṣābhinirvr̥ttēḥ । ata ēvābhidhānamapyuttarakāla-
mēva । atrōcyatē---dīkṣiṣyamāṇa ityadhikāripadamidam ।
﻿<pb n="b1132"/>
na cādhikārāniṣpattērviṣayasiddhiriti ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmādiṣṭērēva
dīkṣitatvasiddhiḥ । samuccayaścaivamupapannō bhavati । utpattisaṁskāra-
bhēdāt । sarvēṣāmutpasyarthatvāta anapēkṣaśravaṇācca । kathaṁ tarhi
ādhānapavamānēṣṭīnāṁ samuccayaḥ ? prayōjanāntarābhāvāt na tatra
tayōrgrāhakaṁ kiñcidasti । iha punarjyōtiṣṭōmavidhēḥ vikalpaḥ
tulyarthānām । tasmādasmatpakṣa ēva samuccayasiddhiḥ । na
cābhidhānābhāvādarthābhāvaḥ śakyatē vak‍tumiti darśitam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1133"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 12 ।। 1aṅgavatkratūnāmānupūrvyama ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cāvaśyaṁbhāvini kramē pāṭhānniyama uktaḥ । kratvantaravaditi
ca vyatirēkō varṇitaḥ bhinnaprayōgavacanatvānnaiṣāṁ krama upapadyata
iti । kathamatra pūrvapakṣaḥ ? ucyatē---anēkānuṣṭhānanibandhanō'yaṁ
kramaḥ । anēkaṁ ca kāmyaṁ kurvataḥ kāminaḥ yuktaḥ kramaniyama iti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । kathaṁ tarhi sarvasvārē pāṭhakramaḥ ? arthā-
dbādhō bhaviṣyatītyadōṣaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---vidhivitāna-
cintēyam na puruṣēcchāvitānacintā, acōdanālakṣaṇatvāttasya
﻿<pb n="b1134"/>
ēkasya cādhikāravidhēraṅgavidhivitānasaṁbandhō nādhikāramapēkṣatē
saṁbandhābhāvāt । asaṁbandhasya ca śābdataiva na śakyatē vak‍tum ।
na ca sarvakāmasyādhikāraḥ yōgasiddha‍yadhikaraṇē pratyuktatvāt ।
arthasya sambandhaviṣayatvāta । tasmāta kāmyēṣvaniyamaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1135"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 13 ।। ya ētēnētyagniṣṭōmaḥ prakaraṇāt ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>uparitanasyādhikaraṇasya viṣayapradarśanārthamidamadhikaṇam ।
agniṣṭōmapradarśanādityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 14 ।। 1athānyēnēti saṁsthānāṁ sannidhānāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>ya ētēnētyagniṣṭōmasaṁsthasyāvamarśāt anyēnēti saṁsthāntarāva-
marśaṁ manyatē pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu ēṣa vāva prathamō
yajñō yajñānāmiti yajñaśabdaśrutēḥ yajñāntaramēvānyaśabdēna
﻿<pb n="b1136"/>
pratīyata ityuktavān । ag‍niṣṭōmasaṁsthasya nityatvāt ya ētēnē-
tyucyatē । tathā cāpattivihārāvupapannau bhavataḥ । āpattyākṣēpa-
samādhānaṁ ca darśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="43">।। 15 ।। 1ēkastōbhē vā kratusaṁyōgāta ।। 43 ।।</ab>
<p>ēkastōmānāṁ vākyaśēṣādanyēnēti grahaṇam । na cānyēnētya-
nyatvamātrāvagatēḥ । nanu ca vākyaśēṣādviśēṣāvagatirityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b1137"/>
sandigdhēṣu vākyaśēṣānnirṇaya ityuktam । iha tu asandigdhaiva
jyōtiṣṭōmādanyēṣvavagatiriti arthavādamātramētata ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ pañcamādhyāyasya
tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1138"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>br̥hatyāṁ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1kramakōpō'rthaśabdābhyāṁ śrutiviśēṣādarthaparatvācca ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>atra balābalacintā । pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ avidhēya-
tvātkramasya avagatēśca tulyatvādvikalpa iti । rāddhāntastu
vidhēyavirōdhādavagatērēvātulyatvamiti śrutyarthayōrēva tu balavattvam ।
atra śrutyarthayōrvirōdhē kathaṁ ? naivōdāharaṇamasti । artha ēva
﻿<pb n="b1139"/>
balīyān । kāryaṁ hyatrārthaśabdēnōcyatē । kāryārthaśca kramaḥ । ataḥ
śrutimapabādhatē kāryaviṣayatvāttasyāḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। avadānābhidhāraṇāsādanēṣvānupūrvyaṁ pravr̥ttyā syāt ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi balābalacintaiva । pravr̥ttēḥ pūrvapravr̥ttatvāta pravr̥tti-
rbalīyasīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । kāryārthatvātkramasya avadānasya ca
pradānōpakramatvāt mukhyakramō balīyāniti rāddhāntaḥ । darśana-
maktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">।। 3 ।। 1vacanādiṣṭipūrvatvam ।। 5 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1140"/>
<p>atrāpyakṣaraparaṁ kramamaṅgīkr̥tya cintā । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī
sōmēna yakṣyamāṇa’ iti nākṣaraparatā kramasya sambhavatīti manvānaḥ,
iṣṭipūrvatāmēvāha । kathaṁ punarna saṁbhavati ? ādhānavidhānaparatvā-
dvākyasya । darśapūrṇamāsāviṣ‌ṭvēti tu kālavidhānātsiddhiḥ । atrā-
bhidhīyatē---yēyamadyatanī vibhaktiḥ sā nādhānānantaryādr̥tē
sambhavatītyarthāt atrāpi kramasiddhiḥ sōmādhānayōḥ । kva
punariyaṁ na sambhavati ? adhikārē । adhikārāyattañca vidhānaṁ
﻿<pb n="b1141"/>
ityādhānavidhānēpyarthāta kramākṣēpaḥ । abhyuccayō darśitaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 4 ।। 1utkarṣādvā brāhmaṇasya sōmaḥ syāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇē pūrvādhikaraṇārthasya viṣayaviśēṣē avasthā-
panam । yadanyattatprāsaṅgikamēva । yaḥ punarayamantarāgarbhiṇyupanyāsaḥ
sa kimarthaḥ ? ēvamarthō'sau । yadyanantaraṁ sōmādhānaṁ tadā
brāhmaṇasya kalpadvayaṁ sambhavati । anyasya vā svakālē
punariṣ‍ṭipūrvakatvamēvati niyamyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1142"/>
<p>kathaṁ punaridamavagamyatē brāhmaṇasyaiva kalpadvayamiti
rāddhāntastu iṣ‍ṭipūrvatvē haviṣa utkarṣāt tasmāt sōmā-
dhānaṁ tasyaiva । anyathā hi brāhmaṇasyaivōtkarṣē'napēkṣitārtha-
vidhānaṁ syāt । śēṣamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1143"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 6 ।। 1purōḍāśastvanirdēśē tad‌yuk‍tē dēvatābhāvāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>ēkasya haviṣa utkarṣa iti sthitē tadviśēṣāvadhāraṇāyēdama-
dhikaraṇam । uktaṁ ca ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 7 ।। vikr̥tēḥ prakr̥tikālatvāt sadyaskālōttarā vikr̥tiḥ
tayōḥ pratyakṣaśiṣṭatvāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvaṁ nyāyatō'sambhavamuktvā tasminnēvāhani samāp‍tyupakramau
darśitavān sambhavārtham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1144"/>
<p>sadyaskālataiva vikr̥tīnāmityuktavān ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 8 ।। sānnāyyāgnīṣōmīyavikārāḥ ūrdhvaṁ sōmāt prakr̥tivat ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 9 ।। tathā sōmavikārāḥ darśapūrṇamāsābhyās ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p>ihādhikaraṇadvayēpyadhikārādr̥tē kālalakṣaṇā na sambhavatīti
kr̥tādhikārasyaiva kramasyādhikāra iti tadvikārāṇāmapyēvamēvēti
yuktam । kimarthaṁ tarhi adhikaraṇadvayam ? pūrvatra kartr̥tānirdēśāt
nāsōmayājīti sōmayāgasya kartā sānnāyyē kartr̥tayā'bhidhīyatē
﻿<pb n="1145"/>
dvitīyādhikaraṇē tu darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvēti punarāśaṅkitavān
kartr̥nirdēśābhāvāt । kathaṁ tarhi rāddhāntē nyāyatulyatā ? nādhi-
kārādr̥tē kālalakṣaṇā sambhavatīti tulyatōktā ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ pañcamādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
